## How to View your Final Grades – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17397789183117-How-to-View-your-Final-Grades

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17397789183117-How-to-View-your-Final-Grades#main-content)

**Overview**

This article explains how to view your **final grades** at Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC) using the student portal (Camu). It walks you through the steps to access your official academic performance once grades are posted at the end of every term. Use this guide to check your results, understand the grading display, and verify your completed courses each term.

_![How-To (1).png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17710037714957)_

_This article offers a step-by-step guide for MMDC students to access and view their final grades for a particular term or academic year._

### How can I view my final grades on Camu?

To view your final grades for a specific term or academic year, follow these simple steps:

1. Log in to your My Camu account.
2. On the left side panel, locate and click on " **Transcript**".![Transcript.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17397783372557)

By following these steps, you will be able to access and review your transcript, which includes your final grades.

Here are some important notes and explanations to help you understand the terms used in your academic records:

- **CA (Credits Accumulated)**: This refers to the total number of units or credits you have taken during a specific term.
- **CP (Credits Passed)**: This represents the number of units that you have successfully passed or completed during the term.
- **GP (Grade Point)**: The grade point is calculated by multiplying the credits of each course by the corresponding grade you have achieved, and then summing them up for all courses.
- **GPA (Grade Point Average)**: The GPA is obtained by dividing the total grade points (GP) by the total credits accumulated (CA) for the term. This value is also known as the **Term Weighted Average (TWA)** and reflects your average performance for that specific term.
- **CGPA (Cumulative GPA)**: The CGPA is the cumulative average of your GPA across all terms. It is calculated by summing up the GPAs from each term and dividing it by the total credits accumulated across all terms. The CGPA is also referred to as the General Weighted Average (GWA) and provides an overall representation of your academic performance throughout your college journey.

Understanding these terms will help you interpret and assess your academic progress accurately.

#### **MMDC Grading system**    **Course Grade**

1. Students shall be graded or marked in accordance with the following grading system:

| **Grade/Mark** | **Percentage/Equivalent** | **Description** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| 1.00 | Above 96.00 | Excellent |
| 1.25 | 91.51 - 96.00 | Superior |
| 1.50 | 87.01 - 91.50 | Very Good |
| 1.75 | 82.51 - 87.00 | Good |
| 2.00 | 78.01 - 82.50 | Meritorious |
| 2.25 | 73.51 - 78.00 | Very Satisfactory |
| 2.50 | 69.01 - 73.50 | Satisfactory |
| 2.75 | 64.51 - 69.00 | Fairly Satisfactory |
| 3.00 | 60.00 - 64.50 | Passed |
| 5.00 | Below 60.00 | Failed |
| INC |  | Incomplete |
| DRP |  | Dropped |
| P |  | Passed |
| F |  | Failed |

2. A grade of 5.00 or F will be given to a student who: failed to meet the minimum final grade; unofficially dropped; or has a proven case of academic dishonesty.

3. A mark of **lNC** will be given to a student who fails to complete the required minimum number of milestones due to illness or other valid reasons, provided that the projected completion results of the deficient final course requirement/s will merit a passing grade when integrated into the final computation of the grade.

4. The mark of **INC** must be completed within the succeeding term; otherwise, the grade of INC lapses and the student shall be given a grade of 5.00 or F.

5. A mark of **DRP** will be given to a student who officially dropped the course within the prescribed period.

## Tuition Fee Calculator – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17463924733453-Tuition-Fee-Calculator

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17463924733453-Tuition-Fee-Calculator#main-content)

_The **Tuition Fee Calculator** is designed to give you an approximate estimation of the fees you can anticipate for your education. However, please note that the actual fees may vary based on factors such as your chosen program, residency status, and any additional charges that may apply._

While this calculator provides a general idea, we strongly recommend referring to your official Generated Statement of Account (GSA) or reaching out to the relevant offices for more precise and detailed information regarding tuition fees. Conducting your own research and budgeting accordingly for your educational expenses is crucial.

DISCLAIMER: Please be reminded that **the Tuition Fee Calculator only covers regular courses**. For students who have filed for a **petition course**, kindly note that petitioned courses follow a **different tuition fee structure**. For more details, please refer [**HERE**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38541627793421-Petition-to-Open-a-Special-Class):

### How to use the calculator

1. Click the " **Compute my fees**" button below.
2. Create a copy of the file by selecting **File** \> **Make a copy**.

Fill in the following details:

a. Select your preferred payment scheme in cell B8. The available options are:

**Full payment**

**Installment 1** (with 5% interest - 40%, 30%, 30%)

**Installment 2** (with 7.5% interest - 20%, 40%, 40%)

b. In cell **E8**, enter the number of units you plan to enroll in for the term (excluding NSTP).

c. If you will be enrolling in an NSTP class, tick the box in cell **E11**.

For **SY 22-23 batch (Pioneer scholars)** of students, please use this calculator.

[![Click](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17463900440973)](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1r1fbP5gyY4vK46QrIhoy3XtjO0fjnKHApj7N77rVVzA/edit?gid=2119244489#gid=2119244489)

For students admitted **SY 23-24** onwards with Asenso 20% +16% tuition fee discount, please use this calculator.

[![Click](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17463900440973)](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1fVMha41iInq3j8Oajuok2598KgGN1evXK0nXVF-9UEk/edit?usp=sharing)

For students admitted **SY 23-24** onwards with Asenso 20% tuition fee discount, please use this calculator.

## Google Accounts Management – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17464024034573-Google-Accounts-Management

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17464024034573-Google-Accounts-Management#main-content)

|     |
| --- |
| ## **Overview**<br>Your MMDC Google account is your primary access point to essential student tools, including the Camu Student Portal, Google Drive, email, and other learning resources. This article explains how Google Single Sign-On (SSO) works, how to make sure you’re using the correct account, and how to manage multiple Google accounts without login issues. Use this guide to avoid access problems and ensure a smooth digital learning experience at MMDC. |

* * *

## **Table of Contents**

- [Your Official MMDC Learner Google Account](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17464024034573-Google-Accounts-Management#h_01KG4MASEBF5YYVF0JJMKA22X1)
- [The Google Single Sign-On (SSO)](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17464024034573-Google-Accounts-Management#h_01KG4HVVAW5QX8RSQKPYXJVSGN)
- [Using the Correct Google account](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17464024034573-Google-Accounts-Management#h_01KG4HYZD3TY0FD028PVN1A38P)
- [Adding another Google account](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17464024034573-Google-Accounts-Management#h_01KG4J5A45WR6E24WENWVKAHCF)
- [Logging in to Camu using google SSO](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17464024034573-Google-Accounts-Management#h_01KG4JD66ZESRESQEWPB5VGHZG)

## **Your Official MMDC Learner Google Account**

Your official MMDC Google account  follows this format:

[**lr.yourname@mmdc.mcl.edu.ph**](mailto:lr.yourname@mmdc.mcl.edu.ph)

The prefix "lr." stands for learner.

|     |
| --- |
| **📌 Note:**<br>This is different from your personal Gmail account. Your MMDC account is issued and managed by the institution and should be used for all academic-related access. |

[> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17464024034573-Google-Accounts-Management#h_01KG4J2YWK6721SAE1B9YMGDX7)

## **Single Sign-on (SSO)**

**Single Sign-on (SSO)** simplifies the login process for users by allowing them to sign in once and gain access to multiple applications. With SSO, you can seamlessly log in to your learning tools without the need to repeatedly enter your username and password. Google SSO specifically enhances your experience when using learning tools, as you can utilize your MMDC account to access these tools.

For the best experience, we recommend using Google Chrome, as it allows you to save your MMDC login information securely. As part of your suite of learning tools, My Camu also utilizes SSO for authentication, in addition to the login credentials provided by My Camu itself. This streamlines the login process and ensures convenient access to your My Camu account.

[> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17464024034573-Google-Accounts-Management#h_01KG4J2YWK6721SAE1B9YMGDX7)

## **Why This Matters**

Most MMDC systems rely on **Google Single Sign-On (SSO)**. This means that if you are logged in using the wrong Google account, you may encounter access errors—even if your username and password are correct.

Using your MMDC-issued Google account correctly ensures:

- Seamless access to **Camu**

- Proper syncing of your learning tools

- Fewer login and permission issues

- Faster resolution of support concerns


[> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17464024034573-Google-Accounts-Management#h_01KG4J2YWK6721SAE1B9YMGDX7)

## **Using the Correct Google Account**

#### How do I make sure that I am using the correct Google account?

**Step 1**

Make sure that you are using your MMDC account when working with your files and/or worksheets.

To do verify, click the account icon on the top-right side of the page.

![step](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43065555981837)

**Step 2**

The account name shown on top is the one currently logged in.

If the logged-in or default account is not your MMDC account, locate and click it from the available list.

![step](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43065508371725)

**Step 3**

The account icon will change once you have successfully changed accounts.

![step](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43065508371981)

**Step 4**

If your MMDC account is not saved in your browser, add your account to the browser's saved accounts. To add your account, see [Adding another Google Account](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17464024034573-Google-Accounts-Management#h_01KG4J5A45WR6E24WENWVKAHCF) below.

[> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17464024034573-Google-Accounts-Management#h_01KG4J2YWK6721SAE1B9YMGDX7)

## **Adding another Google Account**

### How do I add another Google account?

**Step 1**

Open a Google Chrome browser or tab.

![1.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43065508372109)

**Step 2**

Click the account icon on the top-right side of the page.

![2.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43065555983757)

**Step 3**

Select **Add another account**. You will be redirected to the Google Sign In Page.

![3.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43065508372365)

**Step 4**

Log in using your MMDC ( _@mmdc.mcl.edu.ph_) credentials.

![4.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43065508372493)

**Step 5**

The account icon will change according to the logged in user.

![5.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43065508372749)

[> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17464024034573-Google-Accounts-Management#h_01KG4J2YWK6721SAE1B9YMGDX7)

## **Logging in to Camu using Google SSO**

### How do I access My Camu?

**Step 1**

Open an internet browser or new tab. Go to [www.mycamu.com](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/www.mycamu.com).

![camu](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43065508372877)

**Step 2**

Since your MMDC account is hosted by Google, you can use the [Google SSO](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17464150752653-The-Google-Single-Sign-On-SSO-) feature to log in to MyCamu. Just click **Google**.

![camu](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43065508373133)

If you have multiple accounts logged in, select your MMDC account and enter your password (if requested).

![camu](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43065555984397)

This error message appears if the Google Account you have selected is incorrect. Make sure that you select your MMDC account to log in to Camu.

**NOTE**: If you have selected your MMDC account and you are still experiencing log in issues, you may use your Camu credentials to login.

![camu](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43065508373517)

**Step 3**

After a successful login, you will be redirected to Camu Student Portal. In the Student Portal, you may use the different features Camu including accessing the learning management system (LMS).

**![camu](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43065508373901)**

[> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17464024034573-Google-Accounts-Management#h_01KG4J2YWK6721SAE1B9YMGDX7)

## Accessing Camu – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17498570466317-Accessing-Camu

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17498570466317-Accessing-Camu#main-content)

## **Overview**

This article explains how to access and log in to **Camu**, the learning management system used by Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC).

Whether you’re a new or returning student, you’ll learn how to sign in correctly, navigate the initial access steps, and ensure you’re logged in using your MMDC credentials.

This will help you start your online classes, view your courses, and engage smoothly from your first login.

![How-Tos.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17498570463501)

### How do I access My Camu?

**Step 1**

Open an internet browser or new tab. Go to [www.mycamu.com](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/www.mycamu.com).

![camu](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17498557050381)

**Step 2**

Since your MMDC account is hosted by Google, you can use the [Google SSO](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17464150752653-The-Google-Single-Sign-On-SSO-) feature to log in to MyCamu. Just click **Google**.

![camu](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17498562310029)

If you have multiple accounts logged in, select your MMDC account and enter your password (if requested).

![camu](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17498570464781)

This error message appears if the Google Account you have selected is incorrect. Make sure that you select your MMDC account to log in to Camu.

**NOTE**: If you have selected your MMDC account and you are still experiencing log in issues, you may use your Camu credentials to login.

![camu](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17498557050765)

**Step 3**

After a successful login, you will be redirected to Camu Student Portal. In the Student Portal, you may use the different features Camu including accessing the learning management system (LMS).

**![camu](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17498562310413)**

[**Submit a request here!**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/requests/new?ticket_form_id=17374628006797)

## Accessing the Learning Management System (LMS) – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17500431094285-Accessing-the-Learning-Management-System-LMS

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17500431094285-Accessing-the-Learning-Management-System-LMS#main-content)

![How-Tos.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17500445119117)

**Step 1**

After a successful login (either by [using your Camu credentials](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17498570466317-Accessing-Camu) or by [Google SSO](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17464150752653-The-Google-Single-Sign-On-SSO-)), you will be directed to the home screen of the Camu Student Portal.

![accessing-the-lms-1.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17500458684301)

**Step 2**

In the upper left side of the Student Portal screen, click **My Learning**.

![accessing-the-lms-2.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17500433062413)

**Step 3**

You will be redirected to the home screen of the Camu LMS.

![accessing-the-lms-3.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17500449297677)

[<< Back to logging in to My Camu](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17500397674893-Accessing-Camu)

## Navigating Camu LMS – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17532530640141-Navigating-Camu-LMS

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17532530640141-Navigating-Camu-LMS#main-content)

![Click](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17532534841101)

The Camu LMS Homescreen:

![camu](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17532500315277)

**1\. MY COURSES**

Lets you return to the courses page. _(See more [My Courses](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17532593512077-My-Courses).)_

**2\. MY SCHEDULES**

This shows you your scheduled activities for the week across all courses, including synchronous sessions and due dates.

**3\. STUDENT PORTAL**

This redirects you to the Student Portal.

**4\. COURSE LIST**

Displayed in this section are the courses you are enrolled in at a given term. Clicking a course takes you to the course content.

**5\. LOG OUT**

This logs your account out of the LMS and redirects you back to the Student Portal.

**6\. TERM SELECTION**

This allows you to toggle between terms, enabling you to view the content for courses you have previously taken.

[<< Back to See all Camu LMS Categories](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17597079861645-See-all-Camu-LMS-categories)

## Exploring the Course Page – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17532624611469-Exploring-the-Course-Page

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17532624611469-Exploring-the-Course-Page#main-content)

![Click](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17532667116173)

The Course Page:

![camu-courses.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17565219441037)

**1\. COURSE DETAILS**

This shows the course details so you'll know that you're looking at the right course. This includes the course code, course title, term, and year.

**2\. CONTENT**

This is the default page for the course. It lists down the course content.

**3\. SCHEDULES**

This lists the activities scheduled for the course. It works the same as My Schedules except that it only shows the activities for that specific course.

**4\. ASSIGNMENTS**

This lists the outputs that you need to complete within the term. Although marked as assignments, this includes milestones and assessments that you need to complete. These outputs are part of the weekly instructions, so you'll still be able to view and complete them as you go through each week's content.

**5\. QUIZZES**

This lists the quizzes that you will be taking within the term. Since you'll be immersed in projects, problems, and cases, do not be surprised if you see this blank. Similar to assignments, quizzes (if there are any), will be part of your weekly activities.

**6\. GRADE BOOK**

This provides information about the outputs you are required to complete within the term, namely, the status, due date, grade, and facilitator feedback.

**7\. COURSE CONTENT**

This contains the learning materials and references that you need to go through and complete to be successful in the course.

**8\. COLLAPSE ALL**

This allows you to collapse all chapters and sub-chapters (in case you have a lot of them open).

[<< Back to My Courses](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17532593512077-My-Courses)

## Course Sections – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17532703115021-Course-Sections

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17532703115021-Course-Sections#main-content)

![Click](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17532683918093)

Each course will have the following major sections:

![course-sections.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17532744875789)

**1\. NAVIGATING THIS COURSE**

This contains how-to guides and helpful tips to make your stay at MMDC frustration-free. This includes:

- Adapting to the MMDC learning environment

- Attending synchronous sessions

- Experiencing learning in Camu

- Getting assistance from Student Services


**2\. COURSE DETAILS**

This contains course-specific information, including:

- Syllabus

- Facilitator information

- Coaching schedule and signup sheet

- Course FAQs


**3\. WEEKLY CONTENT**

This shows chapters that correspond to weeks (Weeks 1-12). Depending on the course and course design, you may see weeks grouped together (e.g., Week 6-9). This means that the PPC (problem, project, and case) assigned during that time period either takes a lot of time or requires iteration.

[<< Back to My Courses](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17532593512077-My-Courses)

## Chapters and Sub-chapters – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17533339318797-Chapters-and-Sub-chapters

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17533339318797-Chapters-and-Sub-chapters#main-content)

![Click](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17533392068109)

Each [section](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17532703115021-Course-Sections) contains a chapter, sub-chapter, and content.

![chapters-and-subchapters.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17533370013197)

Click the right arrow ( ► ) to expand the chapters and subchapters until you reach the actual content. Click the **Collapse all**button on the upper right side of the page to collapse all the sections and show only the chapter list.

## Content Prerequisites – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17533499457805-Content-Prerequisites

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17533499457805-Content-Prerequisites#main-content)

![Click](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17533510908941)

You'll notice that some chapters have prerequisite tags.

![course-prerequisites.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17533542441357)

In this example, you will not be able to view or engage with Week 4 content until you complete Week 3 _(left photo)_. However, Week 3 will be inaccessible until you complete Week 2, and so on. Although you can still expand chapters and view items, the actual content will be grayed out and inaccessible _(right photo)_. This restriction ensures that you go through all the relevant content and resources that will help you accomplish the expectations in the succeeding weeks.

## Course Content Types – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17533602560525-Course-Content-Types

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17533602560525-Course-Content-Types#main-content)

![Click](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17533645279245)

There are four icons that identify the type of content:

**1\. REGULAR CONTENT**

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17533556864013)

This indicates that the content contains information about the topic (i.e., text, images, videos, or links to additional resources).

**2\. FILE**

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17533572234125)

This indicates that the content is an attached file that you need to download to be able to view or interact with. You will not see this often as external materials will usually linked or embedded in regular content pages.

**3\. QUIZ**

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17533574569997)

This indicates that the content is a quiz that you need to take.

**4\. OUTPUT**

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17533583711501)

This indicates that the content contains instructions for an output that you need to submit. Each output will include information about the due date and the maximum number of points that you can get based on the rubrics.

[<< Back to My Courses](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17532593512077-My-Courses)

## Content Engagement – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17533904179597-Content-Engagement

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17533904179597-Content-Engagement#main-content)

![Click](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17533904177805)

Aside from engaging with content (at your own pace and time), attending synchronous sessions, or chatting with your peers using Google Chats and other social media platforms, you can also engage with your classmates and facilitators in Camu.

With each content type is a **Conversations** tab that allows you to post questions, initiate discussions, and respond to other posts.

![course-engagement.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17533947474701)

This is a good place for you to post questions or clarifications and help your classmates who may be experiencing difficulties.

![course-engagement-2.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17533889713805)

Simply type your question or insights and click **Enter**.

[<< Back to My Courses](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17532593512077-My-Courses)

- [Camu](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01H5V10RV3ES661TXFGK9APH6N&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")

## My Schedules – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17534026626061-My-Schedules

## Trial Databases – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17535376013325-Trial-Databases

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17535376013325-Trial-Databases#main-content)

This article informs students about trial databases available for a limited time, providing access to additional academic resources.

To access and explore the Trial Databases offered to MMDC students, simply click on the link provided below. These databases are part of the wide range of E-Resources available on MMCL's CLIR website. They provide an opportunity for students to familiarize themselves with various databases and their content, enabling them to enhance their research and access reliable information. By clicking the link, students can directly engage with the Trial Databases and explore the wealth of resources they offer.

## Free Access Databases – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17535434675085-Free-Access-Databases

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17535434675085-Free-Access-Databases#main-content)

This article provides a list of free-access databases and resources that students can use for academic research and scholarly information.

To conveniently access and explore the free-access databases available to MMDC students, simply click on the provided link below. These databases are part of the extensive E-Resources offered on MMCL's CLIR website, providing students with valuable access to a wide range of scholarly materials and information sources. By clicking the link, students can directly engage with the free-access databases and explore the wealth of resources they offer, enhancing their research capabilities and enriching their academic pursuits.

## Open Educational Resources – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17535470119053-Open-Educational-Resources

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17535470119053-Open-Educational-Resources#main-content)

This article explains the concept of Open Educational Resources (OER) and provides resources and platforms for accessing OER materials.

To access and explore the Open Educational Resources (OER) available to MMDC students, simply click on the provided link below. These resources are part of the wide range of E-Resources available on MMCL's CLIR website, offering students access to educational materials that are freely available for use and exploration. By clicking the link, students can directly engage with the OER and explore the diverse collection of resources. These OER materials provide valuable content that can supplement and enhance students' learning experiences, offering a cost-effective alternative to traditional textbooks and resources.

[![Click](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17535499132813)](https://www.google.com/url?q=https%3A%2F%2Fclir.mcl.edu.ph%2FResources%2FOpenEducational.aspx&sa=D&sntz=1&usg=AOvVaw2L6YEj1iSmbYhR4Mk3VKuj)

## Exploring the My Schedules page – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17536483233293-Exploring-the-My-Schedules-page

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17536483233293-Exploring-the-My-Schedules-page#main-content)

![Click](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17536467843469)

The My Schedule page:

![camu-schedules.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17536451571213)

**1\. GO TO TODAY**

If you selected a future date and want to return to the current date, just click **Go to Today**.

**2\. TIME COLUMN**

The leftmost column shows the time in one-hour increments.

**3\. CURRENT DATE**

The date on top shows the current date. Clicking this shows a date picker which enables you to jump to the date selected and view the activities and course schedules not just for that date, but also for the rest of the week. The current date is highlighted in green in the calendar view.

**4\. CURRENT TIME**

Indicated by a green line, it shows the current time of the current date.

**5\. SCHEDULED ACTIVITIES**

This shows the scheduled course schedules and activities.

**6\. VIEW SELECTION**

This enables you to change views. Views can be in **Calendar** or **Task**:

**Calendar**: Displays a week view of the calendar, starting with Sunday, together with the schedules for the week.

**Task**: This enables you view additional details about your schedule.

[<< Back to My Schedules](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17534026626061-My-Schedules)

Related to

- [Camu](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01H5V10RV3ES661TXFGK9APH6N&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")

## View your weekly schedule – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17565323230605-View-your-weekly-schedule

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17565323230605-View-your-weekly-schedule#main-content)

![How-Tos.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17565364253069)

### View weekly schedule

![weekly-schedules.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17565336084237)

The leftmost column shows the time in one-hour increments.

The succeeding columns correspond to the days of the week, starting with Sunday.

The current day is highlighted in green, and the current time is shown as a green line.

## View activities happening in the future – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17565412729101-View-activities-happening-in-the-future

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17565412729101-View-activities-happening-in-the-future#main-content)

![How-Tos.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17565436552973)

### View future activities

![future-activities.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17565423211661)

The date on top shows the current date.

Clicking the date displays the date picker, which enables you to view activities and course schedules in the next couple of weeks. When you click a future date, you will see the activities for the week, not just for the chosen date.

Take note that you cannot view schedules for courses that you have not enrolled in yet (so don't go too far in the future!).

If you clicked a future date and want to return to the current date, just click **Go to Today**button.

[<< Back to My Schedules](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17534026626061-My-Schedules)

## Attending synchronous sessions in My Camu – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17565897322765-Attending-synchronous-sessions-in-My-Camu

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17565897322765-Attending-synchronous-sessions-in-My-Camu#main-content)

![How-Tos.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17565885064077)

**Step 1**

In Camu, go to **My Schedules**.

![attending-sync-engageli-1.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17565897319821)

**Step 2**

Switch from Calendar view to **Tasks** view. This view will show you a list of activities for the week and additional details.

![attending-sync-engageli-2.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17565908631821)

**Step 3**

For courses with synchronous sessions scheduled, a **Launch meeting** button is shown. The button will be enabled on the exact day and time of the synchronous session.

![attending-sync-engageli-3.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17565885066381)

**Step 4**

Click**Launch meeting** to redirect you to your virtual meeting room. Your mentors may use the following virtual meeting rooms:

- Google Meet

- Engageli


### Accessing Synchronous Session Recordings

Select **Content** from the tab in the leftmost column. Link to the Synchronous Session Recordings may be viewed here.

![image (31).png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/29527278298765)

[<< Back to My Schedules](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17534026626061-My-Schedules)

## Exploring the Assignments page – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566077701389-Exploring-the-Assignments-page

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566077701389-Exploring-the-Assignments-page#main-content)

![Click](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17566082849677)

The Assignments page:

![exploring-assignments-page.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17566068480525)

The **Assignments** page is found when you click a specific course. Milestones and assessments assigned to you for the term are listed in this page.

**1\. TO DO**

This tab lists down all milestones or assessments assigned to you for the course you are enrolled in. It shows all upcoming assignments and unsubmitted assignments that are overdue.

**2\. OVERDUE ASSIGNMENTS**

This lists down all unsubmitted assignments that are overdue.

**3\. UPCOMING ASSIGNMENTS**

This shows all assignments assigned that you need to complete for the course you are enrolled in.

**NOTE**: Although they are marked as assignments, the outputs to be submitted through this feature include milestones and assessments. These outputs are part of the weekly instructions, so you'll still be able to view and complete them as you go through each week's content.

**4\. ALL PAST WORKS**

You'll see in this tab all the past works assigned to you that you were able to complete.

[<< Back to Submitting Outputs](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566038499341-Submitting-Outputs)

## Submit outputs in Camu – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566216855693-Submit-outputs-in-Camu

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566216855693-Submit-outputs-in-Camu#main-content)

![How-Tos.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17566212871181)

**Step 1**

In My Schedules page or in the Assignments page, click on the assignment to complete.

![sub1.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17566196793485)

**Step 2**

Once opened, you will see details about the output, including the due date.

![sub2.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17566201317005)

**Step 3**

Instructions and details about the output are shown in the description of the assignment. This may contain links to examples and other useful references.

**NOTE**: Be sure to**read the instructions carefully** for you to fully understand what is being asked for the assignment. **Outputs are expected to be uploaded in Google Drive.**

**![sub3.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17566212872461)**

Completion status is shown in the page. This lets you know whether you have submitted the output or not.

![sub4.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17566196794765)

This changes to **Submitted** once you submit an output.

![sub5.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17566201318413)

**Step 4**

You may also view the **Rubrics used** for the output. This allows you to review the criteria used to assess your output. It also helps you focus your efforts on relevant aspects.

![sub6.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17566216851597)

This is a sample rubric. It shows the different criteria and its description to help you understand how your output is assessed. The total points is also shown.

![sub7.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17566188308877)

**Step 5**

Click the **Submit assignment** button once you have read the instructions, know what you are supposed to submit, and understand the level of quality expected from your output.

![sub8.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17566201322253)

Upon clicking the **Submit assignment** button, you will be shown a text editor where you can type your output or copy and paste from another source (such as Google Docs).

Depending on the type of output required, you can add a **website URL** or **upload a file**.

**NOTE**: When entering a URL, make sure that you include the protocol. For instance, instead of simply typing www.google.com, you need to type **https://www.google.com**.

![sub9.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17566212874381)

Once you've added any type of content, the **Enter an answer to submit** button changes to **Submit assignment**. Click this button to submit your output.

![sub10.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17566188309901)

**Step 6**

To view the output that you submitted, click **View Submission** on the top right-hand part of the output page.

**NOTE**: You can edit and resubmit your output until the due date.

![sub11.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17566201322509)

[<< Back to Submitting Outputs](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566038499341-Submitting-Outputs)

Related to

- [Camu](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01H5V10RV3ES661TXFGK9APH6N&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")

## Editing your course submissions – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566367340301-Editing-your-course-submissions

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566367340301-Editing-your-course-submissions#main-content)

![How-To](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17566563663501)

**Step 1**

Open the Task/Assignment/Assessment.

![media1.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17566339170317)

**Step 2**

Click **View Submission**.

![media2.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17566367336973)

**Step 3**

Click **Edit**.

![media3.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17566376984077)

**Step 4**

Click the “-” (minus/negative) button on the right side of your submission. Replace your submission with a new one, then click **Submit assignment**.

**NOTE**: You can edit and resubmit your output ONLY until the due date.

![media4.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17566347567629)

## Google Meet – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566580445069-Google-Meet

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566580445069-Google-Meet#main-content)

|     |
| --- |
| ## **Overview**<br>This article explains how to use **Google Meet** for your MMDC online classes, meetings, lectures, and academic sessions. It covers how to join or start a meeting, navigate common features (camera, mic, chat, screen share), and make the most of the platform for your virtual learning. Use this guide to feel confident participating in MMDC online sessions without technical confusion. |

* * *

## **Table of Contents**

- [Join a Meeting with a Code](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566580445069-Google-Meet#h_01KG4NCJQX36R287VTF3TB53N3)
- [Join a Meeting via Email](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566580445069-Google-Meet#h_01KG4NHAH0ME637XMK0TZBNVN6)
- [Join a Meeting via Camu](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566580445069-Google-Meet#h_01KG4NM0JV10NYR01FV2M95JJH)
- [Google Meet Controls](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566580445069-Google-Meet#h_01KG4NT6CKK22TR93S295PNSVS)
- [Google Meet keyboard shortcuts](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566580445069-Google-Meet#h_01KG4NZCAVC13XQXVWA0KASWZ9)
- [Send a message via meeting chat box](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566580445069-Google-Meet#h_01KG4P2E9YDWEPS3VB6EB9T4PB)
- [Present during a meet](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566580445069-Google-Meet#h_01KG4P5XT404FW8T0T40NG87Q4)
- [Join a breakout room](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566580445069-Google-Meet#h_01KG4P8YWWFT3NSAFHYNX14QVD)

* * *

## **Join a Meeting with a Code**

**Step 1**

Open a Google Chrome browser or tab.

![v1.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066246157965)

**Step 2**

Go to [Google Meet](http://meet.google.com/).

NOTE: [Verify](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17498071646349-Using-the-correct-Google-account) that your MMDC Account is logged in.

![v2.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066259888269)

**Step 3**

Enter the meeting code or nickname provided to you.

Nicknames are only for people belonging to the same organization ( _i.e., mmdc.mcl.edu.ph_).

![v3.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066246159117)

**Step 4**

Click **Join**.

![v4.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066259894157)

**Step 5**

You will be redirected to a preview of your device settings. You may choose to turn your microphone and camera before joining the meeting.

**NOTE**: Some meetings require the approval of the organizer for you to be able to join the meeting.

**READ**: [Attending synchronous sessions in Camu LMS](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17565897322765-Attending-synchronous-sessions-in-My-Camu)

![v5.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066259894669)

Control buttons in red background means that your microphone and camera is turned off.

![v6.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066246159885)

[> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566580445069-Google-Meet#h_01KG4J2YWK6721SAE1B9YMGDX7)

* * *

## **Join a Meeting via Email**

**Step 1**

Open a Google Chrome browser or tab.

![v1.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066246157965)

**Step 2**

Go to [Google Meet](http://meet.google.com/).

NOTE: [Verify](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17498071646349-Using-the-correct-Google-account) that your MMDC Account is logged in.

![v2.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066259888269)

**Step 3**

Open the email invitation for the meeting.

![email](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066246160525)

**Step 4**

Click **Join****with Google Meet** button to join the meeting.

![joining-a-meeting-with-email.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066246160909)

**Step 5**

You will be redirected to a preview of your device settings. You may choose to turn your microphone and camera before joining the meeting.

**NOTE**: Some meetings require the approval of the organizer for you to be able to join the meeting.

**READ**: [Attending synchronous sessions in Camu LMS](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17565897322765-Attending-synchronous-sessions-in-My-Camu)

![v5.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066259894669)

Control buttons in red background means that your microphone and camera is turned off.

![v6.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066246159885)

[> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566580445069-Google-Meet#h_01KG4J2YWK6721SAE1B9YMGDX7)

## **Join a Meeting via Camu**

**Step 1**

In Camu, go to **My Schedules**.

![camu1.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066259897741)

**Step 2**

Switch from Calendar view to **Tasks** view. This view will show you a list of activities for the week and additional details.

![camu2.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066259900685)

**Step 3**

For courses with synchronous sessions scheduled, a **Launch meeting** button is shown. The button will be enabled on the exact day and time of the synchronous session.

![camu3.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066259903757)

**Step 4**

Click **Launch meeting** to redirect you to your virtual meeting room.

![camu4.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066246162573)

**Step 5**

You will be redirected to a preview of your device settings. You may choose to turn your microphone and camera before joining the meeting.

**NOTE**: Some meetings require the approval of the organizer for you to be able to join the meeting.

**READ**: [Attending synchronous sessions in Camu LMS](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17565897322765-Attending-synchronous-sessions-in-My-Camu)

![v5.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066259894669)

Control buttons in red background means that your microphone and camera is turned off.

![v6.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066246159885)

[> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566580445069-Google-Meet#h_01KG4J2YWK6721SAE1B9YMGDX7)

* * *

## **Google Meet Controls**

**1\. MEETING WINDOW**

The meeting window displays the meeting participants in tiles, the call controls, and the activity controls.

Participants' video or avatar are shown in each tile.

![1-google-meet.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066246162829)

**2\. MEETING CODE**

Meeting codes are given by the organizer to each participant. Participants may use this code to join the meeting.

![2-google-meet.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066259904909)

**3\. CALL CONTROLS**

This section shows the controls to enable participants to:

- turn the microphone, camera, and captions on or off;

- present by sharing their screen, window, or tab;

- change their meeting settings;

- and leave the meeting by ending the call.


![3-google-meet.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066259905421)

**4\. ACTIVITIES PANEL**

This option lists all other tools you may use during the call. This includes breakout rooms and polls. It also includes the chat feature and the option to see the list of participants of the meeting.

![4-google-meet.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066246163597)

**5\. IN-CALL ICONS**

Know the use of each icon in the control panel of Google Meet. You will also learn when a control is turned on or off.

Learn the keyboard shortcuts for these controls [here](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17569674212237-Google-Meet-Keyboard-Shortcuts).

![5-google-meet-controls.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066259906189)

[> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566580445069-Google-Meet#h_01KG4J2YWK6721SAE1B9YMGDX7)

## Google Meet Keyboard Shortcuts

![google-meet-keyboard-shortcuts.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066259907213)

[> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566580445069-Google-Meet#h_01KG4J2YWK6721SAE1B9YMGDX7)

## **Send a Message via Meeting Chat Box**

**Step 1**

Join a Google Meet.

![1-sending-a-message-in-meeting.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066246164621)

**Step 2**

Once inside the meeting room, you may send and view messages through the chat box.

Click the **Chat**button at the lower right of the meeting screen. Chat box will appear afterwards. You may now start sending and viewing messages.

![2-sending-a-message-in-meeting.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066246165133)

**Step 3**

Start typing your message. When you're done typing, click**Send**post your message.

**TIP**: If you share a file in the chat, make sure you give other participants access to it.

![3-sending-a-message-in-meeting.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066246165261)

**Step 4**

Message thread is displayed at the chat box.

![4-sending-a-message-in-meeting.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066246166285)

[> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566580445069-Google-Meet#h_01KG4J2YWK6721SAE1B9YMGDX7)

* * *

## Present during a Meet

**Step 1**

Join a Google Meet.

NOTE: You may join a meeting by [using a code](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17567504042637-Join-a-meeting-with-a-code) or through an [email invite](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17567548588301-Join-a-Meeting-via-Email).

![1present.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066246167309)

**Step 2**

At the bottom controls, click **Present now**.

![2present.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066259913485)

**Step 3**

Select Your entire screen, A window, or A tab.

- If you present a Chrome tab, it shares that tab's audio by default.

- To present a different tab, select the tab you want to present, click Share this tab instead.


![3present.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066259913997)

**Step 4**

Select the window or tab to share. Click **Share**to start presenting your screen, tab or window.

Another tile will appear showing the shared screen, window or tab.

![4present.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066246169101)

**Step 5**

To stop presenting, click **Stop sharing** button at the bottom of your meeting screen.

![5present.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066246169229)

If the option above is missing, you can click **Present now**then select **Stop presenting**. The shared screen, window or tab tile will be hidden.

![6present.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43066246171021)

[> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566580445069-Google-Meet#h_01KG4J2YWK6721SAE1B9YMGDX7)

* * *

## **Join a Breakout Room**

**Step 1**

The meeting organizer will invite you to join a breakout room.

**Step 2**

When your moderator invites you to join a breakout room, you'll see a prompt on your screen. Click **Join**.

**Step 3**

Once you're in a breakout room, you can speak to or send chat messages to other participants.

[> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17566580445069-Google-Meet#h_01KG4J2YWK6721SAE1B9YMGDX7)

## eBooks – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17568190632077-eBooks

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17568190632077-eBooks#main-content)

This article provides information on accessing and utilizing eBooks available in the MMDC online library for academic purposes.

## eBooks

To access MMDC eBooks directly, simply click on the provided link below. This will allow you to conveniently explore and utilize the wide range of eBooks available for your academic needs at MMDC. Whether you're seeking textbooks, reference materials, or supplementary resources, the eBooks platform offers a comprehensive collection to support your studies. Start exploring the MMDC eBooks today by clicking the link below.

**![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/18421735655309)**

### [![Zendesk](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17568183594765)](https://clir.mcl.edu.ph/Resources/MMDCEbooks.aspx)

### Britannica Academic

Britannica Academic is a comprehensive resource that combines the renowned Encyclopaedia Britannica with academic magazines and periodicals. This unique combination offers a diverse range of reliable and credible sources specifically curated to meet the research and productivity needs of colleges and academic libraries. With Britannica Academic, students and researchers gain access to a wealth of information and knowledge from trusted sources, ensuring that their academic endeavors are well-supported and enriched. Whether you're conducting in-depth research, seeking authoritative references, or exploring various academic disciplines, Britannica Academic is a valuable tool that empowers you to achieve academic excellence.

To log in, please enter the following credentials: ID: **mccl111000**

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17568078267021)

### Gale Books

Gale References offers an extensive collection of primary and secondary sources, making it the most comprehensive package available to libraries. It covers a wide range of research areas and disciplines, catering to the needs of undergraduate students as well as experienced researchers. With Gale References, students and researchers gain access to a vast array of reliable and authoritative resources, enabling them to delve deep into their fields of study. Whether you're starting your academic journey or conducting advanced research, Gale References provides the necessary tools and materials to support your scholarly pursuits and enhance your learning experience.

To log in, please enter the following credentials: Password: **balance**

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17568124465677)

### Vital Source eTextbooks

The library offers a wide range of resources with subscriptions to over 20,000 titles from 4 reputable publishers. These publishers include C&E eBooks, Cengage eTextbooks, Pearson (Selected Titles only), and Wiley Digital Textbooks. With this extensive collection, students have access to a diverse selection of educational materials to support their studies and research.

While accessing these resources, it's important to note that there may be limitations on the number of concurrent accesses allowed. Additionally, students have the flexibility to read the books online directly through their browsers. For offline reading, they can utilize the desktop or mobile app called "VitalSource Bookshelf."

Follow the steps below to access the resources:

1. Click the Vital Source image on the CLIR's eBooks page (linked above)
2. Click on the Create a VitalSource Account button.
3. Provide all the necessary information. Use your MMDC Gmail account.
4. Click the Create Account button.

**[_\*Watch a walkthrough video here._](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1KOlAfFdAqenJCBq2YfQTk4VIUKD8N9E4/view)**

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17568169135885)

## eJournals – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17568580755085-eJournals

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17568580755085-eJournals#main-content)

This article provides information on accessing and utilizing eJournals available in the MMDC online library for academic research.

### eJournals

To directly access MMDC eJournals, simply click on the provided link below. These eJournals are a valuable resource available to college students on a wide range of subjects and disciplines. By clicking the link, students can easily access and explore the eJournals, gaining access to scholarly articles, research papers, and other academic publications. These eJournals provide a wealth of knowledge and information, supporting students in their studies, research, and academic pursuits. Take advantage of this convenient access to MMDC eJournals by clicking the link below and start exploring the vast array of valuable resources at your fingertips.

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17568328455565)

[![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17568342019981)](https://clir.mcl.edu.ph/Resources/Ejournals.aspx)

### ScienceDirect

Access the provided link below to explore a leading full-text scientific database that offers a vast collection of journal articles and book chapters. This database includes content from over 2,500 peer-reviewed journals and over 11,000 books, providing access to a wide range of scholarly resources. With more than 9.5 million articles and chapters currently available, and an impressive growth rate of nearly 0.5 million additions each year, this database ensures access to up-to-date and reliable scientific information.

Follow the steps below to access the resources:

1. Visit the ScienceDirect Website
2. Click on " **Sign In**" and choose to " **sign in via your institution**"
3. Under " **Find your institution**", enter " **Malayan Colleges Laguna**" as the institution name.
4. Type in your MMDC Gmail account.
5. Verify your email and access the Elsevier services via the link sent to your MMDC email inbox

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17568426727949)

### Philippine E-Journals

Philippine E-Journals serves as an online database and repository of academic journals covering various disciplines. It provides a centralized platform for accessing scholarly articles from different sources. As a valuable resource for college students, Philippine E-Journals offers a wide range of academic journals that contribute to the knowledge and understanding of different fields of study. By utilizing this platform, students can conveniently explore and access a diverse collection of scholarly articles relevant to their research and academic interests. With its comprehensive database and accessible interface, Philippine E-Journals supports students in their quest for reliable and credible information. Expand your knowledge and enhance your research capabilities by utilizing the resources available through Philippine E-Journals.

Follow the steps below to access the resources:

1. Click the Philippine E-Journals image on the CLIR's eJournal's page (linked above)
2. Click the Log In button from the menu.

3. Use **mclpej** as both the username and password.

4. Click the Login button.


![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17568559160973)

## MMDC E-Library & Services – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17568939949965-MMDC-E-Library-Services

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17568939949965-MMDC-E-Library-Services#main-content)

This article provides information on accessing and utilizing MMDC E-Library & Services available for the students.

By clicking the button below, college students can conveniently access all the available resources and library services offered by MMDC. This link serves as a gateway to a comprehensive range of valuable academic materials, research databases, e-books, e-journals, and other essential resources that support students in their learning and research endeavors. Whether you need access to scholarly articles, reference materials, or specialized databases, this centralized platform provides a seamless and user-friendly experience. Make the most of your academic journey by utilizing the MMDC Resources and Library Services accessible through the provided link.

[![Zendesk](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17569210122509)](https://clir.mcl.edu.ph/Resources/MMDCResources.aspx)

This will take you to Center for Learning and Information Resources or CLIR's  home screen for MMDC, subdivided into the following:

1. Library Services

2. E-Resources

3. Local Databases


## Library Services

### Connect with CORA

Cora, the online librarian from CLIR, is ready to assist college students with their inquiries and provide prompt assistance. You can reach out to Cora from Monday to Saturday, between 8:00am to 5:00pm. Whether you have questions about research resources, need help finding specific information, or require guidance on utilizing library services, Cora is dedicated to providing immediate and reliable support. Don't hesitate to contact Cora for any assistance you need during your academic journey.

[![Zendesk](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17568976888973)](https://clir.mcl.edu.ph/Resources/Connect-with-cora.aspx)

### Online Document Delivery Service

Students have the option to utilize this service to make requests for electronic copies of books, theses, and e-journals. It's important to note that these e-copies are accessible for a limited duration. Therefore, students are advised to make use of this service promptly to ensure they can access the materials they need within the specified timeframe.

[![Zendesk](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17568971753613)](https://clir.mcl.edu.ph/Resources/MMDCdocumentdelivery.aspx)

### Book-A-Librarian

The Book-A-Librarian service is an online platform designed for students who wish to schedule an orientation session about CLIR (College Library and Information Resource Center) and its range of services. By booking a librarian, students have the opportunity to gain a comprehensive understanding of the basic, advanced, and subscribed electronic resources offered by CLIR. This orientation session aims to provide students with valuable insights and guidance on how to effectively utilize the library's resources to support their academic journey. To participate in this orientation, students can easily schedule a session through the Book-A-Librarian online system.

## MMCL Library Visit

The MMCL Library Visit Booking process is designed for MMDC students who wish to access the physical resources and facilities available at the Mapúa Malayan Colleges Laguna campus. By booking a visit, students can take advantage of the library’s resources and other on-site services to support academic success. This guide outlines the simple steps to schedule a visit, along with important reminders to ensure a smooth and productive library experience.

[![Click here. (3 × 1 in) (1).png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/37124051444749)](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37123995828621-How-to-Book-a-Library-Visit-at-MMCL)

## See all Camu LMS categories – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17597079861645-See-all-Camu-LMS-categories

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17597079861645-See-all-Camu-LMS-categories#main-content)

# Camu Learning Management System (LMS)

Camu is a digital campus that combines a Student Information System (SIS) and Learning Management System (LMS). This means you no longer have to bookmark or remember a bunch of sites and login details.

The LMS, in particular, stores and organizes the content and tools you’ll need; supporting you, the learner, as you go through and engage in the course you’re enrolled in.

![accessing](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17597091017101)![navigating](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17597103440013)![My](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17597095955981)

[Accessing Camu](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17500397674893-Accessing-Camu) [Navigating Camu LMS](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17532530640141-Navigating-Camu-LMS) [My Courses](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17532593512077-My-Courses)

## **Create a New Folder**

**Step 1**

Open a Google Chrome browser or tab.

![1-new](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267068593677)

**Step 2**

Go to [Google Drive](http://drive.google.com/).

NOTE: [Verify](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17498071646349-Using-the-correct-Google-account) that your MMDC Account is logged in.

![2-creating-a-folder.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267098474637)

**Step 3**

Click the **New**button then select **Folder**.

![3-creating-a-folder.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267098475149)

**Step 4**

A prompt will appear which will allow you to name your folder. Click **Create**once you're done naming your folder.

![4-creating-a-folder.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267098475917)

**Step 5**

Your new folder is now listed under the _Folders_ section of your drive.

![5-creating-a-folder.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267098476557)

##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17597340884493-Google-Drive\#h_01KG4J2YWK6721SAE1B9YMGDX7)

* * *

## **Upload a File**

**Step 1**

Open a Google Chrome browser or tab.

![1-new](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267068593677)

**Step 2**

Go to [Google Drive](http://drive.google.com/).

NOTE: [Verify](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17498071646349-Using-the-correct-Google-account) that your MMDC Account is logged in.

![2-creating-a-folder.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267098474637)

**Step 3**

Click the **New**button then select **File upload**.

![uploading-a-file-3.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267098476941)

**Step 4**

An upload file dialog box will appear which allows you to select the file(s) you wish to upload. Choose the file(s) then click **Open**.

![4-uploading-a-file-4.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267068595597)

**Step 5**

File upload status is displayed at the lower right section of the screen. It tells the current percentage of upload completion.

![5-uploading-a-file-5.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267068596237)

**Step 6**

If the upload is complete, the thumbnail of the file is added to the _Files_ section of your drive.

![6-uploading-a-file-6.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267068596621)

##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17597340884493-Google-Drive\#h_01KG4J2YWK6721SAE1B9YMGDX7)

* * *

## **Upload a Folder**

**Step 1**

Open a Google Chrome browser or tab.

![1-new](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267068593677)

**Step 2**

Go to [Google Drive](http://drive.google.com/).

NOTE: [Verify](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17498071646349-Using-the-correct-Google-account) that your MMDC Account is logged in.

![2-creating-a-folder.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267098474637)

**Step 3**

Click the **New**button then select **Folder upload**.

![3-uploading-a-folder-3.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267098477965)

**Step 4**

An upload folder dialog box will appear which allows you to select the folder you wish to upload. Choose the folder then click **Upload**.

![4-uploading-a-folder-4.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267068597517)

**Step 5**

Google Drive will ask you to confirm the upload of all the files inside the selected folder. Click **Upload**to continue uploading.

![5-uploading-a-folder-5.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267068597645)

**Step 6**

Folder upload status is displayed at the lower right section of the screen. It tells the current percentage of upload completion.

![6-uploading-a-folder-6.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267068598029)

**Step 7**

If the upload is complete, the folder of the file is added to the _Folders_ section of your drive.

![7-uploading-a-folder-7.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267068598413)

##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17597340884493-Google-Drive\#h_01KG4J2YWK6721SAE1B9YMGDX7)

* * *

## **Share a File or a Folder**

**Step 1**

Open a Google Chrome browser or tab.

![1-new](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267068593677)

**Step 2**

Go to [Google Drive](http://drive.google.com/).

NOTE: [Verify](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17498071646349-Using-the-correct-Google-account) that your MMDC Account is logged in.

![2-creating-a-folder.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267098474637)

**Step 3**

Locate the file or folder that you wish to share.

![3-sharing-files-and-folder-3.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267098481165)

**Step 4**

Right-click on the file or folder then select **Share**.

![4-sharing-files-and-folder-4.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267068598925)

**Step 5**

A dialog box will appear for the file or folder sharing settings. This also shows who is the owner of the file or folder and everyone with current access to the file or folder.

![5-sharing-files-and-folder-5.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267098481933)

You may include specific people or groups to which you would like to share the files or folders with.

To do this, just input their names or email addresses to the **Add people and groups** box in the dialog box. You may also add a message for the person or people you are sharing the file with.

![5a-sharing-files-and-folder-5a.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267068600205)

_General Access_ grants permission for people and groups, or to anyone with link to access the file or folder.

If you chose **Anyone with the link** or click the **Copy link**, Google Drive will generate a link of the file which you can also share.

![5b-sharing-files-and-folder-5b.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267098484365)

**Step 6**

Click **Done** once you have updated the sharing settings.

![6-sharing-files-and-folder-6.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/43267068602765)[> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17597340884493-Google-Drive#h_01KG4J2YWK6721SAE1B9YMGDX7)

## Sharing Files and Folders – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17598226663053-Sharing-Files-and-Folders

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17598226663053-Sharing-Files-and-Folders#main-content)

![How-To](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598191796749)

**Step 1**

Open a Google Chrome browser or tab.

![1-new](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598234627725)

**Step 2**

Go to [Google Drive](http://drive.google.com/).

NOTE: [Verify](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17498071646349-Using-the-correct-Google-account)that your MMDC Account is logged in.

![2-creating-a-folder.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598181905293)

**Step 3**

Locate the file or folder that you wish to share.

![3-sharing-files-and-folder-3.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598191797773)

**Step 4**

Right-click on the file or folder then select **Share**.

![4-sharing-files-and-folder-4.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598232746509)

**Step 5**

A dialog box will appear for the file or folder sharing settings. This also shows who is the owner of the file or folder and everyone with current access to the file or folder.

![5-sharing-files-and-folder-5.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598218287501)

You may include specific people or groups to which you would like to share the files or folders with.

To do this, just input their names or email addresses to the **Add people and groups** box in the dialog box. You may also add a message for the person or people you are sharing the file with.

![5a-sharing-files-and-folder-5a.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598191799437)

_General Access_ grants permission for people and groups, or to anyone with link to access the file or folder.

If you chose **Anyone with the link** or click the **Copy link**, Google Drive will generate a link of the file which you can also share.

![5b-sharing-files-and-folder-5b.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598203245709)

**Step 6**

Click **Done**once you have updated the sharing settings.

![6-sharing-files-and-folder-6.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598181906829)

[<< Back to Google Drive](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17597340884493-Google-Drive)

- [Google](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01H5V4AMYV4K42ZDRD63QD80A7&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")
- [Google Drive](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01H5V4B6NH7GXVQRA6JFC35JRH&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")

## Preventing people from downloading, printing, or copying your file – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17598258912397-Preventing-people-from-downloading-printing-or-copying-your-file

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17598258912397-Preventing-people-from-downloading-printing-or-copying-your-file#main-content)

**![How-To](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598295116685)**

**Step 1**

Open a Google Chrome browser or tab.

![1-new](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598258908685)

**Step 2**

Go to [Google Drive](http://drive.google.com/).

NOTE: [Verify](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17498071646349-Using-the-correct-Google-account)that your MMDC Account is logged in.

![2-creating-a-folder.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598286022541)

**Step 3**

Locate the file or folder that you wish to share.

![3-sharing-files-and-folder-3.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598263567757)

**Step 4**

Right-click on the file or folder then select **Share**.

![4-sharing-files-and-folder-4.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598278810381)

**Step 5**

Click the **Settings**(gear button) at the top.

![5a-preventing-people-from-downloading-5a.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598270176141)

**Step 6**

Uncheck **Viewers and commenters can see the option to download, print, and copy**.

**NOTE**: You can't apply this setting to a folder, but you can apply it to individual files in the folder.

You can limit how people share, print, download, and copy within Google Drive, Docs, Sheets, and Slides, but you can't stop how others share the file content in other ways.

![6-preventing-people-from-downloading-5b.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598263570317)

[<< Back to Google Drive](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17597340884493-Google-Drive)

- [Google Drive](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01H5V4B6NH7GXVQRA6JFC35JRH&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17598318470029-Preventing-people-from-sharing-your-file-or-folder#main-content)

Open a Google Chrome browser or tab.

![1-new](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598315286797)

**Step 2**

Go to [Google Drive](http://drive.google.com/).

NOTE: [Verify](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17498071646349-Using-the-correct-Google-account)that your MMDC Account is logged in.

![2-creating-a-folder.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598327017101)

Locate the file or folder that you wish to share.

## Stop sharing files and folders – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17598388391821-Stop-sharing-files-and-folders

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17598388391821-Stop-sharing-files-and-folders#main-content)

![How-To](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598397512589)

**Step 1**

Open a Google Chrome browser or tab.

![1-new](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598411873677)

**Step 2**

Go to [Google Drive](http://drive.google.com/).

NOTE: [Verify](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17498071646349-Using-the-correct-Google-account)that your MMDC Account is logged in.

![2-creating-a-folder.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17598373259917)
