## Supported files and allowed file sizes – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17673405039245-Supported-files-and-allowed-file-sizes

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17673405039245-Supported-files-and-allowed-file-sizes#main-content)

### ![Click](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17673399623437)

### FILE SIZES

The following are the maximum file sizes you can store in Google Drive:

1. Documents
   - Up to 1.02 million characters.

   - If you convert a text document to Google Docs format, it can be up to 50 MB.

2. Spreadsheets
   - Up to 10 million cells or 18,278 columns (column ZZZ) for spreadsheets that are created in or converted to Google Sheets.

   - Up to 10 million cells or 18,278 columns for spreadsheets imported from Microsoft Excel. The limits are the same for Excel and CSV imports.
     - When you convert a document from Excel to Google Sheets, any cell with more than 50,000 characters will be removed in Sheets.

3. Presentations
   - Up to 100 MB for presentations converted to Google Slides.

4. Google Sites
   - Up to 15,000,000 characters per page.

   - Up to 40,000,000 characters per site.

   - Up to 10,000 pages per site.

   - Up to 15,000 images per site.

5. All other files
   - Up to 5 TB.

### SUPPORTED FILES

Any file type can be stored in Drive. These are the most common file types you can preview in Google Drive:

1. General Files
   - Archive files (.ZIP, .RAR, tar, gzip)

   - Audio formats (MP3, MPEG, WAV, .ogg, .opus)

   - Image files (.JPEG, .PNG, .GIF, .BMP, .TIFF, .SVG)

   - Markup/Code (.CSS, .HTML, .PHP, .C, .CPP, .H, .HPP, .JS, .java, .py)

   - Text files (.TXT)

   - Video files (WebM, .MPEG4, .3GPP, .MOV, .AVI, .MPEGPS, .WMV, .FLV, .ogg)

2. Adobe Files
   - Autodesk AutoCad (.DXF)

   - Illustrator (.AI)

   - Photoshop (.PSD)

   - Portable Document Format (.PDF)

   - PostScript (.EPS, .PS)

   - Scalable Vector Graphics (.SVG)

   - Tagged Image File Format (.TIFF) - best with RGB .TIFF images

   - TrueType (.TTF)

3. Microsoft Files
   - Excel (.XLS and .XLSX)

   - PowerPoint (.PPT and .PPTX)

   - Word (.DOC and .DOCX)

   - XML Paper Specification (.XPS)

   - Password-protected Microsoft Office files

4. Apple Files
   - Editor files (.key, .numbers)

[<< Back to Google Drive](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17597340884493-Google-Drive)

## File and Folder Sharing: General Access options – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17673417672717-File-and-Folder-Sharing-General-Access-options

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17673417672717-File-and-Folder-Sharing-General-Access-options#main-content)

![Click](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17673410140685)

### General Access Options

There are several ways to allow access to your file or folder. These options depend on if your Google Account is through work, school, or Gmail.

- **Public**: Anyone can search on Google and get access to your file, without signing in to their Google Account. If you use aGoogle Account through work or school, you may not see this option.

- **Anyone with the link**: Anyone who has the link can use your file, without signing in to their Google Account. If you use a Google Account through work or school, you may not see this option.


- **Your** **organization**: If you use a Google Account through work or school, anyone signed in to an account in your organization can open the file.


- **Restricted**: Only people with access can open the file.

## Add comments to a document – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17673870259981-Add-comments-to-a-document

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17673870259981-Add-comments-to-a-document#main-content)

![How-To](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17673856352909)

**Step 1**

Open your document in [Google Docs](http://docs.google.com/).

![1-adding-a-comment-1.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17673848756621)

**Step 2**

Highlight the text you want to comment on.

![2-adding-a-comment-2.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17673887467405)

**Step 3**

Add comment by clicking the **Add comment**button.

![3-adding-a-comment-3.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17673856354829)

You may also add comment to the selected text by right-clicking and the selecting **Comment** or using the keyboard shortcut by pressing **Ctrl + Alt + M**.

![3a-adding-a-comment-3a.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17673848758413)

A shortcut icon also appears on the right side of the paragraph.

![3b-adding-a-comment-3b.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17673887468557)

**Step 4**

To tag other people in a comment, just key in the "@" sign followed by their email address. Once you have keyed in the "@" sign, people from your contacts or whom you have shared files with will be listed down for selection. Each person will get an email with your comment and a link to the file.

![4-adding-a-comment-4.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17673863659405)

**Step 5**

Type your comment in and then click **Comment**or **Assign**.

![5-adding-a-comment-5.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17673848760077)

[<< Back to Google Docs, Sheets, and Slides](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17673627287437-Google-Docs-Sheets-and-Slides)

- [Google Docs](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01H5V4BD3W0FX00M76CRTV7ZCQ&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")

## Suggest edits on a document – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17674099113741-Suggest-edits-on-a-document

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17674099113741-Suggest-edits-on-a-document#main-content)

![How-To](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674099103373)

_**NOTE**_:_This feature is only available in Google Docs. You can propose changes to the document without affecting its original content. Your suggested changes won't be applied unless the document owner approves of the proposed changes. For you to be able to suggest edits, you must have edit or comment access to the document._

**Step 1**

Open your document in [Google Docs](http://docs.google.com/).

![1-suggest-a-comment-1.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674107961485)

**Step 2**

Make sure you are in **Suggesting mode**.

![2-suggest-edit-1.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674113549197)

![2a-suggest-edit-1a.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674123081869)

**Step 3**

Simply begin typing the proposed changes. Your suggestion will appear in a new color. Should there be any part of the document that you suggest to be deleted, it would appear to be crossed out. None of the original text will be deleted unless it is approved by the owner of the document.

![3-suggest-edit-2.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674107962509)

**Step 4**

The document owner will be notified of your edit suggestions via email. When they click on the suggestion, they can **Accept** or **Reject** it.

![4-suggest-edit-3.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674130070797)

[<< Back to Google Docs, Sheets, and Slides](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17673627287437-Google-Docs-Sheets-and-Slides)

## Add comments to a spreadsheet – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17674275789709-Add-comments-to-a-spreadsheet

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17674275789709-Add-comments-to-a-spreadsheet#main-content)

![How-To](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674306597389)

**Step 1**

Open your document in [Google Sheets](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets).

![1-add-comment-1.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674291805453)

**Step 2**

Select the cell or text you want to comment on.

![2-add-comment-2.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674294941581)

**Step 3**

Add comment by clicking the **Add comment** button.

![3-add-comment-3.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674306598157)

You may also add comment to the selected text or cell by right-clicking and the selecting **Comment** or using the keyboard shortcut by pressing **Ctrl + Alt + M**.

![3a-add-comment-3a.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674291806989)

**Step 4**

To tag other people in a comment, just key in the "@" sign followed by their email address. Once you have keyed in the "@" sign, people from your contacts or whom you have shared files with will be listed down for selection. Each person will get an email with your comment and a link to the file.

![4-add-comment-4.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674294943373)

**Step 5**

Type your comment in and then click **Comment** or **Assign**.

![5-add-comment-5.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674306599309)

[<< Back to Google Docs, Sheets, and Slides](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17673627287437-Google-Docs-Sheets-and-Slides)

- [Google](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01H5V4AMYV4K42ZDRD63QD80A7&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")
- [Google Sheets](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01H5V4BHZ67DACJMG8PYNBR6TK&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")

## Making a copy of a spreadsheet/ document/ slides – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17674380715917-Making-a-copy-of-a-spreadsheet-document-slides

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17674380715917-Making-a-copy-of-a-spreadsheet-document-slides#main-content)

![How-To](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674380712717)

**NOTES**:

1. The steps below are also applicable when making copies of Google Documents or Slides.

2. Make sure that you are [using the correct Google Account](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17498071646349-Using-the-correct-Google-account).


**Step 1**

Open the document.

If Google prompts " **You need access**" while trying to open the file, you may troubleshoot this by following these [steps](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17674597519501-Google-prompts-You-need-access-).

![1-make-a-copy-1.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674389782797)

**Step 2**

In the menu, click **File**the select **Make a Copy**.

![2-make-a-copy-2.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674360173197)

**Step 3**

A copy document dialog box will appear. Specify the filename. If you are making a copy of a worksheet or file for a course, please be mindful of the naming convention specified.

![3-make-a-copy-3.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674380714381)

You may also specify which folder in your Google Drive the file will be copied. Click the drop-down and locate the folder to which you want the file to be copied.

![3a-make-a-copy-4.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674374021261)

**Step 4**

Click the **Make a copy** button to create the copy on the specified folder with the given filename.

![4-make-a-copy-5.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674367148557)

[<< Back to Google Docs, Sheets, and Slides](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17673627287437-Google-Docs-Sheets-and-Slides)

- [Google Docs](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01H5V4BD3W0FX00M76CRTV7ZCQ&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")

## Google prompts "You need access" – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17674597519501-Google-prompts-You-need-access

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17674597519501-Google-prompts-You-need-access#main-content)

![How-To](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674597513869)

**Step 1**

The files you refer to in your courses are uploaded to Google Drive and are shared within the domain of MMDC. This means that files are accessible only to those who are using their MMDC account.

You are getting this prompt because you are logged in to a non-MMDC account.

![1-you-need-access.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674582146445)

**Step 2**

You need to change the default logged in account first to your MMDC account.

To do so, just click the logged in account. Google will redirect you to the list of available accounts.

![2-you-need-access-2.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674559612685)

**Step 3**

Select your MMDC account to continue.

![3-you-need-access-3.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674597515277)

If your MMDC account is not in the list of available accounts, click **Use another account**to log in your MMDC account.

![3a-you-need-access-4.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674590153101)

**Step 4**

You should be able to access the file after switching to your MMDC account.

To avoid getting the prompt, it is advised to [use your MMDC account](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17498071646349-Using-the-correct-Google-account) as the default account for your Chrome browser.

![4-you-need-access-1.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674559614221)

[<< Back to Google Docs, Sheets, and Slides](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17673627287437-Google-Docs-Sheets-and-Slides)

- [Google Account](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01H5V4BVY73TA72TZZFC2JGW9C&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")

## Google Slides - Add comments – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17674644100621-Google-Slides-Add-comments

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17674644100621-Google-Slides-Add-comments#main-content)

![1-slides.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674644096013)

**Step 2**

Select the text you want to comment on.

![2-slides.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674672566669)

**Step 3**

Add comment by clicking the **Add** **comment** button.

![3-slides.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674649436813)

You may also add comment to the selected text by right-clicking and the selecting **Comment** or using the keyboard shortcut by pressing **Ctrl + Alt + M**.

![3a-slides.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674635597709)

**Step 4**

To tag other people in a comment, just key in the "@" sign followed by their email address. Once you have keyed in the "@" sign, people from your contacts or whom you have shared files with will be listed down for selection. Each person will get an email with your comment and a link to the file.

![4-slides.jpg](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17674628433293)

**Step 5**

## Tuition Fee Payment Channels – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17707754312845-Tuition-Fee-Payment-Channels

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17707754312845-Tuition-Fee-Payment-Channels#main-content)

_This article provides a complete list of the available payment channels students can use to pay their tuition fees. It includes details on each method and explains how to use them correctly._

Please follow the payment instructions in the following how-to guides when settling the payment for your tuition and miscellaneous fees. Please ensure to **submit a copy of your payment receipt or proof of payment** for documentation and tracking purposes, via this 📎 [GForm - https://forms.gle/m1zQzNUrLT7mGDWi6](https://forms.gle/m1zQzNUrLT7mGDWi6)

## How to Pay via RCBC Bills Payment – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17708113232653-How-to-Pay-via-RCBC-Bills-Payment

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17708113232653-How-to-Pay-via-RCBC-Bills-Payment#main-content)

_![How-To (1).png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17708105965581)_

_In this article, we'll walk you through on how to make tuition and fee payments using RCBC online banking services and over-the-counter bills payment. (See more_ [_Tuition Fee Payment channels_](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1Ggk58Zo6LO2diwQ9ToHfsFJtWdRxteT3/view?usp=sharing) _.)_

### Online Bills Payment

01. Go to [www.rcbconlinebanking.com](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/www.rcbconlinebanking.com) or use your RCBC Mobile App.
02. Type your ‘ **User** **ID**’ and ‘ **Password**’. Click Login and enter the **OTP**.
03. Go to **Pay** **Bills** Menu.
04. Under Payment Details:

    • Pay From\* Select **Source Account Number** dropdown

    • Pay To\* Select **List of Billers**

    • Select **Biller Category**, then select **Applicable Biller in the list**.
05. Input Biller’s required references from their payer

    (E.g. - Account Number, Name, etc.)

    **• Reference 1:**

    **• Reference 2:**

    **• Amount:**

    **• Remarks (if applicable)**
06. Click **Submit** button.
07. Click **Proceed** **To** **Payment.**
08. Input the **OTP**, then submit.
09. Finalize your payment and receive your payment confirmation.
10. [**Submit your proof of payment here.**](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSf5Zwr4wOy6Bmdng7RpmOl6-32hHgw6_-36i6TSpHnBglVKzA/viewform)

You can Save the Bills Payment Cyber Receipt by selecting the following options:

• Save Transactions as Template

• Save Receipt as Local file

• Save to Mail Box

[![Click here. (3 × 1 in) (1).png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/18281443887245)](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1pl74A-zAWhpEGD2v-jQasDYgFQZo80Bg/view?usp=drive_link)

### Over-the-Counter Bills Payment Service

Payments for tuition fees, back account, penalty, and other charges (document requests) are accepted via the RCBC over-the-counter Bills Payment Service. Fill out a **green Bills Payment/Collection Slip** with the following details:

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17708137777037)

Reminders:

- All payments will be electronically transmitted and uploaded to student’s account the next business day.
- Only CASH payments are accepted.
- A convenience fee of Php 15.00 per transaction is charged to the customer.

[![Click here. (3 × 1 in) (1).png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/18281443887245)](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1tYe0vU0ZXWOulsEJ-cXL6g2ckMxMtRR-/view?usp=drive_link)

## How to Pay via M Lhuillier Bills Payment – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17708170716685-How-to-Pay-via-M-Lhuillier-Bills-Payment

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17708170716685-How-to-Pay-via-M-Lhuillier-Bills-Payment#main-content)

![How-To (1).png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17708194620557)

_In this article, we'll walk you through on how to make tuition and fee payments using M Lhuillier Bills Payment service. (See more_ [_Tuition Fee Payment channels_](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1Ggk58Zo6LO2diwQ9ToHfsFJtWdRxteT3/view?usp=sharing) _.)_

1. Simply visit the branch nearest you and fill out the following in the Bills Payment Slip:

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17708177745037)

- Submit your [**proof of payment here.**](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSf5Zwr4wOy6Bmdng7RpmOl6-32hHgw6_-36i6TSpHnBglVKzA/viewform)

**Important** **Reminder**:

Please make sure to write only the correct biller’s name – **Mapua Malayan Digital College** – as MMDC’s bank account is separate and distinct from Mapua University and Malayan Colleges Laguna Inc.

## How to Pay via Gcash Bills Payment – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17708277617549-How-to-Pay-via-Gcash-Bills-Payment

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17708277617549-How-to-Pay-via-Gcash-Bills-Payment#main-content)

![How-To (1).png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/17708269257997)

_In this article, we'll walk you through on how to make tuition and fee payments using Gcash, a mobile payment platform. (See more_ [_Tuition Fee Payment channels_](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1Ggk58Zo6LO2diwQ9ToHfsFJtWdRxteT3/view?usp=sharing) _.)_

### [Gcash Bills Payment](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1KT1rdl7e5UFmBs0kjMrXIRdb7lo_kT9z/view?usp=drive_link)

1. From the main menu, click **Bills**.
2. In the **Bills** section, you'll find an option labeled " **schools**". Simply click on this option to proceed.
3. From the Schools list, click **Mapua Malayan Digital College**.
4. Enter your Student Application details and the amount in your **Generated Student Assessment**.
   - Your Student number can be found in your MMDC MyCamu Student Profile
5. Finalize your payment and receive your payment confirmation.
6. [**Submit your proof of payment here.**](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSf5Zwr4wOy6Bmdng7RpmOl6-32hHgw6_-36i6TSpHnBglVKzA/viewform)

[![Click here. (3 × 1 in) (1).png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/18281426224781)](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1KT1rdl7e5UFmBs0kjMrXIRdb7lo_kT9z/view?usp=drive_link)

[<< Back to Tuition Fee Payment Channels](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17707754312845-Tuition-Fee-Payment-Channels)

## Checking Course Section on Camu – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/18009313697933-Checking-Course-Section-on-Camu

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/18009313697933-Checking-Course-Section-on-Camu#main-content)

_If you want to know where you can check your section for a specific course, refer to the instructions below._

Kindly go to your Camu account ( [mycamu.com](http://mycamu.com/)). Upon logging in, click **My Learning** on the upper left side of your screen.

When you go to your Camu LMS (My Learning), click **My Schedules**.

On the upper left of your screen, you should be able to see the details about the course namely:

1. Current term (e.g. Term 1)
2. School Year (e.g. SY 2023-24)
3. Type of the course (e.g. General Education)
4. Section (e.g. S1102)

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/attachments/token/HbNVbS3dYdioXxl9dxvNKM1ew/?name=image.png)

If you still need help in checking, you may take a screenshot of this on your view and [submit a ticket](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/requests/new) so an IA can help you locate your section for a course.

## Payment Guide – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/18281475617549-Payment-Guide

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/18281475617549-Payment-Guide#main-content)

Throughout your journey as an MMDC student, you may encounter different types of fees and payments required for various aspects of your academic life. To help you navigate these financial obligations, here’s a breakdown of the three main types of billing you may need to settle:

### **1\. Tuition and Matriculation Fees**

These are the primary fees covering your enrollment, course access, and academic services at MMDC. Tuition fees are billed per term and must be settled before the start of classes or according to your preferred payment scheme.

For instructions on how to pay for tuition and matriculation fees, see the **🔗 [Tuition Fee Payment Channels Help Guide](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17707754312845).**

### **2\. Processing Fees for Requests**

Certain requests and administrative processes require a separate fee. These include, but are not limited to:

- **Document Requests** – Official transcripts, certificates, and other school documents
- **Course Load Revisions** – Adjustments to enrolled courses
- **Dropping of Courses** – Official withdrawal from one or more courses
- **Shifting to a Different Program** – Changing your degree program and specialization
- **Enrollment Cancellation**
- **Course Completion**

The corresponding processing fees for these requests are communicated during the request process and must be settled before they can be processed.

For instructions on how to pay for processing fees, see the **🔗 [How to Pay for Processing Fees for Requests and Services](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34560176570637)**

For a video walk through, please see this **🔗** [link](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1EmggDlJALBFMpCuFL2THYu3bIjctXmnJ/view?usp=drive_link).

### **3\. Computer-Lease-to-Own Program Payments**

For students from **SY 2022 and SY 2023 batches** who availed of MMDC’s Computer-Lease-to-Own program, payments for the leased devices must be made according to the agreed schedule and payment channel. Failure to settle these payments may impact account clearance and future transactions with MMDC.

## **For instructions on how to pay for processing fees, see the 🔗 **[How to pay for Laptops under the Computer Lease-to-Own Program SY22 and SY23](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34386842189197)****

## **Reminder:**

MMDC provides different payment options for each type of billing. Some payment channels may take time to process before they reflect in the system. Students are advised to review the payment instructions carefully and always **submit proof of payment** to ensure proper documentation and tracking.

- [Gcash](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01H5V0H15QNHE6FE0KCBYMKFEW&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")

- [M Lhuillier](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01H5V0HF267KVSX6NPHE1XEWVA&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")

## How to Submit a Support Ticket – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/18569673594253-How-to-Submit-a-Support-Ticket

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/18569673594253-How-to-Submit-a-Support-Ticket#main-content)

|     |
| --- |
| ## **Overview**<br>If you need help that cannot be resolved through the MMDC Learner Help Center, you can contact the Integrated Advising (IA) team by submitting a support ticket. This allows you to send your concern directly to the appropriate support team and receive updates on the status of your request. This guide explains how to submit a ticket through the Help Center. |

* * *

## **Table of Contents:**

1. [**When Should You Submit a Ticket?**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/18569673594253-How-to-Submit-a-Support-Ticket#h_01KMMPDVVN73SXJ9SJPZYEKVWV)
2. [**How to Submit a Support Ticket**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/18569673594253-How-to-Submit-a-Support-Ticket#h_01KMMPDVVVK45DV3608NVXWXD0)
3. [**What Happens After You Submit a Ticket?**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/18569673594253-How-to-Submit-a-Support-Ticket#h_01KMMPDVW4Q6MGZDPZM6Y16PBH)
4. [**Tips for Faster Support**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/18569673594253-How-to-Submit-a-Support-Ticket#h_01KMMPDVW6ZY3VZGYA9XXCNZ6C)
5. [**Related Articles**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/18569673594253-How-to-Submit-a-Support-Ticket#h_01KMMPDVWC0MHVR69NNWVGWFBY)

* * *

##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/18569673594253-How-to-Submit-a-Support-Ticket\#h_01KG4HGT9QG8Y4K21BRSX5W7K4)

# When Should You Submit a Ticket?

Most common questions about enrollment, payments, systems access, and academic policies already have step-by-step guides in the Help Center.

Before submitting a ticket, we recommend:

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/44604086576781)

- using the **Help Center search bar**
- browsing relevant Help Center categories
- reviewing related help articles

If you still cannot find the answer or need personalized assistance, you may submit a support ticket.

Submitting a ticket allows the Integrated Advising team to review your concern and provide direct assistance.

* * *

##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/18569673594253-How-to-Submit-a-Support-Ticket\#h_01KG4HGT9QG8Y4K21BRSX5W7K4)

# How to Submit a Support Ticket

Follow these steps to submit a request through the Help Center.

|     |
| --- |
| ### Step 1: Go to the MMDC Help Center<br>Open the MMDC Learner Help Center.<br>You may:<br>- browse categories<br>- use the search bar to find answers to your question<br>If you cannot find the information you need, proceed to the next step. |
| ### Step 2: Click “Submit a Request”<br>At the **top-right corner of the Help Center page**, click the **Submit a request** button. This will open the support request form.<br>![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/44604119546381) |
| ### Step 3: Select the Request Category<br>Choose the category that best matches your concern.<br>Examples may include:<br>- enrollment concerns<br>- billing or payment issues<br>- academic requests<br>- system access concerns<br>Selecting the correct category helps route your request to the appropriate team. |
| ### Step 4: Complete the Request Form<br>Fill in the required information, including:<br>- subject or request title<br>- description of your concern<br>- relevant details about the issue<br>- attachments such as screenshots (if applicable)<br>![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/44604119546637)<br>Providing clear and complete information helps the support team resolve your request more efficiently. |
| ### Step 5: Submit Your Request<br>![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/44604086578061)<br>After completing the form, click **Submit**.<br>Your request will be sent to the Integrated Advising team for review. |

* * *

##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/18569673594253-How-to-Submit-a-Support-Ticket\#h_01KG4HGT9QG8Y4K21BRSX5W7K4)

# What Happens After You Submit a Ticket?

Once your request is submitted:

- you will receive a **confirmation email**
- the request will be assigned to the appropriate support team
- you may receive follow-up questions if additional information is needed
- updates will be sent to your email as the request is processed

Please monitor your **MMDC learner email inbox** for responses and status updates.

* * *

##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/18569673594253-How-to-Submit-a-Support-Ticket\#h_01KG4HGT9QG8Y4K21BRSX5W7K4)

# Tips for Faster Support

To help the support team assist you more efficiently:

- describe your concern clearly
- include important details such as course, term, or system involved
- attach screenshots if you are experiencing a technical issue
- include links to related Help Center articles if applicable

Providing complete information helps reduce back-and-forth communication and speeds up resolution.

* * *

## Student Document Requests – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/19658103958413-Student-Document-Requests

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/19658103958413-Student-Document-Requests#main-content)

This guide outlines everything you need to know to successfully request official school documents.

- [**What are Student Document Requests**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/19658103958413-Student-Document-Requests#h_01JZM8SCY08MM31EFDVE35GR21) **:** Provides an overview of a Student Document Request and why it’s used.

- [**Document Requests Menu**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/19658103958413-Student-Document-Requests#h_01JZKTSR7AKRP35GSDBF9T7CNC) **:** View the available document types along with their corresponding processing fees and estimated turnaround times.

- [**Request Process**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/19658103958413-Student-Document-Requests#h_01JZM8N3D4GE7JRT3Y5D06CGY8) **:** Step-by-step instructions for submitting a student document request.


## **What are student document requests?**

**Student Document Requests**, also referred to as **Applications for Various Documents**, is a service provided to students who need official copies of their school records. This includes, but is not limited to, transcripts, certificates, enrollment certifications, and other academic or administrative documents.

## **Document Requests Menu**

_For the processing fees of document requests, please refer to the table below:_

|     |     |     |     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Document Name** | **Turnaround Time\*** | **Price** | **Description** | **Inclusions** | **Purpose** |
| Official Certificate of Matriculation | after 7 working days | Php 100 | An official document showing the student’s registration for a specific term | Name, student number, program, academic term, tuition and miscellaneous fee breakdown, schedule, section, list of enrolled courses | Required for visa, scholarship, or employment verification |
| Certificate of Assessment | after 7 working days | Php 100 | Statement of the student’s assessed fees per term | Breakdown of tuition, miscellaneous, and other school fees, total amount | Used for financial aid applications, reimbursement, and personal records |
| Certificate of Course Description | after 7 working days | Php 75 (first 3 pages)<br>+25 (for each succeeding page) | Lists the official course descriptions of courses in the student's enrolled program | Course codes, course titles, number of units for each course, and 1-paragraph course descriptions | Used for credit transfer, international applications, or employment |
| Certificate of Enrollment | after 7 working days | Php 100 | Certifies the current enrollment of a student in a particular term | Name, student number, program, academic year/term, enrollment status | For applications to scholarships, internships, or government programs |
| Certificate of Good Moral Character | after 7 working days | Php 100 | Affirms the student’s satisfactory conduct | Name, student number, good moral statement | For work requirements, licensure applications, school transfers, or further studies |
| Grade Certification | after 7 working days | Php 100 | Lists the grades obtained in courses during specific term(s) | Course titles, final grades, term/year taken | For employment, academic evaluation, or school transfers |
| GWA Certification | after 7 working days | Php 100 | Indicates a student’s General Weighted Average | GWA, academic term covered, course/program | For applications to scholarships, awards and honors, and graduate school or further studies. |
| Certificate of Grading System | after 7 working days | Php 100 | Indicates MMDC's official Grading System | Name, MMDC's Grading System (table), purpose | For applications to scholarships, credit evaluation to another school, or for further studies |
| Certified True Copy of Transcript of Records (CTC TOR) | after 7 working days | Php 100 | A verified copy of the official academic transcript | Complete academic record, “Certified True Copy” stamp | For personal reference, document authentication, or verification |
| TOR for Employment, Board/PRC, Evaluation, and further studies. | after 7 working days | Php 300 | Official academic record of all the grades in the courses taken | Course grades, program, grading system, remarks, registrar’s dry seal | Used for employment, licensure, academic review, or applications |
| Transfer Credentials Package:<br>Honorable Dismissal - Php 400<br>Transcript of Records - Php 440<br>Grade Certification - Php 100<br>Good Moral Certificate - Php 100 | at least 21 working days<br>_**(subject to student exit clearance)**_ | Php 1,040 | A set of documents consisting of all credentials required for school transfer | Honorable Dismissal, TOR, Grade Certification, Good Moral Certificate | Required for transferring to another school or institution |

_**\*Note: Processing of document requests will only commence once all valid documentary requirements are submitted, including the physical copies of your Admission documents.**_

## **Request Process**

To facilitate the process and provide you with the requested documents, please follow the

steps outlined below:

1\. Complete the **Request Form**: Please take a moment to fill out the form, indicating the specific documents you wish to request.

Download the form here to initiate your student document request: [**Document Request Form**](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1YCeFBFMnyY53K85baf2KBvrm57clzU0-/view)

Download this form if you wish to transfer out and would like to request your Transfer Credentials: [**Application for Transfer Credentials.**](https://drive.google.com/file/d/185yECWXKeJNJL3RkwzDfQERwkdUo92tC/view)

2\. Processing Fee: For each document request, there will be a corresponding processing

fee. Please refer to the [**table of fees.**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/19658103958413-Student-Document-Requests#h_01JZKTSR7AKRP35GSDBF9T7CNC) If you are requesting multiple documents, please

ensure you calculate the total fees accurately. Only indicate any of the following processing

codes when making a payment: 2020654321, 2020123456, and 2020765432. You can

also refer here: [**How to Pay for Processing Fees for Requests and Services.**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34560176570637-How-to-Pay-for-Other-Charges-and-Processing-Fees-for-Requests-and-Services)

3\. Submission: After completing the [**Application for Various Documents** **Form**](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1YCeFBFMnyY53K85baf2KBvrm57clzU0-/view) and completing the payment for the processing fees, please submit a document request Google form by clicking the button below, and upload the document request form and proof of payment.

**IMPORTANT: Please submit one Google Form for EACH document request.**

[![Screenshot 2025-07-08 1.30.51 PM.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/37898918507789)](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLScfLMkaUP6_i_1tFyivDsRL-2IcMLkd4iQefi9yohSCturF2w/viewform?usp=sharing&ouid=115558910485059255561)

- [Document Request](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01H8F75XJBGDJXT3RJ8SQTR702&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")

- [Document request form.pdf](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/article_attachments/37898823909773)

## GGives – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/25571916719885-GGives

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/25571916719885-GGives#main-content)

#### G na mag-enroll dahil sa GGives!

[![video-capture-7379.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/25571916717965)](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1B_-LRRVkWaF8NiM9u2rVulXpj3yrkvXL/view?usp=drive_link)

### GGives allows for a Study Now, Pay Later payment plan fitting for working students, so that you can budget your take-home pay while preparing for your dream career.

🔗  [Click for the promotional video of a flexible payment plan for a flexible online college like MMDC - Powered by GCash.](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1B_-LRRVkWaF8NiM9u2rVulXpj3yrkvXL/view?usp=drive_link)

GGives is the ultra-accessible installment loan service by GCash that can help you make lighter and more flexible payments.

**Step-by-Step Process:**

1\. Open the GCash app and tap on "Bills"

2\. Choose "Schools"

3\. Select "(MMDC) MAPUA MALAYAN DIGITAL COLLEGE"

4\. Enter the necessary details and the amount to pay.

5\. Select GGives as your payment method.

6\. Choose your preferred installment plan.

7\. View and agree to the disclosure statement.

**Requirements:**

**Note:** If you have multiple GCash accounts for different mobile numbers, only one of your mobile numbers can be eligible for GGives. Once your GGives is activated, you can only use GGives in the account connected with that mobile number.

To be eligible for GGives, you must meet the following criteria:

- 21-65 years old
- A Filipino citizen
- A Fully Verified GCash user
- Maintain a good credit record and did not commit any fraudulent transactions

**Resources:**

🔗  [https://new.gcash.com/services/ggives](https://new.gcash.com/services/ggives)

- [Tuition Payment](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01H65HRVJBW7N6VSDTPFA7R8X4&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")
- [flexible payment options](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01HTH2EE0J681SPQV21F42463X&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")

## Bukas.ph Loan – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/25572469881997-Bukas-ph-Loan

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/25572469881997-Bukas-ph-Loan#main-content)

### _Convert your tuition balance in up to 12 monthly installments when you apply for a Bukas tuition plan._

_![video-capture-374.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/25572474832013)_

🔗  [Click here for an introductory video about Bukas.ph' offerings.](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1jKKQVVOWWgrgk5WqQiTZ7ZbHxuFrQKuI/view?usp=sharing)

**Bukas** is an education financing platform that offers affordable tuition installment plans (student loans) to college and graduate school students.

Bukas is a partner of MMCL and MMDC with the endeavor to support students in achieving their academic goals by providing flexible and manageable financing solutions. Through this partnership, we aim to ensure that financial barriers do not hinder our students' educational aspirations, allowing them to pursue their studies with confidence and peace of mind.

**Step-by-Step Process:**

**1\. Create an account**

- To create a Bukas account, you'll need to enter your mobile number and password. Make sure your phone is with you to verify your mobile and complete the registration.

- Set up your student profile. You'll need to fill out your student profile before you can get started on your application. Make sure you reach profile level 3 to be eligible to apply for a tuition installment plan.


**2\. Submit an application**

- After you submit your application via the website or via the app, it will take Bukas 3 to 5 working days to process and provide feedback.

- Once you receive the installment offer, you and your co-borrower will need to confirm the agreement;
  - you, the borrower will need to confirm the agreement on your Bukas account,
  - while your co-borrower, will receive a signing link via SMS.
- Once you and your co-borrower completed the confirmation process, Bukas will disburse the full tuition amount directly to the student's school in 1 to 2 business days.
- In case your application needs revisions, kindly update your account and submit again to continue your application process.

**Requirements:**

1\. Valid IDs from Borrower & Co-Borrower

2\. Proof of Residence from Borrower & Co-Borrower

3\. School Assessment Form for student

- For MMDC, you may submit your Certificate of Matriculation (CM) or a screenshot of the Billing section in Camu)

4\. Proof of Income from Borrower and/ or Co-Borrower

**Note:**  Additional documents may be required by the Bukas assessment team.

**Resources:**

🔗 [https://bukas.ph/partners/mmdc/](https://bukas.ph/partners/mmdc/)

Related to

- [Tuition Payment](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01H65HRVJBW7N6VSDTPFA7R8X4&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")
- [flexible payment options](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01HTH2EE0J681SPQV21F42463X&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")

## Flexible Financing and Financial Aid Options – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/27934419530893-Flexible-Financing-and-Financial-Aid-Options

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/27934419530893-Flexible-Financing-and-Financial-Aid-Options#main-content)

Pursuing a college degree is a significant investment, and we understand that managing the costs and budgeting can be challenging. To support you, we’ve partnered with loan providers and have looked into a variety of financial aid options designed to make education more accessible and affordable.

This help guide provides an overview of the different types of flexible financing and financial aid available, including scholarships, loans, and work-study programs. By exploring these options, you can find the best financial support tailored to your needs, helping you focus on your academics without the added stress of financial constraints.

### [**🔗 Bukas.ph**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/25572469881997)

**Description:**

**Bukas** is an education financing platform that offers affordable tuition installment plans (student loans) to college and graduate school students.

Bukas is a partner of MMCL and MMDC with the endeavor to support students in achieving their academic goals by providing flexible and manageable financing solutions. Through this partnership, we aim to ensure that financial barriers do not hinder our students' educational aspirations, allowing them to pursue their studies with confidence and peace of mind.

**Step-by-Step Application Process:**

**1\. Create an account**

- To create a Bukas account, you'll need to enter your mobile number and password. Make sure your phone is with you to verify your mobile and complete the registration.

- Set up your student profile. You'll need to fill out your student profile before you can get started on your application. Make sure you reach profile level 3 to be eligible to apply for a tuition installment plan.


**2\. Submit an application**

- After you submit your application via the website or via the app, it will take Bukas 3 to 5 working days to process and provide feedback.

- Once you receive the installment offer, you and your co-borrower will need to confirm the agreement;
  - you, the borrower will need to confirm the agreement on your Bukas account,
  - while your co-borrower, will receive a signing link via SMS.
- Once you and your co-borrower completed the confirmation process, Bukas will disburse the full tuition amount directly to the student's school in 1 to 2 business days.
- In case your application needs revisions, kindly update your account and submit again to continue your application process.

**Requirements:**

1\. Valid IDs from Borrower & Co-Borrower

2\. Proof of Residence from Borrower & Co-Borrower

3\. School Assessment Form for student

- For MMDC, you may submit your Certificate of Matriculation (CM) or a screenshot of the Billing section in Camu)

4\. Proof of Income from Borrower and/ or Co-Borrower

**Note:**  Additional documents may be required by the Bukas assessment team.

**Resources:**

🔗  [https://bukas.ph/partners/mmdc/](https://bukas.ph/partners/mmdc/)

### **GCash - GGives Personal Loan**

**Description:**

GGives is the ultra-accessible installment loan service by GCash that can help you make lighter and more flexible payments.

**Step-by-Step Process:**

1\. Open the GCash app and tap on "Bills"

2\. Choose "Schools"

3\. Select "(MMDC) MAPUA MALAYAN DIGITAL COLLEGE"

4\. Enter the necessary details and the amount to pay.

5\. Select GGives as your payment method.

6\. Choose your preferred installment plan.

7\. View and agree to the disclosure statement.

**Requirements:**

**Note:** If you have multiple GCash accounts for different mobile numbers, only one of your mobile numbers can be eligible for GGives. Once your GGives is activated, you can only use GGives in the account connected with that mobile number.

To be eligible for GGives, you must meet the following criteria:

- 21-65 years old
- A Filipino citizen
- A Fully Verified GCash user
- Maintain a good credit record and did not commit any fraudulent transactions

**Resources:**

🔗  [https://new.gcash.com/services/ggives](https://new.gcash.com/services/ggives)

### **SSS Educational Assistance Loan Program**

**Description:**

The SSS Educational Assistance Loan Program (EALP) was implemented in 2012 to help member-borrowers and their covered beneficiaries defray their educational expenses for undergraduate/college degrees, as well as vocational or technical courses.

**Process:**

1\. Obtain the EALP Application Form. Visit the nearest SSS branch or download the form from the official SSS website.

2\. Fill out Part I of the form. After filling it out, send the form to the nearest MMDC Learning Hub so the Registrar's Office can sign Part III of the form. (Please note that before the Registrar’s Office signs the SSS EALP form, you need to request a Certificate of Matriculation. You must settle the initial tuition fee down payment before you can request for a Certificate of Matriculation. The Certificate of Matriculation is also one of the requirements for SSS EALP.)

3\. After the Registrar’s Office signs the SSS EALP form, we will send the form and the Certificate of Matriculation back to the learning hub. You can claim them once they arrive at the learning hub.

4\. Submit all required documents to SSS.

**Requirements:**

1\. **For first time borrowers:**

- Must be below 60 years old
- Actual monthly basic salary or income is Php 25,000 or below
- With at least 36 posted monthly contributions, six of which are posted within the last 12 months prior to the month of filing the EALP application
- Up-to-date in payment of all other member loan amortization

**For Existing EALP borrowers:**

- With six posted monthly contributions within the last 12 months prior to the month of filing the subsequent EALP application
- Up-to-date in payment of all other member loan amortization

2\. Accomplished EALP Application form

3\. Valid Identification Card/s or Document/s

4\. Current School's Assessment/Billing Statement (Certificate of Matriculation)

5\. Proof of Monthly Salary/Income of member-borrower

**Resources:**

How to Apply for an SSS Education Loan?

🔗  [https://www.facebook.com/jhovzvlog/videos/paano-mag-apply-ng-sss-educational-loan-2023-application-process/1747527485681177/](https://www.facebook.com/jhovzvlog/videos/paano-mag-apply-ng-sss-educational-loan-2023-application-process/1747527485681177/)

SSS EALP form

📎 [https://www.sss.gov.ph/sss/DownloadContent?fileName=mlp-01338.pdf](https://www.sss.gov.ph/sss/DownloadContent?fileName=mlp-01338.pdf)

## Reactivation of Student Accounts for Returning Students – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/27746288776205-Reactivation-of-Student-Accounts-for-Returning-Students

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/27746288776205-Reactivation-of-Student-Accounts-for-Returning-Students#main-content)

### **Welcome Back to MMDC, Returnees!**

## **Overview**

This article explains the return process after taking a break from enrollment. Follow these steps to reactivate your account, settle any balances, and enroll for the upcoming term smoothly.

* * *

## Who Is a Returnee?

A **returnee** is a former MMDC student who did not enroll for **one or more terms** but now wishes to resume studies and continue to complete their college journey with MMDC.

## Step-by-step Guide of the Return Process:

### Step 1: Signify Your Intent to Return

Start by filling out the **Intent to Return Form:**

- **No outstanding balance:** Use the [Intent to Return Form](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLScZMra6E4DXI9wuNIBAUHW4RmOz5jL5mh9g3viE9rSWe52Ang/viewform?usp=dialog) for students with no previous balances.

- **With Outstanding balance:** Use the [Intent to Return Form](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSccXFiUuGh7cnOYGor56DBKZvGaW8TCeVtgSpLYO1LzkXHjUQ/viewform) for students with previous balances and attach proof of payment so records can be updated.


Submitting this form allows the Enrollment Team to prepare your account for reactivation reactivation as an important preparation step for enrollment to the upcoming term.

### Step 2: Account Reactivation Process & Timeline

Once the form is submitted:

- Your **MMDC learner email** and **Camu account** will be reactivated if:
1. There is no outstanding balance from previous terms

2. The Intent to Return Form was submitted correctly
- **Timeline:** Reactivation is typically completed a few days before enrollment begins. Wait for confirmation from the Enrollment Team.


_If you have an outstanding balance, settle it first and_ [_**submit proof of payment**_](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSf5Zwr4wOy6Bmdng7RpmOl6-32hHgw6_-36i6TSpHnBglVKzA/viewform) [_**here**_](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSf5Zwr4wOy6Bmdng7RpmOl6-32hHgw6_-36i6TSpHnBglVKzA/viewform) _**.**_

### Step 3: Enroll for the Upcoming Term

After your account is active, access the **Camu Enrollment Module** during the official enrollment period.

📌 For step-by-step instructions, refer to the [**Enrollment Guide for Returning Students**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17533971814797-How-To-Enroll-A-Step-by-step-Guide) **.**

* * *

## **Frequently Asked Questions (FAQs)**

**1\. How do I check if I have an outstanding balance?**

Submit your inquiry [here](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/27746288776205-Reactivation-of-Student-Accounts-for-Returning-Students#), and your account will be checked.

**2\. When will my learner email and Camu be reactivated?**

Accounts are reactivated a few days before enrollment, provided the Intent to Return Form is completed and there’s no outstanding balance. If your MMDC learner email and CAMU access have not yet been activated within that timeframe, please email us at **iaservices@mmdc.mcl.edu.ph** so we can assist accordingly.

**3\. When can I request my Digital ID?**

Digital ID processing begins once the list of officially enrolled students is finalized. Kindly keep an eye on announcements for further updates.

**4\. I’m not sure if I can enroll this term. What should I do?**

File a **Leave of Absence (LOA)** to make future returns smoother.

📌 [Leave of Absence Help Guide](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/27746288776205-Reactivation-of-Student-Accounts-for-Returning-Students#)

**5\. Will files saved before account deactivation still be available?**

Yes. Files remain in your Google Drive, but only academic files should be stored. MMDC is not responsible for retrieving non-academic files.

**6\. Will my Camu progress be reset?**

No. Your progress will be retained unless enrolled courses are dropped.

**7\. I need more help. Who can I contact?**

Check the [**Help Center**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us) first. If you can’t find an answer, [**submit your inquiry/request**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/requests/new) to the **Integrated Advising Team**.

* * *

## Applying for a Leave of Absence (LOA) – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28025147595405-Applying-for-a-Leave-of-Absence-LOA

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28025147595405-Applying-for-a-Leave-of-Absence-LOA#main-content)

**Overview**

This article explains how to apply for a **Leave of Absence (LOA)** at Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC), including eligibility, required documents, and the step-by-step process. It also outlines the impact of an LOA on your enrollment, account status, and academic timeline. Use this guide to understand when and how to request a leave so you can pause your studies with confidence and clarity.

This help guide provides detailed information on how to apply for a leave of absence or LOA, including eligibility requirements, the application process, and important considerations.

Taking a leave of absence allows you to temporarily step away from your studies for various reasons, such as personal issues, professional challenges, health concerns, or other significant life events.

It is important to inform MMDC of your planned leave so MMDC can keep your academic records on hand, and your accounts secured in the database. This will also allow a quick and easy return process.

**Types of Leave of Absence**

- **Term Leave (Term LOA)**: A leave of absence lasting 1 term, which requires notifying MMDC.
- **Extended Leave (Extended LOA)**: A leave of absence of at least 2 terms, which requires submitting a formal application and a fee.

**Term LOA**

1\. Notify MMDC of your intention to take a short-term leave. This can typically be done by

- filling out this Gform: [Notification for Term LOA,](https://forms.gle/BNmBqANs6dtm15Nc6)
- OR, [submitting a request here.](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/requests/new)

**Extended LOA**

1\. Complete the [Application for Leave of Absence form](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1UIXDYHi9X9SvRkjE0HGzsH0OtzLTdmam/view?usp=sharing).

2\. Pay the processing fee of P50 via MMDC's payment channels.

3\. Submit the form and the proof of payment to the Integrated advising team, via email, or via a ticket.

## Annual Physical Exam (APE) for MMDC Students – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28216296339469-Annual-Physical-Exam-APE-for-MMDC-Students

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28216296339469-Annual-Physical-Exam-APE-for-MMDC-Students#main-content)

As part of MMDC’s student health services, we offer a free **Annual Physical Exam (APE)** through partner laboratories across the Philippines. While **optional**, we highly encourage you to take part in this benefit to stay on top of your health.

You may choose the partner laboratory that is most convenient for you. Access the link below for the list of partner laboratories available this July 2025.

🔗 [Directory of MMDC Partner Laboratories, as of July 1, 2025](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1AcuDtmRSBlqtDZiR4vN1Tf8rgGMhR4F_/edit?usp=sharing&ouid=117260214977294108184&rtpof=true&sd=true)

### **Why take the Annual Physical Exam?**

The Annual Physical Exam is designed to help you stay on top of your health by providing routine checks and identifying any potential health issues early. Regular health assessments are crucial for maintaining overall well-being and ensuring that any medical concerns are addressed promptly.

- **Early Detection**: Identifying health issues early allows for prompt treatment and better outcomes.
- **Preventive Care**: Routine exams can help prevent serious conditions by managing risk factors early.
- **Overall Well-being**: Maintaining good health supports your ability to focus on your studies and perform at your best.

### **🩺 What's Included in the APE?**

The APE includes the following routine checks:

- **Physical Exam**: A comprehensive assessment of your physical health by a medical professional.
- **Complete Blood Count (CBC)**: A blood test to evaluate your overall health and detect a variety of disorders.
- **Urinalysis**: A urine test to check for infections, kidney problems, and other health conditions.
- **Fecalysis**: (Optional) A stool test to screen for digestive disorders, infections, and other gastrointestinal issues.
- **X-ray**: Imaging to detect abnormalities in your chest, bones, or other areas as needed.
- **Drug Testing**: Optional and randomly tested

### **Partner Laboratories:**

You may visit any of MMDC's accredited partner laboratories and diagnostic centers. Check the full list of locations here:

🔗 [Directory of MMDC Partner Laboratories, as of July 1, 2025](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1AcuDtmRSBlqtDZiR4vN1Tf8rgGMhR4F_/edit?usp=sharing&ouid=117260214977294108184&rtpof=true&sd=true)

**Note:** Access the link using your MMDC-issued Google accounts.

### **APE Period for 2025**

**July 8-31, 2025**

You may visit any of our partner laboratories within this period.

**Note:** The APE Period is scheduled every term 3 of the SY.

### **How to Schedule Your APE**

Follow these simple steps:

**Step 1: Choose a Partner Laboratory**

- Select a laboratory from our list of partnered facilities closest to your location.

**Step 2: Schedule an Appointment**

- Contact the laboratory directly to schedule your exam. Be sure to mention that you are an enrolled student of MMDC.

**Step 3: Fill out and Have your Referral Form Signed**

- Download the 🔗 [Referral Form.](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1yEWE9lCYuXrOW9M3PqpOv1-0LGQ7rXd0/view?usp=drive_link)
- Fill out the referral form with your student information and check the services you would like done.
- Upload the fully-filled out Referral Form to via the 🔗 [GForm: MMDC Referral Form-Request for Authorization](https://forms.gle/AEokwbYGYDDxv1V86) to have it signed. Expect a 1-day turn-around time. If you sent the referral form today, you should be able to receive the signed form the next day.

**Step 4: Attend your APE at your chosen laboratories**

- Bring the signed referral form, and your student ID to your appointment. Follow any pre-exam instructions provided by the laboratory.
- Please be guided by the expected examination flow below:![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/28216614813453)

**Step 5: Receiving and Handling Your Results**

- **Pick Up Your Results**: You will be notified when your results are ready. Please pick them up directly from the laboratory or ccess them online.
- **Privacy**: Your results are confidential and will only be shared with you. It is your responsibility to maintain the privacy of your medical information.
- **Follow-Up**: Carefully review your results and follow through with any recommendations provided. If any issues are identified, seek further medical advice and treatment as necessary.

### **FAQ's:**

- **Is the APE mandatory?**   - No, the APE is optional but highly recommended.
- **Do I have to pay for the APE?**   - The cost is covered as part of the health services benefit for enrolled students.
- **What if there are no partner laboratories near me?**   - For now, we only have the listed laboratories available. We recommend making arrangements to visit one of these locations. There is continued efforts to expand the network of laboratories all over the Philippines in the coming years.

**Helpful Links:**

- **🔗 [Directory of MMDC Partner Laboratories, as of July 1, 2025](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1AcuDtmRSBlqtDZiR4vN1Tf8rgGMhR4F_/edit?usp=sharing&ouid=117260214977294108184&rtpof=true&sd=true)**
- **🔗 [Referral Form](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1yEWE9lCYuXrOW9M3PqpOv1-0LGQ7rXd0/view?usp=drive_link)**
- **🔗 [GForm: MMDC Referral Form-Request for Authorization](https://forms.gle/AEokwbYGYDDxv1V86)**

## How to Pay via Credit Card – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28696993735565-How-to-Pay-via-Credit-Card

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28696993735565-How-to-Pay-via-Credit-Card#main-content)

**How to Use the RCBC Pay Portal Facility for Credit Card Payments**

**![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/28696963624973)**

Step 1: Access the Payment Portal

- Click on this link: [MMDC Credit Card Payment.](https://enrollmate.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/credit-card-payment)

Step 2: Enter Your Details

- Provide your MMDC Email Address, Student Number, and Birth Date.
- Click on the "Proceed to Payment Portal" button.

Step 3: Select Your Bill

- Choose the bill you want to pay by clicking the corresponding check box.
- Check the “I agree to the Terms and Conditions” box.
- Click on the RCBC icon to proceed. This action will redirect you to the Xendit Payment Portal.

Step 4: Enter Payment Information

- Fill in the required payment details on the Xendit Payment Portal.
- Click the "Pay Now" button.

Step 5: Confirm Your Payment

- An OTP (One-Time Password) will be sent to your registered mobile number.
- Enter the OTP in the provided field and click "Submit."

Step 6: Payment Confirmation

- A thank you page will appear, confirming your successful transaction.
- After a few seconds, you will be redirected back to the MMDC payment confirmation page, where your reference number will be displayed.
- Take a screenshot of this confirmation page for your records.

Step 7: Submit Proof of Payment

- Submit the screenshot of the payment confirmation page as your proof of payment using this Google Form: [Google Form for Proof of Payment.](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSf5Zwr4wOy6Bmdng7RpmOl6-32hHgw6_-36i6TSpHnBglVKzA/viewform)

## MMDC's Tuition and Fees – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28700437224333-MMDC-s-Tuition-and-Fees

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28700437224333-MMDC-s-Tuition-and-Fees#main-content)

Understanding the tuition and fees at MMDC is crucial for managing your educational expenses and planning your budget effectively. This guide provides information about the costs associated with your studies, including your tuition, additional fees you might encounter, and available payment options.

### Tuition Fees

Your tuition fee at MMDC covers a comprehensive range of educational services, including access to online courses, digital learning materials, academic services, and the use of our virtual campus and learning environment. It ensures you have all the resources needed to succeed in your studies.

- Generally, for batch and school year 2024, the per unit cost is Php 1,335.
- For a 3-unit course, it's equivalent to Php 4,005.
- For those who have been granted the Pioneer Scholarship Discount, a 36% discount is applied, making it only Php 2,563 for a 3-unit course.
- Additionally, the Asenso Scholarship Discount, currently an active offering, offers a 20% discount, with an opportunity for an additional 16% discount for those who meet the eligibility criteria.
- There are also other variables that may affect ones tuition cost:
  - NSTP is computed on a standard rate, and not on a per unit rate.
  - There are some IT courses which require an additional Laboratory fee. See below: [Virtual IT Laboratory Fes.](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28700437224333-MMDC-s-Tuition-and-Fees#h_01J3P3ZTMEHJ8VFV06BFW4YT9A)
- The students payment scheme preference also affect the overall assessed fees, with installment schemes having a slight difference because of a small interest charge applied.
  - | Payment Scheme | Description | Additional Cost | Breakdown |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | **Full Payment** | Pay the entire amount upfront | None | 100% upon enrollment |
    | **Installment Option 1** | Three-installment plan | **+7.5% interest** | 20% – 40% – 40% |
    | **Installment Option 2** | Three-installment plan | **+5% interest** | 40% – 30% – 30% |

### Miscellaneous Fees

The miscellaneous fees refer to the various fees that apply in providing you with a comprehensive and effective digital college experience. This includes, but not limited to, registration fees, technology fees, and support services fees.

- Typically, the miscellaneous fees total Php 7,155 per term.
- For those who are enrolled to only 9 units and less, you get to enjoy a 40% discount, making it only Php 4,293 for the term.

* * *

### Virtual IT Laboratory Fees

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/28721761106317)

Beginning Year 3, all IT laboratory courses will be conducted using the Virtual IT Lab platform provided by CloudSwyft. This virtual laboratory is accessible from any device, requiring only a browser and an internet connection. But this virtual laboratory will provide a robust sandbox where the students get to experience, exercise, develop and build on technological skills required by each course, and ultimately be prepared for real-world and employment.

- Each laboratory course is Php 2,080 in addition. This fee is necessary to cover the cost of the resources and software.
- For instance, for term 1, you plan to enroll to 2 laboratory course - Scaling Networks and Web Systems and Technology - it will be Php 2,080 x 2 = Php 4,160 in addition to your tuition and miscellaneous fees for that term.
- This fee is not part of the tuition fee, but is a separate fee specific to the use of the virtual laboratories.

**Benefits of the Virtual IT Lab:**

1. **Hands-On Practice:** The Virtual IT Lab offers a comprehensive virtual classroom environment where you can practice and hone the skills required for your course. You will have access to a wide range of software and tools essential for your studies.
2. **Flexibility:** You can access the virtual lab from anywhere at any time, making it easier to fit your lab work into your busy schedule. This flexibility ensures that you can work at your own pace and revisit exercises as needed.
3. **Real-World Experience:** The virtual lab simulates real-world IT environments, providing you with practical experience that is crucial for your future career. You will be able to work on projects and tasks that mirror those found in professional settings.
4. **Collaborative Learning:** The platform supports collaborative learning, allowing you to work with classmates on projects and share insights and solutions.

* * *

### **Update for SY2024-2025:**

MMCL, and therefore MMDC being a college under Mapua Malayan Colleges Laguna, is implementing a 5% Tuition Fee increase. The Miscellaneous Fees, however, will remain the same.

This is after performing the necessary requirements and approval for the implementation of such an increase. The community consultation for the whole MMCL community took place on February 26, 2024. For MMDC specifically, we did an additional meeting on July 5, 2024. This consultation meeting were attended by representatives from all the MMCL and MMDC stakeholders. Among others, MMDC student representatives were in attendance - a student representative of the BSIT program, another student representative for the BSBA program, a scholar representative, a club leader representative, and an MMDC parent representative as well.

To get an estimate of your possible tuition and fees for the term, you may refer to the [Tuition Fee Calculator Help Guide.](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17463924733453-Tuition-Fee-Calculator)

## How to submit Proof of Payments (POP) – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28725739585421-How-to-submit-Proof-of-Payments-POP

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28725739585421-How-to-submit-Proof-of-Payments-POP#main-content)

Ensuring that your tuition and fees payments are properly recorded is crucial for maintaining accurate financial records and avoiding any disruptions to your enrollment status.

Submitting your proof of payment is the last and essential in the payment process. It provides official confirmation that your payment has been received and processed. In addition, it ensures your financial records are up-to-date and accurate, preventing any potential issues with your enrollment status. It also helps both you and MMDC keep clear and transparent records of all financial transactions.

As a proof of payment, you may submit a photo or screenshot of any of the following:

- bank transfer receipts
- online payment confirmations, or
- bank deposit slips

You may upload this as well your your student and payment information via the

- [MMDC - Proof of Payments for Tuition and Fees GForm](https://forms.gle/GikSGpsgvQkiifgM8).

## Enrollment Related FAQs – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28817649792525-Enrollment-Related-FAQs

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28817649792525-Enrollment-Related-FAQs#main-content)

## Course Load related

**What is the maximum load or maximum number of units I can enroll in this term?**

- The maximum load is as prescribed by the curriculum of the student based on the program and specialization enrolled in.

- Generally, the maximum number of units is 17 units per term.

- You may also refer to your [Curriculum Plan](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/categories/16972655156109-Academics) \- the total number indicated is the maximum allowed for your specific program for that specific term.![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/28847938043789)

## Billing and Payment related

**I've just recently paid and sent my proof of payment for my outstanding balance from the previous term, when will I be able to enroll?**

- Generally, allow a 24-hr turn-around time for the enrollment module from your Camu Student Portal to be enabled.
  - This takes into account the posting time it takes your payments from the different payment channels to be posted and reflected in the MMCL finance systems.
  - The payment channel with the fastest and next day posting time is GCash Bills Pay. For other payment channels, allow 24-48 hrs posting time.
  - For future enrollments, we recommend that balances be fully paid before the enrollment period to avoid any delays.

## Load Management Guidelines – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28849385472141-Load-Management-Guidelines

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28849385472141-Load-Management-Guidelines#main-content)

## **Overview**

This article explains how to manage your academic load effectively each term at Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC). It covers the maximum load, eligibility and procedures for requesting an overload, and key policies on pre-requisite and co-requisite courses. Use this guide to plan a balanced and successful academic schedule that fits your goals and commitments.

1. [Maximum Course Load](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28849385472141-Load-Management-Guidelines#h_01KC7J25QBPJRBFCVG3NKX763M)

2. [Overload](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28849385472141-Load-Management-Guidelines#h_01KC7J2D9QJZZSFY0CQ2TS1SK1)

3. [Pre-Requisite Course Regulation](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28849385472141-Load-Management-Guidelines#h_01KC7J2R8RPGHSMFGY3CX3JN8M)

4. [Co-Requisite Course Regulation](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28849385472141-Load-Management-Guidelines#h_01KC7J32PYZMM2SARFZG5EV9B6)


* * *

Effective load management is crucial for academic success, especially in an online learning environment like MMDC. Load management involves understanding the maximum number of courses you can take, the policies for requesting an overload, and the regulations surrounding prerequisite and co-requisite courses. This guide provides detailed information on these aspects to help you plan your academic journey effectively, ensuring you stay on track and achieve your educational goals within the timeline you've personally set without overwhelming yourself.

## Maximum Course Load

The maximum student load per regular term is generally eighteen (18) or as prescribed by the curriculum of the student based on the program and specialization.

Enrolling in 18 units a term renders the student a full-time status.

## Overload

An overload is defined as enrolling in more than the maximum course load per term, typically over 18 units. In some cases, this allows students to take additional courses beyond the standard load.

- **Eligibility Criteria:**  - **Academic Standing:** A strong academic record is required to request for a study overload.
  - **Completion Status:** A student requesting for study overload must be on their graduation year, or on their last 3 terms of study. It is strongly recommended however to maintain a low number of units to enroll in during the internship term which is the last term before graduation.
  - **By Approval:** Overload requests are for evaluation and approval by the Program Heads to ensure students can manage the additional courses without negatively impacting your academic performance.
- **Application Procedure:**  - **Application Period:** Request for study overload must be requested after the grade posting day of the preceding term and before the start of the enrollment period when the student plans to take a study overload.
  - **Formal Request:** Student submits a formal request addressed to their Program Head. This request should include your reasons for needing the additional units, such as the need to graduate on time, prerequisites for advanced courses, or other academic goals.
  - **Advisor Consultation:** An academic advising session will then be scheduled to discuss the feasibility and implications of taking an overload.
  - **Review and Approval:** Approval is based on your academic history, current performance, and justification for the overload.
- **Conditions and Restrictions:**  - **Limits on Overload:** Even if approved, there may be an upper limit on the number of additional units a student can take, to prevent overextension. This is based on the evaluation and approval of the Program Heads.

## Pre-Requisite Course Regulation

Pre-requisite courses are courses which must be taken, completed and passed during the term before advanced courses may be taken.

- **Purpose:**   - Prerequisites ensure that students have the necessary background knowledge and foundational skills to succeed in more advanced courses. They help maintain academic standards and improve the learning experience.
- **Policy:**  - A student must complete and pass a prerequisite course before enrolling in subsequent courses. The Camu enrollment system will block enrollment in courses for which prerequisites have not been met to ensure compliance.
  - Prerequisites are listed in the Curriculum Plan and Per Term Course Offerings to help students plan and make it easy to see which courses need to be taken before advancing.
  - As prescribed by the Commission on Higher Education, courses taken and completed without satisfying the prescribed pre-requisites shall not be given credit.
  - A student who receives a grade of INC (Incomplete) in a pre-requisite course shall not be allowed to take its advanced courses. The student must first complete/pass the pre requisite course before he is allowed to take any of its advance courses.
  - In certain cases, a student may request to take a prerequisite alongside the advanced courses by obtaining approval from the Program Heads. This is typically granted to graduating students and if you can demonstrate equivalent knowledge or experience.

## Co-Requisite Course Regulation

A co-requisite is a course which must be completed or enrolled concurrently with the course for which it is prescribed.

Similarly, Lec and Lab courses need to be taken concurrently per term.
