## Requesting for Enrollment Cancellation – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/29962498535181-Requesting-for-Enrollment-Cancellation

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/29962498535181-Requesting-for-Enrollment-Cancellation#main-content)

**Overview**

This article explains how to request **enrollment cancellation** at Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC), including eligibility, required steps, and important deadlines. It outlines the process you need to follow if you choose to cancel your enrollment and no longer wish to proceed with your college studies. Use this guide to understand what documents to submit, how to file your request, and what to expect after cancellation.

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/29962498529805)

**Enrollment Cancellation Request (ECR)**

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| **Description** | An Enrollment Cancellation Request is a formal procedure for students who have decided not to continue their enrollment with MMDC. It allows students to officially withdraw from their program and discontinue their enrollment with the institution. |
| **Applicable Period** | There are 2 types of ECR, depending on the time when it is submitted. <br>ECR with Refund are those submitted within the first weeks of the term. ECR without refund are those submitted after the ECR period with refund.<br>Please refer to the [Term Calendar](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/sections/28318507978637-MMDC-s-Calendar-of-Activities). |
| **Form** | [Enrollment Cancellation Request Form](https://drive.google.com/file/d/14bMPN-zxJ9wE8lOUGhOOfpo7I0jNJn3h/view?usp=sharing)<br>_Please download a copy of the form._ |
| **Requirements** | 1. Enrollment Cancellation Form<br>   <br>2. Proof of Payment (50 pesos)<br>   <br>3. Letter of Intent to Cancel Enrollment<br>   <br>4. Student’s valid ID<br>   <br>5. Parent/ Guardian Valid ID |
| **Terms and Conditions/ General Guidelines** | 1. Students submitting this request should have completed their submission of physical admission docs. They need to be marked as first officially enrolled with MMDC-MMCL.<br>2. Students who filed ECR should have NO TUITION BALANCE.<br>3. All requirements must be submitted during or within the ECR period indicated in the term calendar. |

|     |
| --- |
| **Step-by-step Guide:** |
| **Step 1:**<br>**Fill out the Enrollment Cancellation Request Form accurately and completely.**<br>1. Completely fill out and sign the form.<br>**Sample:**<br>![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXe-8Kcet941D_6vkgSdgl5GhVRQJKf8HVKII2a_JSURWmvnZV9yrqVLUHoZIshX-KirNIdrBfs60hg2acFmIM76QrxCdDyucwRRrPt3s-0fghDubJGjSAHTNBJXth62h7YSghOHbT4YMy1bV44DbnHPI-jCyRTMDFYxsOg0?key=3g2vrMa8jVl3HxzF1iWQCg) |
| **Step 2:**<br>**Submit a letter indicating the reasons for the cancellation request.**<br>1. Write a letter indicating your reasons for cancellation. <br>2. Include in the letter if you are of legal age and funding your own college education. <br>3. If you are not of legal age or if being supported by parents or guardians, please request the endorsement of your parent or guardian funding your college education. Request for them to sign the letter as well. <br>4. You may also attach **supporting documents** such as work schedule, medical certificates, if any.<br>**Note:** If for Refund, please indicate your complete bank details in the letter as well.<br>**Sample:**<br>**![](https://lh7-rt.googleusercontent.com/docsz/AD_4nXe4i6gOANPWpH0CdXgpIBTA31c_mdgYc27PSYORf57RJOla4Jb4U0hX06KVNr1CTw7s-PRsJQMqdZvMb8rB0EKbaqFjk7oZ-aGMhrYj6vZCvULDe9I3RATg38nW54-Om0zyv0CK3zrVx5QLocTqOkzbsnqVtSnrwF0bwnT9Tg?key=3g2vrMa8jVl3HxzF1iWQCg)**<br>**Step 3:**<br>**Submit a Proof of payment for the processing fee amounting to 50 pesos per request.**<br>1. When paying for services such as this, DO NOT USE YOUR OWN STUDENT NUMBER. <br>2. Please use **2020654321** or **2020123456** as the assigned processing code. Please see payment instructions here.<br>[**![Click here. (3 × 1 in) (1).png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/34939464264333)**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34560176570637-How-to-Pay-for-Processing-Fees-for-Requests-and-Services) |
| **Step 4:**<br>**Submit a copy of your valid ID.**<br>The following are the recognized valid ID's:<br>- e-Card / UMID<br>  <br>- Employee’s ID / Office Id<br>  <br>- Driver’s License\*<br>  <br>- Professional Regulation Commission (PRC) ID \*<br>  <br>- Passport \*<br>  <br>- Senior Citizen ID<br>  <br>- SSS ID<br>  <br>- COMELEC / Voter’s ID / COMELEC Registration Form<br>  <br>- Philippine Identification (PhilID / ePhilID)<br>  <br>- NBI Clearance \*<br>  <br>- BIR (TIN)<br>  <br>- Pag-ibig ID<br>  <br>- Person’s With Disability (PWD) ID<br>  <br>- Philippine Postal ID <br>  <br>- Phil-health ID<br>  <br>- School ID <br>  <br>**Step 5:**<br>**Submit a copy of parent or guardian's valid ID.**<br>For students who are supported by parents or guardians, please submit a copy of their valid ID as well. The signature should be visible, so this may be verified with the letter of cancellation. <br>**Step 6:**<br>**Submit your ECR via the GForm.**<br>1. Access the link to the [Enrollment Cancellation Request GForm](https://forms.gle/W8gTMvzrJrpHW7b3A) and upload all the requirements.<br>2. Requests submitted after the ECR period indicated in the term calendar will no longer be processed. |

## Feedback and Suggestions – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/29965563553293-Feedback-and-Suggestions

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/29965563553293-Feedback-and-Suggestions#main-content)

**We Value Your Feedback!**

At MMDC, we are constantly striving to improve your learning experience and ensure that your journey is both enjoyable and effective. To achieve this, we want to hear from YOU!

We’ve made it easier for you to share your thoughts and suggestions through our [**Feedback and Suggestions Form**.](https://forms.gle/6X6FaZTgkykugq9z8)

This form allows you to:

- Share your insights on what’s working well and what could be improved. We are open to hearing both the positives and negatives.
- Offer suggestions for campus initiatives, online tools, or course materials.
- Provide feedback on your overall MMDC experience.

We understand that some feedback may be sensitive or personal, so we’ve designed the form to offer you the option to submit your feedback **anonymously**. This ensures your comfort in sharing your thoughts freely, without any concerns.

### How to Submit Your Feedback:

1. **Access the Form**: Click on [this link](https://forms.gle/6X6FaZTgkykugq9z8) to open the **MMDC Feedback and Suggestions Form**.
2. **Fill out the Form**: Enter your feedback or suggestions in the provided fields.
3. **Choose Your Privacy Preference**: If you'd like to remain anonymous, simply check the box to submit your response without sharing your name or contact details.
4. **Submit**: Hit the submit button, and your voice will be heard!

Your input is invaluable in helping us shape a better MMDC. Thank you for taking the time to share your thoughts!

## Shifting to a New Program of Study – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/29966106112269-Shifting-to-a-New-Program-of-Study

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/29966106112269-Shifting-to-a-New-Program-of-Study#main-content)

**Overview**

This article explains the process for shifting to a different program of study at Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC). It outlines the requirements, steps, and criteria you need to follow to request a program shift. Use this guide to understand what is involved, how shifts are evaluated, and how the change may affect your academic progress.

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/29966106110221)

* * *

**Description**

Shifting is the voluntary transfer from one program or specialization to another. Shifting to another program shall take effect on the succeeding term after the request to shift has been approved.

**Application Period**

Shifting requests are processed after the enrollment period until the deadline indicated in the term calendar.

Please refer to the [Term Calendar](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/sections/28318507978637-MMDC-s-Calendar-of-Activities).

**Form**

[Application to Shift to a New Program of Study Form](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1KP2pPrjbWMJwWGJWHzG--mHjnHyv8rwS/view?usp=sharing)

_Please download a copy of the form, and fill out completely and accurately._

**Requirements**

1. [Application to Shift to a New Program of Study Form](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1KP2pPrjbWMJwWGJWHzG--mHjnHyv8rwS/view?usp=sharing)
1. Please see sample below for guidance on how to fill out the Shifting form:
      ![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/41965901319181)
2. [Credit Evaluation Form for Shifters](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1YBXXjTRxM_1Caka_TvZCOeDjJfgMLD1xwEDLuFCyz0Q/copy)
1. Please see sample below for guidance on how to fill out the Credit Evaluation Form for Shifters:![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/41965904825869)
3. Proof of Payment (50 pesos)

4. Letter of Intent to shift to a new program


**Additional Requirements:**

Career Counseling with the Guidance Office

Academic Advising and Credit Evaluation with Program Heads

**Terms and Conditions/ General Guidelines**

1. Once the request has been approved, the shift to the new program will take effect on the succeeding term.
2. The Grades on courses under the new program, and the courses credited to the new program taken in MMDC, shall be included in the computation of the General Weighted Average (GWA).

**Step-by-step Guide:**

**Step 1:**

**Fill out the** [**Application to Shift to a New Program of Study Form**](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1KP2pPrjbWMJwWGJWHzG--mHjnHyv8rwS/view?usp=sharing) **accurately and completely.**

1. Download the form.
2. Fill out completely and accurately.
3. Attach your signature.

**Step 2:**

**Submit a letter addressed to the Program Heads indicating the reasons for the shifting request.**

**Sample:**

**![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/30943582207757)**

**Step 3:**

**Submit a Proof of payment for the processing fee amounting to 50 pesos per request.**

1. When paying for services such as this, **DO NOT USE YOUR OWN STUDENT NUMBER.**
2. Please use **2020654321** or **2020123456** as the assigned Shifting processing reference code. Please see payment instructions below **>>>**

[![Click here. (3 × 1 in) (1).png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/34941004388365)](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34560176570637-How-to-Pay-for-Processing-Fees-for-Requests-and-Services)

**Step 4:**

**Fill out the** [**Credit Evaluation For Shifters**](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1YBXXjTRxM_1Caka_TvZCOeDjJfgMLD1xwEDLuFCyz0Q/copy) **.**

1. Download the [Credit Evaluation for Shifters](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1YBXXjTRxM_1Caka_TvZCOeDjJfgMLD1xwEDLuFCyz0Q/copy) form.
2. Fill out completely and accurately.
   - Refer to the curriculum of the Program/Specialization you are planning to shift to.
     - [IT Curriculum Plans](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17705503954445)
     - [BA Curriculum Plans](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/24877691535117)
   - Identify which of the courses listed in the curriculum plan have already been completed and have been taken in MMDC with a passing grade.
3. Attach your signature.
4. Bring this with you and present it to the Program Head during your academic advising.

**Step 5:**

**Submit your Shifting request via the GForm.**

1. Access the link to the [Shifting Request GForm](https://forms.gle/FmCKjX3xFgT8qnSS6) and upload all the requirements.

**Step 6:**

**Schedule and attend interviews with the Program Head for Academic Advising and the Center for Guidance and Counselling for Career Advising**

1. After the request and requirements are received via the Gform, await and schedule your advising meetings with the Program Head and Guidance office. An Integrated Advisor will get in touch with you to coordinate regarding the scheduling of the meetings.

| **GForm to submit a Shifting request** | [Shifting Request GForm](https://forms.gle/FmCKjX3xFgT8qnSS6) |

## Online Etiquette for a Connected Online MMDC Campus – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/31675288917389-Online-Etiquette-for-a-Connected-Online-MMDC-Campus

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/31675288917389-Online-Etiquette-for-a-Connected-Online-MMDC-Campus#main-content)

In today’s digital world, how you present yourself online matters just as much as in person. This is your guide to navigating MMDC's online environment with professionalism and respect. We’ll cover the essentials of digital communication, including email and chat etiquette, online conduct, decorum, and virtual classroom behavior. This will ensure you make the most of your online interactions, fostering a positive and respectful MMDC campus community.

Pls access this [link](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1LpoHl3oVM-40y8wiYSZfJ9Ic9AaSvaJR/view?usp=sharing) for the full guide.

## Document Requirements for Admission of New Transfer Students – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/31678357089293-Document-Requirements-for-Admission-of-New-Transfer-Students

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/31678357089293-Document-Requirements-for-Admission-of-New-Transfer-Students#main-content)

## **Overview**

This article lists the documents required for **transfer student or transferee admission** to Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC), a college under Mapúa Malayan Colleges Laguna (MMCL).

During your admission process, you may have already **uploaded digital copies** of your documents. However, **submitting the original physical copies** of these requirements is a **separate and essential step** to complete your official enrollment.

You will only be considered **officially enrolled** once MMDC has received and verified your complete physical documents. Students with pending requirements are considered **conditionally enrolled** until all credentials are submitted.

* * *

**📌 Note:**

A **transfer student** refers to someone who has **previously enrolled in a college or university** and is now applying to continue their studies at MMDC.

* * *

## **Document Requirements**

Prepare the following major documents for freshman admission:

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/31678357085325)

**🔗** Please access this link for the full guide and the rest of the minor requirements.

[![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/31678357086093)](https://docs.google.com/presentation/d/1KjmoFWe0aL6Oqg6siozEhSTbXtrogTrFzdXpGMYvUd8/edit?usp=sharing)

* * *

**📌 Note:**

All official documents—such as transcript of record, transfer credentials, or certifications—must be **addressed to** _**Mapúa Malayan Colleges Laguna (MMCL)**_ as the recognized legal and institutional name. **Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC)** operates as a college under **MMCL**, and therefore, all official documents should be addressed to MMCL.

* * *

## **Why do I need to submit my physical admission documents?**

Submitting your **physical admission documents** is required for MMDC to officially confirm your enrollment. Failure to submit your credentials may lead to the following:

- Delay in course crediting and evaluation
- You **cannot be officially promoted** to the next level.
- You **cannot officially graduate** from the program.
- You **cannot be recognized for honors or awards**, even if qualified.
- You **cannot enroll in succeeding academic terms** without being cleared.
- You **will not be released any official records** (e.g., transcript, certifications, or permanent record).
- Your **enrollment may be cancelled** if documentary requirements remain incomplete beyond the deadline.

If your documents are still being processed by your previous school, coordinate immediately with your former registrar to ensure timely transmittal to MMDC/MMCL.

* * *

**📌 Note:**

These terms are detailed in the **Affidavit of Undertaking** you signed during admission. By signing the affidavit, you acknowledged your temporary or conditional enrollment status and agreed to submit all required credentials within the given timeline to maintain your official standing at MMDC.

* * *

## **Notes & Reminders**

- Digital submission during the application process **does not replace** the need for original physical copies.
- Submit all requirements on or before the set deadline to avoid interruption of enrollment or access to student services.


* * *

## Sign In to Your Google Account to Access Help Center Links – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/32088818236685-Sign-In-to-Your-Google-Account-to-Access-Help-Center-Links

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/32088818236685-Sign-In-to-Your-Google-Account-to-Access-Help-Center-Links#main-content)

## **Overview**

This article explains how to access Help Center documents using your MMDC learner Google account and what to do if you see an access error.

* * *

Some Help Center links lead to documents that are shared **only within the MMDC Google environment**. To open these files successfully, you must be signed in using your **MMDC-issued Google account**.

* * *

## **Step 1: Make Sure You’re Signed In to Your MMDC Google Account**

To access shared documents, you must be logged in to your MMDC learner email (example: lr.jdelacruz@mmdc.mcl.edu.ph).

### **How to Sign In**

1. Open your browser and go to [**www.google.com**](http://www.google.com/).
2. Click **Sign in**. ![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/32088818229645)

3. Enter your MMDC learner email and password. ![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/32088812959885)
4. Once signed in, your MMDC account will be active and ready to access shared files.


**Tip:**

You can confirm you’re logged in by checking the profile photo in the upper-right corner of your browser. Make sure it’s your **MMDC learner account**, not a personal Gmail account.

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/34450683435021)

* * *

## **Why This Matters**

Help Center documents are restricted to MMDC accounts for **privacy and security**.

If you’re signed in using a personal Google account, you may see an **“Access Denied”** message. This usually means the document is working correctly—you just need to switch to your MMDC account.

* * *

## **Step 2: Open the Shared Link**

Once you’re signed in to your MMDC account:

1. Click the link provided in the Help Center article.
2. The document should open automatically if permissions are set correctly.
3. Google Docs, Sheets, or Slides will open in the appropriate Google app. ![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/32088818232845)

If the file still doesn’t open, continue to the next step.

* * *

## **Step 3: Use Your MMDC Email When Requesting Access**

If you need to request access to a document:

- Make sure the request is sent **from your MMDC learner email**.
- Requests sent from personal Gmail accounts cannot be granted access.


**Reminder:**

Always use your school-issued email when interacting with MMDC documents and systems.

* * *

## **Helpful Tips to Avoid Access Issues**

- Check that you’re logged in to your MMDC account before opening links.
- Consider creating a **separate browser profile** for school use to avoid account mix-ups.
- Keep personal and school accounts signed in under different browser profiles.

* * *

## **Optional: Create a Separate Browser Profile (Recommended)**

Creating a dedicated browser profile for school helps prevent access errors.

### **Example: Google Chrome**

1. Open Chrome.
2. Click your profile icon.
3. Select **Add** to create a new profile. ![ClickProfile.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/32088812963085)
4. Name it something like **“MMDC School”**.
5. Sign in using your MMDC learner email. ![NewProfile_SignIn.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/32088812964877)

After setting this up, use this profile when accessing Camu and Help Center links.

* * *

## **Need More Help?**

If you’re still unable to access a document after following these steps, [submit a request](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/requests/new) through the [**Help Center**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us) so the appropriate team can assist you.

## Course Completion for INC Grades – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/32265959292557-Course-Completion-for-INC-Grades

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/32265959292557-Course-Completion-for-INC-Grades#main-content)

## **Overview**

This article explains how to complete a course in which you received an **INC (Incomplete)** grade at Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC). It outlines the steps you need to take, the forms you must submit, and the deadlines for resolving incompletes so your grade can be finalized. Use this guide to make sure your incomplete courses are properly completed before they lapse into a failing grade.

* * *

## Students with INC or C

_Students who receive an **INC (Incomplete)** grade in any course must complete the necessary requirements and process to finalize their grade during the **succeeding term**._ _Failure to resolve an INC grade within the succeeding term will result in an automatic conversion to an **F** or a grade of **5.00**__. However, if the requirements are completed, the grade will be finalized as **3.00**._ _Please refer to the instructions and requirements outlined below to complete this process._

_Students who receive a **C (Continuing)** grade in any of the **Integrative Courses (Thesis/ Feasibility, Capstone)** or **Internship** must complete the necessary requirements and process to **finalize their grade within the next 1 or 2 terms depending on the program**._ _Failure to complete a C grade within one year will result in an automatic conversion to a grade of **F** or a grade of **5.00**__.__Please refer to the instructions and requirements outlined below to complete this process:_

* * *

## Requirements

- [Request to Complete Course (RTC) Form](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/34710868756621)
- Proof of Payment (50 pesos)

* * *

## Step-by-step Guide to Complete

**Step 1: Submit Required Documents**

- Fill out the completion form accurately with your **Student Information**, **Course Code** and **Section**.
- If you have both a lecture and laboratory course (e.g., **MO-IT101 and MO-IT101L**), complete a separate form for each course.

**Step 2: Pay the Processing Fee**

- Pay **50 pesos per course** (total **100 pesos** if completing both lecture and laboratory).
- Follow the payment guidelines using any of the **processing codes** for processing fees. _(Do not use your student number, as this will misdirect the payment as tuition fees instead.)_
- Learn more here: [How to Pay for Processing Fees for Requests and Services](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34560176570637-How-to-Pay-for-Processing-Fees-for-Requests-and-Services)

**Step 3: Consult with Your Mentor or Program Head**

- Communicate with your mentor your intention to complete the course. Identify what coursework you still need to submit to be able to complete the course.
- Be informed about the process of submission, consult with your mentor the deadline for submission, as well as the process for submission of your coursework.
- With the information you gathered from your consultation with your mentor, fill out the Course and Submission information of the RTC form.
- If your mentor isn’t available, you may reach out to the Program Heads, **Ms. Joedy Cruel** (GE and BA) or **Mr. Noel Torregoza** (IT) for assistance.

**Step 4: Request for Your Mentor’s Signature on the Form**

- After you’ve completely filled out the form, submit the RTC form to your mentor for validation and signature.
- If your mentor isn’t available, you may reach out to the Program Heads, **Ms. Joedy Cruel** (GE and BA) or **Mr. Noel Torregoza** (IT) for assistance.

**Step 5: Submit your Request to Complete**

- Submit your completed form, documents, and payment proof as soon as possible or before the deadline for Course Completion, as indicated in the term calendar.
- Click the button below to submit your documents to the Google Form.

[![Submit a request to complete course.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/39178302940557)](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSd--_ln9-GSiU_PqJRZe8SGUVRWOGFckcRssC1p5obTZJgqyw/viewform)

### Submission of Coursework Requirements for the Completion of INC Grades

Stay in regular communication with your mentor or program head throughout the process:

1. **Account Reactivation**: Your Google and Camu accounts will be reactivated once you submit the complete "Request to Complete Requirements."

2. **Submit Coursework**: Upload your completed coursework to MyCamu and notify your mentor and/or Program Head once submitted.

3. **Grade Outcome**: Upon successfully completing the coursework requirements, you will receive a grade of 3.00. Please be aware that if you fail to complete the coursework, even after submitting the "Request to Complete Requirements," your grade will automatically convert to 5.00.


* * *

## How to Request for Study Overload – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/32574438451853-How-to-Request-for-Study-Overload

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/32574438451853-How-to-Request-for-Study-Overload#main-content)

**Overview**

This article explains how to request a **Study Overload** at Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC), including eligibility criteria, application steps, and required documentation. It outlines the process for enrolling in additional units beyond the standard course load so you can stay on track with your academic goals when needed. Use this guide to understand when and how to apply for an overload and what to prepare for a successful request.

**Overload**

An overload is defined as enrolling in more than the maximum course load prescribed per term, typically over 17 or 18 units as indicated in the Curriculum Plan. An approved Study Overload allows students to take additional courses beyond the standard load.

- **Eligibility Criteria:**
  - **Academic Standing:** A strong academic record is required to request for a study overload.

- **Completion Status:** A student requesting for study overload must be on their graduation year, or on their last 3 terms of study. It is strongly recommended however to maintain a low number of units to enroll in during the internship term which is the last term before graduation.

- **By Approval by the Program Heads:** Overload requests are for evaluation and approval by the Program Heads to ensure students can manage the additional courses without negatively impacting their academic performance.

- **Application Procedure:**
  - **Application Period:** Request for study overload must be requested after the grade posting day of the preceding term and before the start of the enrollment period when the student plans to take a study overload.

- **Formal Request:** Student submits a formal request, via email, addressed to their Program Head. This request should include the reasons for needing to enroll in the additional units, such as the need to graduate on time, needing to accomplish the prerequisites for advanced courses, or other academic goals.

- **Advisor Consultation:** An academic advising session may be scheduled, if deemed necessary by the Program Heads, to discuss the feasibility and implications of taking an overload. The student need to be able to present a Plan of Study which lists the courses he/she is planning to take in the current and succeeding terms until graduation.
- **Review and Approval:** The Program Heads evaluates and grants approval based on the student's academic history, performance, and justification for the overload.

- **Conditions and Restrictions:**
  - **Limits on Overload:** Even if approved, there may be an upper limit on the number of additional units a student can take, to prevent overextension. This is based on the evaluation and approval of the Program Heads.

- **Requirements:**
  - The following are the requirements for the Request to Study Overload to be processed. These need to be completely filled out and signed by the Program Head to indicate their approval.
    1. **Letter from the Student with attached Plan of Study**\- sent to the Program Heads via email _(cc: academics@mmdc.mcl.edu.ph)_

           Please use the templates below:
       - [Letter of Request](https://drive.google.com/file/d/17ms9nCNj-oFFNlQZx5xQBX9JZbZPao8H/view) Template - Fill out and sign this Letter of Request
       - [Plan of Study](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1DwH522ss5a8p2zk9jbfhDeRY_TYE4ZIw/edit?gid=1383318924#gid=1383318924) Template - Click "File" > Make a Copy > Fill out the Plan of Study > Save as PDF
    2. [**Request to Study Overload Form**](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1uHz82x_jzkefn4KbX7i-iYAe0qKgMuQ_/view?usp=drive_link) \- also sent to the Program Heads via email _(cc: academics@mmdc.mcl.edu.ph)_
- **Steps:**
1. Student submits the request, including the letter and form, to the Program Heads (and cc: academics@mmdc.mcl.edu.ph) and seeks their approval.
2. The student complies with the additional requirements of the Program Heads when necessary.
3. Upon receiving the approval and signed forms of the Program Head, the student submits the request to the Enrollment Officer via the [Gform](https://forms.gle/3DtSFHPSQX3w45GR9).
     1. Link to the Gform: [https://forms.gle/3DtSFHPSQX3w45GR9](https://forms.gle/3DtSFHPSQX3w45GR9)
4. The Enrollment Officer processes the overload requests.
5. The student waits for confirmation of the request from the Enrollment Officer.
6. The student completes the next steps for enrollment.

* * *

## Academic Integrity – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/32744004272781-Academic-Integrity

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/32744004272781-Academic-Integrity#main-content)

## **Overview**

Academic integrity is a core value at MMDC. It guides how we learn, create, and collaborate in an online community built on trust and fairness. Upholding academic integrity means completing your work honestly, acknowledging sources properly, and following all guidelines set by the institution.

This article outlines MMDC’s official policies on academic integrity. It explains the standards expected of every student, lists actions considered violations, and details the corresponding procedures and consequences. It also provides practical reminders to help you protect your work, manage your responsibilities, and contribute to a learning environment where everyone’s efforts are respected.

Use this guide to understand your responsibilities and the rules that support a fair and credible academic experience for all MMDC learners.

* * *

## Policies on Academic Integrity

At MMDC, we uphold academic integrity as a cornerstone of our educational philosophy. Academic integrity refers to the **commitment to honesty, fairness, and responsibility in all academic pursuits**. It means submitting original work, respecting intellectual property, and adhering to ethical standards in learning, teaching, and research.

Maintaining academic integrity is essential because it fosters trust and mutual respect within the academic community. It ensures that your achievements genuinely reflect your abilities and efforts, builds your professional reputation, and prepares you to meet the ethical expectations of the workplace. Upholding these values also preserves the credibility of MMDC’s programs and the degrees we confer.

By embracing academic integrity, you contribute to an environment where knowledge thrives, and excellence is recognized. In this guide, we’ll explore the key principles of academic integrity, common violations to avoid, and tips for cultivating ethical habits in your studies.

Violations to Academic Integrity

- Plagiarism (presenting someone else’s work or ideas as your own).
- Significant failure to appropriately and accurately acknowledge the work of others.
- Failure to appropriately and accurately acknowledge one’s own work where original work has been reused from previous assessment tasks (also known as self-plagiarism).
- Washing’, or the use of software services to disguise plagiarism.
- Submitting the work of another person or from an online study platform as one’s own, or undertaking an assessment task for another person (contract cheating or ghostwriting).
- Collusion or unauthorized collaboration in the preparation or presentation of work.
- Falsification, fabrication, manipulation or misrepresentation of data or results.
- Unauthorized sharing of course materials and previously submitted assessment items including via online study platforms.

Some tips to prevent academic dishonesty:

- Do your assignments on time.
- If you're having difficulties, ask for help from your Mentor as early as possible.
- If you are struggling with time and submissions,  talk to your Mentor about deadlines ahead of the day of submission.
- Cite and point out any references or sources you used for your homework.
- Acknowledge portions where you used exact words from a reference.

* * *

## Official Dropping of Courses – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/33992612249357-Official-Dropping-of-Courses

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/33992612249357-Official-Dropping-of-Courses#main-content)

**Overview**

This article explains the **official course dropping process** at Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC), including when and how you can drop a course and what forms or steps are required. It also outlines the implications of dropping a subject on your academic record and fees. Use this guide to understand your options and responsibilities if you need to drop a course during the term.

Dropping refers to the process of officially withdrawing from an enrolled course. The official dropping of a course must take place not later than the deadline set by the Registrar’s Office as indicated in the term calendar, or no later than the 10th week of the term.

## Guidelines:

1\. Requests for official dropping of courses must be done within the deadline or no later than the 10th week of the current term. Courses will not be allowed to be dropped after the deadline set forth by the office of the College Registrar as posted in the Term Calendar.

2\. A grade of "DRP" shall be earned to the course officially dropped regardless of the academic performance of the student. The grade of “DRP” can neither be removed nor completed. It has no bearing on the rules regarding refunds or payments made as stipulated in a memorandum from the Commission on Higher Education (CHED). **Note:** Approved drop requests are not eligible for refund.

3\. Students who intend to drop a course should be cleared of any disciplinary cases. Students shall obtain clearance from the Student Discipline and the Registrar's office.

4\. Request to drop a course should not violate the pre-requisite course regulation.

5\. Dropping a course that is a co-requisite of another course constitutes dropping of both courses.

6\. In cases wherein the student fails to officially drop a course, the faculty member shall be guided by the following:

- The student shall be given a final grade of “5.00” or “F” (Failed); or,
- The student shall be given a final grade of “FA” (Failure due to Absences) if he incurs excessive absences.

## Requirements:

1. [Application for Official Dropping of Course Form](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1NjwJoxwz2uKbA3BN3EUWDecnPtMhLCKs/view?usp=sharing)
2. Processing Fee of Php 50 per course
3. Student’s Valid ID or student ID

## Step-by-step Guide to Drop A Course:

1. Download a copy of the  [Application for Official Dropping of Course Form](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1NjwJoxwz2uKbA3BN3EUWDecnPtMhLCKs/view?usp=sharing). Fill it out and ensure that the form is complete with your student information and course information of the subjects you wish to drop.

- Course Information: Be sure to include the accurate course code and section (e.g., MO-SS033, H1102) for each course you wish to drop. Lec and Lab courses need to be indicated separately.
- Save as PDF: Save the completed form as a PDF file using the following format: \[Your Name\] \[Your Student Number\]. For example: Juan Dela Cruz 2022170945.
- Please see the sample below to be guided on how to fill out the Drop Form: ![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/41965765625613)

2\. Submit a Proof of payment for the processing fee amounting to 50 pesos per course.

1. When paying for services such as this, DO NOT USE YOUR OWN STUDENT NUMBER.
2. Please use 2020654321 or 2020123456 as the assigned processing code. Please see payment instructions below

[![Click here. (3 × 1 in) (1).png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/34941005081741)](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34560176570637-How-to-Pay-for-Processing-Fees-for-Requests-and-Services)


3\. Upload your completed requirements (the filled-out form, proof of payment, and student's valid ID) through this **Google Form:**[**https://forms.gle/AsQmFyv6WTbaWKq57**](https://forms.gle/AsQmFyv6WTbaWKq57)

**Note:**

Please allow 5-7 days for the changes to be reflected in your Camu account. You can expect an email from our team informing you whether your request has been approved or whether other necessary requirements/ clarifications are needed.

* * *

## Frequently Asked Questions (FAQs)

**1\. What does a DRP grade mean?**

A **DRP (Dropped)** mark means you officially withdrew from a course during the allowed period.

It does **not** affect your GWA, but it **stays permanently** on your academic record.

* * *

**2\. Will my tuition fees be reduced if I drop a course?**

No. MMDC does **not** adjust tuition or miscellaneous fees for dropped courses.

This is why it’s important to be certain before submitting your request.

* * *

**3\. Can I re-enroll the course I dropped?**

Yes. Any course marked **DRP** must be **re-enrolled and passed** in a future term if it is required in your curriculum.

* * *

**4\. Can dropping a course delay my graduation?**

Yes.

Dropping a course may affect your:

- Course sequencing

- Ability to take pre-requisite or co-requisite subjects

- Target graduation timeline


Always check your **Curriculum Plan** and consult your Integrated Advisor if unsure.

* * *

**5\. Can I drop multiple courses in one term?**

Yes, but consider the impact carefully.

Dropping several courses:

- May reduce you to a light load

- May affect scholarship eligibility (if applicable)

- May extend your program duration


When in doubt, seek advising.

* * *

**6\. What if I miss the official dropping deadline?**

Requests submitted **after the deadline** cannot be processed.

You will need to:

- Continue with the course, or

- Let the final grade be recorded based on submitted work


Late drops are not permitted.

* * *

**7\. Can I reverse a dropping request after submitting it?**

No. Once the dropping request is processed and approved, it is **final**.

Please review your decision carefully before submitting.

* * *

**8\. Will my instructors be notified?**

Yes. Your instructor and relevant offices will be notified once the dropping is officially recorded.

* * *

**9\. What if I am struggling for personal or medical reasons?**

You may explore other options such as:

- **Academic advising**

- **Course Completion for INC** (if applicable)


* * *

## Financial Services Related FAQs – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/33994484537357-Financial-Services-Related-FAQs

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/33994484537357-Financial-Services-Related-FAQs#main-content)

### **Payment Options and Methods**

#### **What are the available payment options?**

You can conveniently settle your school fees through any of the following payment channels:

- GCash
- Maya
- RCBC Over-the-Counter
- RCBC Online Banking
- MLhuillier
- Visa or Mastercard Debit and Credit Cards
- Remittance Services

#### **How can I pay using a credit or debit card?**

You can pay your tuition fees using any Visa or Mastercard debit or credit card. For step-by-step instructions, please refer to our [How-To Guide](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28696993735565).

If you encounter issues accessing the MMDC credit card payment portal, please submit a support ticket to our Integrated Advisors (IAs) for assistance.

### **How long does it take for my tuition payment to reflect in my Camu account?**

Payments are typically updated in your Camu account within two (2) days after the transaction is posted in the system.

### **Installment Plans and Late Payments**

#### **What installment plans are available?**

We offer two flexible installment plans to help you manage your tuition payments:

- Plan 1: 40%-30%-30%
  - 40% due upon enrollment
  - 30% due for the second installment
  - 30% due for the final installment
- Plan 2: 20%-40%-40%
  - 20% due upon enrollment
  - 40% due for the second installment
  - 40% due for the final installment

#### **Are there penalties for late payments?**

There are no penalties for late payments, but we strongly encourage you to pay on or before the scheduled due dates to avoid any disruptions to your enrollment.

### **Refunds and Excess Payments**

#### **What happens to excess payments?**

Any excess payments will be credited to your account and applied toward future fees or balances.

#### **How can I request a refund if I withdraw my enrollment?**

If you decide to withdraw your enrollment, you must submit an Enrollment Cancellation Request (ECR) to officially discontinue your studies at MMDC.

- If your ECR is submitted within the refund period (typically the first few weeks of the term), you may be eligible for a refund.
- Refund requests made after the designated period will no longer be eligible, and any remaining balance must still be settled.
- Refund processing may take up to 10 weeks.

### **Enrollment and Financial Requirements**

#### **Can I enroll for the next term if I still have an outstanding tuition balance?**

No, you must settle any outstanding tuition fees before you can re-enroll for the next term.

### **Payment Issues and Troubleshooting**

#### **I accidentally paid the wrong biller through GCash or Maya. What should I do?**

If you made a payment to the wrong biller, please contact ECPay Helpdesk for a reversal request. This ensures proper coordination between the school, GCash, and you as the student.

To request a reversal:

1. Email ECPay Helpdesk at helpdesk@ecpay.com.ph and provide your ECPay ticket number for tracking.
2. Submit a request to GCash through this link: [GCash Support Form](https://tinyurl.com/3srt77jb).

For further assistance, you may contact ECPay Customer Support at:

- Landline: (02) 7906-9530
- Globe: 09560797166, 09175432729, 09178008352, 09178009915, 09178013426, 09178028996
- SMART: 09190632729, 09988415489, 09985326629

### **Official Receipts and Documentation**

#### **How can I request an official receipt (OR)?**

Students can request either a physical or digital copy of their official receipt:

- Digital Copy: We will scan and send it to your registered email.
- Physical Copy:
  - Available for pick-up at Learning Hub QC (LH QC).
  - For students in Negros Occidental, it can be shipped to LH BCD for pickup.
  - For other locations, we can arrange shipping, but students must cover the shipping fee. MMDC’s partnership with LBC only covers deliveries between MCL, LH QC, and LH BCD.

To request a receipt, contact iaservices@mmdc.mcl.edu.ph.

### **Discounts and Financial Assistance**

#### **Do you offer discounts for Persons with Disabilities (PWDs)?**

MMDC does not offer direct PWD discounts. However, students may apply for financial aid programs offered by CHED, such as the Private Education Student Financial Assistance (PESFA) Program.

Under R.A. 7277, Section 13, financial assistance is available to economically marginalized but deserving PWD students pursuing post-secondary or tertiary education. This may include:

- Scholarships
- Student loan programs
- Subsidies and other incentives

Note: Being a PWD alone does not guarantee qualification. Applicants must meet both economic and academic eligibility criteria.

### **Flexible Financing Option from Bukas.ph**

#### **How can I apply for a Bukas loan?**

Applying for a Bukas loan is easy! Simply visit [this link](https://bukas.ph/partners/mmdc/) and follow the step-by-step application process.

#### **Can I request a refund for excess payments from my Bukas loan?**

No, excess payments from Bukas loans cannot be refunded to students. As stated in the loan agreement, the funds are strictly for educational purposes. Any excess amount will be:

- Credited toward your tuition for the next term, or
- Returned to Bukas.

## Your Guide to MMDC's Integrated Advising Team – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/33993546653837-Your-Guide-to-MMDC-s-Integrated-Advising-Team

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/33993546653837-Your-Guide-to-MMDC-s-Integrated-Advising-Team#main-content)

## **Overview**

This article explains what the **Integrated Advising Team** does and how they support you throughout your student journey.

## **What Is the Integrated Advising Team?**

The **Integrated Advising Team (IA)** is your **one-stop support group** for all MMDC-related concerns. Instead of visiting multiple offices for different services, you can reach out to the IAs for guidance, coordination, and assistance.

We support you with:

- **Student Records and Documents** – Requests and Registrar-related concerns

- **Financial Matters** – Payments, fees, and account inquiries

- **Technology Concerns** – Help with portals and MMDC systems

- **Personal, Psychological and Disciplinary Concerns** – Coordinating with the Discipline and Guidance and Counseling Office

- **General Student Services** – Any non-academic needs related to your student life


If your concern needs action from another department, your IA will coordinate on your behalf.

## **How to Reach the Integrated Advisors**

### Step 1: Start at the Help Center

|     |
| --- |
| ![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/41437126012301)[https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us) |

The [**MMDC Help Center**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us) is one of your most powerful tools as an MMDC student. It’s designed to give you **immediate access to clear answers, step-by-step instructions, and helpful guides**—anytime, anywhere you are.

The Integrated Advising team continuously builds and updates these articles so you can:

- Resolve common concerns **quickly and independently**

- Understand processes with easy-to-follow instructions

- Access accurate information without waiting for assistance


Think of the Help Center as **support at your fingertips**: fast, reliable, and available 24/7. Many of the questions students regularly ask already have complete, easy-to-use guides you can follow right away.

Using the Help Center empowers you to take control of your learning experience. And whenever you need personalized guidance or your situation requires a deeper conversation, the Integrated Advisors remain ready to support you in the next step.

### Step 2: Submit a Ticket

If you need further assistance or your case requires review, [**submit a ticket**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/requests/new) through the Help Center.

|     |
| --- |
| ![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/41437114859917) |

- This ensures your concern is logged, tracked, and properly queued for action.

- IAs prioritize tickets throughout the day.

- You may raise all types of inquiries or reqeusts here - if unsure on what to choose from the drop-down menu, feel free to use the **General Inquiry** option.


### Step 3: Schedule a Call (If Needed)

If your concern needs a conversation, you may coordinate with an IA to schedule a call **after** submitting your ticket.

- This helps the IA prepare the details of your case before the call.


### IA Availability

**Monday to Friday, 7:00 AM to 10:00 PM, Saturday 8:00 AM to 5:00 PM**

You can reach the team anytime within operating hours through:

- [**Help Center**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us)

- [**Submit a Request**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/requests/new) \- you m

- Official IA contact details (see related article: [_IA Contact Details_](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17465294854669-IA-Contact-Details))


* * *

## **How IAs Help You**

Your IA can:

- Answer your questions

- Process your requests

- Coordinate with other departments when needed

- Provide updates on your submitted tickets


They streamline support so you don’t need to navigate multiple offices or departments.

* * *

## **Proactive Support: We Check In With You!**

IAs also reach out from time to time to check on you and your experience and well-being. You may receive official emails from:

- **iaservices@mmdc.mcl.edu.ph**

- [**kumusta@mmdc.mcl.edu.ph**](mailto:kumusta@mmdc.mcl.edu.ph)


* * *

## **Your Success, Simplified**

The IA Team is here to make your student services experience simple and seamless, giving you more time to focus on your academic journey. Whenever you need support or have a question, you can count on the IAs to guide you.

## How to pay for Laptops under the Computer Lease-to-Own Program SY22 and SY23 – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34386842189197-How-to-pay-for-Laptops-under-the-Computer-Lease-to-Own-Program-SY22-and-SY23

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34386842189197-How-to-pay-for-Laptops-under-the-Computer-Lease-to-Own-Program-SY22-and-SY23#main-content)

_This article explains how students can pay their laptop balance using the official payment channel provided by the school. It includes the exact steps to follow and where to send your payment._

#### **via Bank Transfer**

1. Make a Fund Transfer to **MMCL's RCBC Bank Account**

Bank Name: Rizal Commercial Banking Corporation (RCBC)

Account Name: Malayan Colleges Laguna, INC. A Mapua School

Account Number: 7590679940
2. Finalize your payment and receive your payment confirmation.
3. Send a copy of your proof of payment to [mmdc\_treasury@mcl.edu.ph](mailto:mmdc_treasury@mcl.edu.ph), CC in the email [iaservices@mmdc.mcl.edu.ph](mailto:iaservices@mmdc.mcl.edu.ph). Indicate the following info in your email:

THIS PAYMENT IS FOR LAPTOP

Student Name

Student Number

Amount Paid

Date of Payment
4. Submit also your proof of payment using this Google Form - [https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSfhB9D\_xOEIL8gE8zEeEP90N0MZ5YG6nz9I5XgmtdJwRwXk8Q/viewform](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSfhB9D_xOEIL8gE8zEeEP90N0MZ5YG6nz9I5XgmtdJwRwXk8Q/viewform)

**Note:** This is the only payment channel available for laptop payments. Other channels are for tuition and matriculation fees. If payments are made via the other channels, it will automatically be deducted from your tuition balance, and NOT from your laptop balance.

## Welcome to the MMDC Learner Help Center! – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34019974488589-Welcome-to-the-MMDC-Learner-Help-Center

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34019974488589-Welcome-to-the-MMDC-Learner-Help-Center#main-content)

|     |
| --- |
| ## **Overview**<br>The **MMDC Learner Help Center** is your primary guide for navigating your academic journey—from enrollment and payments to academic policies, systems access, and student services. It brings together step-by-step guides, FAQs, and troubleshooting resources in one easy-to-use platform. **Use this Help Center anytime to get clear, reliable answers—often within minutes.** |

* * *

## **Table of Contents:**

1. [What is the MMDC Learner Help Center?](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34019974488589-Welcome-to-the-MMDC-Learner-Help-Center#h_01KGPHYBCCGVRSP8AQPSCFJ11A)

5. [How to Use the Help Center Effectively](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34019974488589-Welcome-to-the-MMDC-Learner-Help-Center#h_01KGPJMVBFNYSW3RV40SAPJRZF)
6. [When to Contact Support](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34019974488589-Welcome-to-the-MMDC-Learner-Help-Center#h_01KGPK7KCBRWHDWFMQJ5Z64HTX)

* * *

## **What Is the MMDC Learner Help Center?**

The MMDC Learner Help Center is your centralized online support hub. It contains verified information, official guidelines, and practical instructions to help you manage your studies independently and confidently.

Here, you can find:

- Enrollment and registration guides

- Tuition and payment information

- Academic policies and procedures

- System and account support

- Student services

- Practicum and graduation requirements

- Forms, requests, and reminders


All articles are reviewed and updated by MMDC offices to ensure accuracy and consistency.

##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34019974488589-Welcome-to-the-MMDC-Learner-Help-Center\#h_01KG4HGT9QG8Y4K21BRSX5W7K4)

* * *

## **Why Use the Help Center?**

The Help Center is designed to give you **fast, reliable answers—24/7**, wherever you are.

By using it, you can:

- Get immediate responses to common questions

- Follow step-by-step guides without waiting for replies

- Resolve concerns at your own pace

- Avoid unnecessary delays in processing requests


Most student concerns already have ready-to-use guides, making it easier for you to move forward without interruption.

|     |
| --- |
| 📌 **Tip:**<br>Many questions about enrollment, payments, grades, and systems access can be resolved in just a few clicks. |

##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34019974488589-Welcome-to-the-MMDC-Learner-Help-Center\#h_01KG4HGT9QG8Y4K21BRSX5W7K4)

* * *

## **How the Help Center Supports You**

The Help Center works alongside your Integrated Advisors.

When you use the Help Center:

- You receive instant guidance for routine concerns

- Advisors can focus on cases that need personalized support

- Requests are processed more efficiently

- Support services remain responsive and accessible


This system ensures that you get the right level of help—quick self-service when possible, and personal support when needed.

##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34019974488589-Welcome-to-the-MMDC-Learner-Help-Center\#h_01KG4HGT9QG8Y4K21BRSX5W7K4)

* * *

## **Bookmark This Page**

We recommend bookmarking the Help Center and visiting it regularly. It serves as your main entry point to student support throughout your stay at MMDC.

Having it easily accessible helps you:

- Stay updated

- Meet deadlines

- Avoid missed requirements

- Stay informed each term


##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34019974488589-Welcome-to-the-MMDC-Learner-Help-Center\#h_01KG4HGT9QG8Y4K21BRSX5W7K4)

* * *

## **How to Use the Help Center Effectively**

### 1\. Use the Search Bar

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/41921051944845)

Type keywords related to your concern (e.g., _enrollment_, _grades_, _Google account_, _LOA_).

The system will suggest the most relevant articles as well as a Quick Answer.

**Quick Answers** are AI-powered response that scans Help Center content to provide a short answer, similar to a Google search.

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/41921071314957)

|     |
| --- |
| _Please note:_ AI-generated answers may occasionally be incomplete or inaccurate. For full context and the most reliable information, we recommend reviewing the related help article. |

### 2\. Browse by Category

Explore organized sections such as:

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/41921071314445)

- Enrollment and Admissions

- Academic Programs and Policies

- Student Services

- Internship and Graduation

- Career Development Services


### 3\. Follow Step-by-Step Guides

Most articles include clear instructions, timelines, and reminders to help you complete processes correctly.

### 4\. Using the Chatbot

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/41921071314701)

The chatbot widget answers questions based on Help Center articles and is helpful when you’re unsure where to start.

If the chatbot is unable to provide the answer you need, it may guide you to submit a request so the **Integrated Advising (IA) team** can assist you.

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/41921071315213)

##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34019974488589-Welcome-to-the-MMDC-Learner-Help-Center\#h_01KG4HGT9QG8Y4K21BRSX5W7K4)

* * *

## **When to Contact Support**

If you cannot find the answer you need after checking the Help Center, you may contact the Integrated Advisors by raising a ticket

|     |
| --- |
| 📌 **Important:**<br>When reaching out, including screenshots and reference links from Help Center articles helps speed up assistance. |

## **Final Reminder**

Make the MMDC Learner Help Center your first and trusted resource. With clear guides, updated policies, and 24/7 access, it is designed to help you stay informed, confident, and in control of your academic journey.

##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34019974488589-Welcome-to-the-MMDC-Learner-Help-Center\#h_01KG4HGT9QG8Y4K21BRSX5W7K4)

## Suggest Edits & Article Requests for the Help Center – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34422551539341-Suggest-Edits-Article-Requests-for-the-Help-Center

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34422551539341-Suggest-Edits-Article-Requests-for-the-Help-Center#main-content)

At MMDC, we strive to provide you with a **comprehensive and up-to-date Help Center** to support your college journey. If you come across an article that needs an update or if there’s a topic you think should be added, **we’d love to hear from you!**

Your feedback helps us improve and ensures that all students have access to the most relevant and helpful information. If you would like to suggest edits to an existing article or request a new help guide, please fill out the form below:

📌 **[Suggest Edits or Request a New Help Article](https://forms.gle/4ARSebZZuZKHk2SG8)**

_Google Form link: [https://forms.gle/4ARSebZZuZKHk2SG8](https://forms.gle/4ARSebZZuZKHk2SG8))_

### **What Can You Request?**

✅ Updates to outdated information

✅ Additional details to improve an existing article

✅ A new guide on a topic that isn’t covered yet

✅ Clarifications on policies, procedures, or student services

### **How It Works**

1. **Submit your request** through the form.
2. Our team will **review your suggestion** and assess its relevance.
3. If approved, we’ll **update or create the article** and notify you once it’s published.

We appreciate your help in making the MMDC Help Center better for everyone! Thank you for contributing to a more **informed and empowered student community.** 💡✨

## How to Pay for Other Charges and Processing Fees for Requests and Services – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34560176570637-How-to-Pay-for-Other-Charges-and-Processing-Fees-for-Requests-and-Services

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34560176570637-How-to-Pay-for-Other-Charges-and-Processing-Fees-for-Requests-and-Services#main-content)

To make paying for other charges and processing fees for requests and services easy and hassle-free, we provide multiple payment options. Below are the available options along with step-by-step instructions for each.

### For Document Request and other services such as Course Load Revision, Dropping, Shifting, Enrollment Cancellation and Course Completion

#### **via GCash Bills Payment:**

1. From the main menu of the **GCash App**, click “Bills”.
2. In the **Bills** section, you'll find an option labeled "Schools". Simply click on this option to proceed.
3. From the **School** s list, choose **(MMDC) Mapua Malayan Digital College**.

**Note:** Please ensure to select Mapua Malayan Digital College (MMDC), and NOT Mapua Malayan Colleges Mindanao (MMCM) or Mapua University

4. Enter the required information: **Amount**, **Student Number**, **Surname** and **Purpose of Payment, Email Address.** For other requests and services, instead of your personal Student Number, use the following **processing codes**:


**2020123456 / 2020654321 / 2020765432 /2020876543 / 2020987654**


**Note:** Payments using the student’s personal student number will automatically be deducted from the tuition fees. The processing codes listed above are the indicators that the payment are for other services and requests.

5. Finalize your payment and receive your **payment confirmation**.
6. Attach a copy of the payment confirmation to submit your request to the IA Services.

#### **via Maya Bills Payment**

1. From the main menu of the **Maya App**, click “Bills”.
2. In the **Bills** section, you'll find an option labeled " **Schools**". Simply click on this option to proceed.
3. From the Schools list, click **Mapua Malayan Digital College**.
4. Enter the **Account number**, **Amount** and **Surname and Purpose of Payment.** For the Account Number, you may use any of the following **processing codes**:


2020123456 / 2020654321 / 2020765432 / 2020876543 / 2020987654


5\. Finalize your payment and receive your payment confirmation.

6\. Attach a copy of the payment confirmation to submit your request to the IA Services.

## The Outstanding Working Students of MMDC – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34941403931917-The-Outstanding-Working-Students-of-MMDC

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34941403931917-The-Outstanding-Working-Students-of-MMDC#main-content)

At Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC), we recognize that being a working student is more than just balancing responsibilities—it’s a testament to resilience, ambition, and perseverance.

## TOWS of MMDC Award

The **Outstanding Working Students of MMDC (TOWS of MMDC) Award** is a recognition program that honors **students who successfully juggle academics and work while making a positive impact in school, their workplace, community, or industry**. This award celebrates individuals who embody excellence, leadership, exceptional character and dedication, proving that **hard work and education can go hand in hand.**

## Recognition Ceremony on March 21, 2025

In recognizing the efforts of working students, MMDC is also celebrating **National Working Students Day (NWSD)**. As we celebrate the **first-ever National Working Students Day** on **March 21, 2025**, we are proud to launch **The Outstanding Working Students of MMDC (TOWS of MMDC) Award.** Through this award, we aim to inspire fellow students, highlight the incredible journeys of MMDC’s working learners, and showcase the real-world application of education in the workforce.

More than just an award, TOWS of MMDC is a platform to uplift and empower working students by providing them with well-deserved acknowledgment, motivation, and opportunities to grow professionally.

**If you are one of MMDC’s Outstanding Working Students,** share your story, inspire others, and gain well-earned recognition for your dedication. We are eager to hear your story and recognize your hard work!

## Why and How to Apply for The Outstanding Working Students of MMDC Award

If you are balancing both work and academics, this is your opportunity to be acknowledged for your dedication and achievements. To apply for **The Outstanding Working Students of MMDC (OWS-MMDC) Award**, simply submit a portfolio that showcases how you manage your work and studies while making a positive impact in your workplace or community. This portfolio should demonstrate your leadership, commitment, and ability to excel in both your professional and academic endeavors. By applying, you’ll not only receive well-deserved recognition but also inspire your fellow students and gain valuable experience that can boost your professional profile.

## 📌 How to Apply: Portfolio Submission Guide

**Step 1: Prepare Your Portfolio**

Your portfolio must include **clear proof** that you meet the **10 eligibility criteria** to qualify for the TOWS of MMDC Award. You may submit a **combination of documents, images, videos, or testimonials** that showcase your qualifications.

**Step 2: Organize Your Portfolio**

Arrange your portfolio in a **Google Drive folder** and include:

📌 **A Cover Page** – Your name, MMDC student ID, course, and a brief personal statement (max 200 words) about your work-study journey.

📌 **A Table of Contents** – Listing the eligibility criteria and corresponding proof for each.

📌 **Files & Documentation** – All supporting documents, screenshots, testimonials, or media files properly labeled.

**Step 3: Submit Your Portfolio**

📅 **Deadline:** The Monday before the National Working Students Day Celebration

For 2025, the deadline is on March 17, 2025.

📍 **Where to Submit:** Upload your portfolio to Google Drive and share the link via the

GFORM: [https://forms.gle/GKdeuaCGnTSaNn8f6](https://forms.gle/GKdeuaCGnTSaNn8f6)

Ensure **viewing permissions** are set to allow access to anyone from the Mapua Malayan Digital College Organization.

**Step 4: Evaluation & Announcement**

✔ Portfolios will be reviewed by a selection committee based on completeness, impact, and alignment with MMDC’s values.

✔ **Finalists** will be notified 2 days after the submission deadline and invited to the **Recognition Ceremony** during **Hustle & Thrive on March 21, 2025.**

## 🔹 10-point Eligibility Criteria

To qualify for **The Outstanding Working Students of MMDC (TOWS of MMDC)**, applicants must meet the following criteria and provide proof through a portfolio submission:

**Academic Commitment & Performance**

1️⃣ **Currently Enrolled at MMDC** – Must be a consisten enrollee and an active MMDC student at the time of application.

_(Proof: Screenshot of student portal)_

2️⃣ **Actively Employed or Managing a Business** – Must be working part-time, full-time, freelancing, or running a business.

_(Proof: Employment ID/ Certificate of Employment/ business permit/ freelancing portfolio employment documents/ photos)_

3️⃣ **Good Academic Standing** – No failing grades in all courses taken so far.

_(Proof: Screenshot of grades or transcript from Camu.)_

**Work-School Balance & Dedication**

_(Proof: Personal essay or work-study schedule/ letter or reviews from work/ employer, business testimonials, or client reviews)_

4️⃣ **Demonstrates Effective Work-Study Balance** – Shows the ability to manage both responsibilities successfully.

5️⃣ **Strong Work Ethic & Commitment** – A positive record in the workplace or business, with good feedback from employer, clients, or colleagues.

**Impact & Contributions**

_(Proof: Any of a combination of the following: Work samples, project reports, or employer feedback/ Short essay or video testimony explaining the challenges and how they were managed/ Leadership role documentation, work project, or community initiative/ Peer recommendations, feedback from team members, or mentoring logs)_

6️⃣ **Applies Learning from MMDC in the Workplace** – Uses skills or knowledge gained from MMDC to improve work performance.

7️⃣ **Demonstrates Resilience & Perseverance** – Has overcome challenges while continuing studies and work.

8️⃣ **Shows Leadership or Initiative** – Has taken initiative at work, in academics, or in a community setting.

9️⃣ **Positive Influence on Peers & Colleagues** – Actively supports or mentors others in either school or work settings.

**MMDC Engagement & Values**

🔟 **Embodies MMDC’s Values** – Shows integrity, excellence, and responsibility as a working student. _(Proof: short statement on how MMDC’s values are applied in their academic and professional life.)_

_Note: Feel free to add any additional proof that you see fit._

## MMDC's Position on the Use of AI Tools – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37180248710541-MMDC-s-Position-on-the-Use-of-AI-Tools

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37180248710541-MMDC-s-Position-on-the-Use-of-AI-Tools#main-content)

## **Overview**

This article explains MMDC’s official policy regarding the use of AI tools in coursework and learning. It clarifies what tools are permitted, how students should disclose AI-generated content, and the ethical standards expected. Use this guide to understand what constitutes acceptable use — and to avoid academic integrity issues.

* * *

## **Generative AI Policy for MMDC:**

At MMDC, we recognize the significant potential of generative artificial intelligence (AI) as a productivity tool, particularly in the realm of written outputs. This policy outlines our stance on the careful and transparent use of generative AI within our college community, emphasizing its positive role as an aid to enhance learning and academic growth.

### **1\. Importance of Generative AI in College:**

Generative AI is poised to become an essential tool for the future, providing opportunities for increased efficiency and innovation. While its application in grade school and high school environments may present some difficult decisions, at the college level, we encourage students to embrace and learn how to utilize generative AI as part of their educational journey.

### **2\. Responsible Use of Generative AI:**

Students are expected to exercise caution when using generative AI, ensuring it serves as an assistance tool rather than a means to bypass thinking. Brief and thoughtless prompts that merely task generative AI with completing college work on behalf of the student won’t help students learn and won’t help students succeed when they graduate from college. Further, these types of outputs will be detectable in their general and generic nature. They will lack specificity - and professors will spot this and not accept this work. Instead, students should provide long and detailed prompts that reflect their own thought processes. Good use of generative AI requires telling it, in detail, what you want it to write. This approach encourages students to engage with generative AI in a manner that promotes personal growth and comprehension of the subject matter.

### **3\. Iteration and Editing:**

When utilizing generative AI, it is crucial to recognize that the output it generates should be treated as an iterative process. The initial output from the AI system should be carefully reviewed, refined, and iterated upon by the student. This is done by literally directing the generative AI to add, change, delete and edit what its prior versions. This iterative approach ensures that the final product reflects the student's own understanding, thoughts, goals and intentions.

### **4\. Enhancing Language Skills:**

Generative AI can be particularly beneficial for students who struggle with writing in English, as it can help improve grammar and syntax. It is important to remember that generative AI should not replace the student's effort to develop their language skills. It should serve as a support mechanism, providing suggestions and guidance, while the student actively engages in the learning process.

For example, when a student plans to produce a written output that is approximately 2 pages and 7 paragraphs, they can type each paragraph into the prompt and simply direct the generative AI to correct the grammar and syntax. The generative AI will “clean up” the English, quite nicely. The student can then re-read what the generative AI produced, noting the difference between what she wrote and the AI wrote. Through this, the student can see how to produce more accurate sentences. A student should never just copy and paste what generative AI wrote, without reading it and being sure it reflects THEIR thoughts and ideas, simply written with better English.

### **5\. Disclosure of Generative AI Use:**

Students must indicate whether they have utilized generative AI to assist in their writing tasks when submitting assignments to professors. This disclosure is meant to foster a culture of transparency and open communication. It is important to note that indicating the use of generative AI will not be counted against students in the grading process. We value academic honesty and believe that acknowledging generative AI use can contribute to constructive feedback and support from professors.

### **6\. Limits of Generative AI in Dealing with Recency of Information:**

While generative AI holds great promise as a tool to aid students in their academic pursuits, it is essential to acknowledge its limitations, particularly concerning the recency of information. Generative AI systems are trained on vast amounts of data up until a specific cutoff date, which means they may not possess knowledge of events or developments that have occurred after their training data was last updated. This limitation implies that generative AI might not accurately reflect the most recent information, emerging trends, or current events. Therefore, it is crucial for students to exercise caution when relying solely on generative AI outputs as a source of up-to-date and accurate information. To address this limitation, we encourage students to complement generative AI with additional research and verification methods, ensuring the inclusion of the latest information relevant to their academic work.

MMDC aims to create an environment where generative AI is harnessed responsibly, fostering academic growth and empowering students to develop critical thinking skills. We trust that our students will embrace the potential of generative AI while upholding the principles of integrity, transparency, and personal growth in their academic pursuits.

**\\_\\_\\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_**

This policy is subject to periodic review and may be updated as technology advances and new considerations arise. _Version 001. August 16, 2023_

## New Student Orientation – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/36111115429901-New-Student-Orientation

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/36111115429901-New-Student-Orientation#main-content)

**Welcome to Mapúa Malayan Digital College** — we’re thrilled to have you on board!

As you begin your journey with us, we want to make sure you’re equipped with all the tools and information you need to succeed in our digital campus.

You may have missed attending the Orientation session where we walked you through the essentials of being an MMDC student — from navigating our platforms (Google and Camu) and managing your schedule, to understanding the PPC learning model, student services, online etiquette and making the most of your learning experience. If you missed the live session or simply want to review the materials at your own pace, we’ve got you covered.

Click the link below to access the **New Student Orientation Deck**. This contains all the slides and key points discussed during the session, including helpful tips, quick guides, and links to important resources.

📂 **\[ [Access the Orientation Deck Here](https://docs.google.com/presentation/d/10wNMBvBh-4A2K6GeiEP3q9_qX1FK_vPP/edit?usp=sharing&ouid=115558910485059255561&rtpof=true&sd=true)\]**

**📂 \[ [Watch the Orientation Recording Here](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1hF_u4W5wsG0TB196Dxp5hATm0_gkQ9rQ/view?usp=sharing)\]**

We’re here to support you every step of the way. If you have any questions after reviewing the deck, don’t hesitate to reach out through our Help Center or message our student support team.

Let’s make this term a meaningful start to your college journey.

Welcome to MMDC!

## Form 137 Request Letter – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37478613702669-Form-137-Request-Letter

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37478613702669-Form-137-Request-Letter#main-content)

## **Overview**

This article explains how to request a **Form 137 (School Form 10 / Learner’s Permanent Academic Record)** request letter, which is often required by schools to release your academic records.

* * *

## **Who Needs This**

Incoming freshmen may need a Form 137 request letter with the remark:

> **“Copy for Mapúa Malayan Colleges Laguna”**

Some schools require an official letter to release this document.

* * *

## **How to Request a Form 137 Letter**

1. **Submit a Request**
   - Go to the [**Help Center**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us) to [**submit a ticket**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/requests/new?ticket_form_id=24991884450061) **.**
2. **Include the Following Information**
   - Full Student Name

   - School Name

   - Complete School Address
3. **Processing Time**
   - A **digital copy** of the Form 137 request letter will be sent to you.

   - Allow **1–3 business days** for processing.

* * *

|     |
| --- |
| 🎓 **Not yet an MMDC student?**<br>Discover [Mapúa Malayan Digital College](https://www.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/)— a flexible online college built for working students.<br>Start your [BS IT degree](https://www.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/college-programs/) or upskill through [Certification Programs.](https://www.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/certification-programs/) |
