## Asenso Scholarship Discount Program – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37450066753805-Asenso-Scholarship-Discount-Program

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37450066753805-Asenso-Scholarship-Discount-Program#main-content)

## About the Program

At MMDC, we remain committed to providing affordable, flexible, and meaningful education to every learner. We understand that for many, financial support isn't just helpful—it’s essential.

Since its launch on Term 1 of SY 2023, the **Asenso Scholarship Discount Program** has been a key part of that commitment. Originally launched as a promotional initiative, it has continued to serve our students for six consecutive terms, providing a 36% tuition fee discount to all.

To ensure the program remains sustainable and responsive to those who need it most, we are introducing an updated structure beginning **School Year 2025–2026**.

## What’s Changing?

Starting **Term 1, SY 2025–2026**, the **Asenso Scholarship Discount Program** will transition to a **tiered discount structure,** allowing for sustainable and continuous support for all students while providing greater assistance to those experiencing more financial difficulty.

| Category | **Current Structure: SY 2023-2024 and SY2024-2025** | **Revised Structure: SY 2025-2026 Onwards** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Tuition Discount** | 36% for all students | 20% automatic tuition discount for all students |
| **Additional Discount** | Not applicable | +16% for students with monthly income of ₱10K–₱49.9K |
| **Total Possible Discount** | 36% flat rate | 20%–36%, depending on financial need |
| **Income Requirement** | None | Income eligibility requirement (₱10K–₱49.9K) for the additional 16% discount |
| **Validity** | Ongoing | 20% Ongoing; Additional 16% valid per term; reapplication needed |

## Who Is Eligible?

The updated Asenso Scholarship Discount Program applies to:

- **all MMDC students admitted from SY 2023–2024 onwards**
- **new applicants starting SY 2025–2026**

This applies to students enrolled in:

- **BS in Business Administration**
- **BS in Information Technology**

**Note:** **The** Asenso Scholarship Discount, launched in Term 1 of SY2023- 2024, differs from the Pioneer Scholarship Discount, which was introduced in SY2022- 2023. Students admitted in SY22-23 are under the Pioneer Scholarship Discount. For more info on this, check the [Pioneer Scholarship Discount Help Guide](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37478793749517/live_preview/01JY3DAVDGFEZBK8MSEX29PJ1E).

### What Discounts Are Available?

- **Automatic 20% Tuition Fee Discount:** All students automatically receive a **20% tuition fee discount**
- **Additional 16% Tuition Fee Discount:** Available to students with a monthly personal income between **₱10,000 and ₱49,999,** upon submission and approval of required documents

### Requirements for the Additional 16% Discount

Students applying for the additional 16% must submit **all of the following documents**, depending on their employment status:

#### For Formally Employed Students or Parents/Guardians:

- Latest 3 months' **payslips**
- **Certificate of Employment** with salary details
- **BIR Form 2316**
- **Bank Statement** (past 3 months)

#### For Informally Employed Students/ Freelancers/ Self-Employed:

- **Financial Declaration / Affidavit of Income** (notarized) or **proof of freelance/part-time work contracts**
- **Bank Statement** (past 3 months)
- **Business Permit / DTI Registration** (if applicable)
- **Latest Income Tax Return** (if applicable)

#### For Financially Dependent Students (Not Employed):

- Financial documents of supporting parent/guardian (see above)
- **Proof of relationship** (e.g., NSO Birth Certificate or legal affidavit)

**Note:**You may also submit **additional supporting documents** not listed if you believe they can strengthen your application.

## How to Apply for the Additional 16% Discount

### Step 1: Prepare Your Documents

Depending on your (or your family’s) source of income, please see the required documents listed above.

_Important:_ MMDC may request additional documents or conduct interviews to verify your eligibility. Submitting falsified documents will result in disqualification and disciplinary action.

### Step 2: Submit Your Application

- Fill out the [**Asenso +16% Application Form**](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1tBOpJTckL7isNO0AWMV-Hm493gG5bbsf/view?usp=sharing)
  - Download the PDF Version of the application form linked here: [**Asenso +16% Application Form**](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1tBOpJTckL7isNO0AWMV-Hm493gG5bbsf/view?usp=sharing)
- Submit your application and documents during the designated application window

(opens **4 weeks before the start of enrollment** for each term)
- Upload all required documents via the official Google Form submission link: [**Submission for Asenso +16% Discount**](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSeI2bGG1HYAvWp7U8ZQ23SbSzFJARR8F226uoz4BMvOyhV-Bg/viewform?usp=pp_url)

**Note:**Applications submitted **after the set deadline** will not be accepted.

### Step 3: Notification of Results

- Results will be sent **within 5 business days** after submission of all complete requirements.
- If approved, the additional 16% discount will be applied to the next term's enrollment and will be valid for one term only.

**Note:** Students must **reapply every term** to continue receiving the additional support. This takes into account the changing financial circumstances of students from term to term.

## Application Timeline

- The application period typically opens **4 weeks before the enrollment period begins**
- Applications must be finalized **before the first day of enrollment**
- Late or mid-term applications will **not be accepted**

* * *

## 🔔 Key Reminders

- The **20% base discount** is automatic—no need to apply
- The **additional 16% discount** is not automatic—students must apply and qualify
- Students may apply for the additional discount in **later terms** if their financial situation changes (e.g., job change)
- The discount is **applicable to tuition fees only.**
- Students who do not enroll during the official enrollment period will **forfeit the approved discount** for that term
- Dropped courses will still be included in tuition fee calculations
- The Asenso Discount is **non-convertible, non-transferable, and non-deferrable**
- Program terms are effective until further notice. Eligibility, coverage, and validity are final and will remain in place until the next official update.

* * *

## 🤔 Frequently Asked Questions (FAQs)

### **Will my tuition or fees increase next year?**

No. MMDC is keeping **all tuition and miscellaneous fees unchanged** for SY 2025–2026.

### **How long will the revised program be in place?**

The updated Asenso Scholarship Discount Program 2025 will remain in effect **until further notice** from MMDC.

## Pioneer Scholarship Discount Program – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37478793749517-Pioneer-Scholarship-Discount-Program

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37478793749517-Pioneer-Scholarship-Discount-Program#main-content)

## About the Program

The **Pioneer Scholarship Discount Program** was MMDC’s founding financial assistance initiative, created to support and incentivize the very first batch of learners who enrolled during **School Year 2022–2023**.

This exclusive program granted a **36% tuition fee discount** to all qualified students, without the need for submission of financial documents. It was designed to recognize the trust placed in MMDC by our first students—and to honor our commitment to seeing them through to graduation.

## Who Is Covered?

The Pioneer Discount is available **only** to students who were admitted in **SY 2022–2023** and are currently enrolled in:

- **Bachelor of Science in Business Administration**
- **Bachelor of Science in Information Technology**

Students admitted in later school years are **not eligible** for this program and are instead covered by the [Asenso Scholarship Discount Program 2025 Help Guide](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37450066753805).

## What Are the Benefits?

🎓 **36% Tuition Fee Discount**

This discount is automatically applied and valid until:

- The student completes their program **or**
- The end of **SY 2025–2026**, **whichever comes first**

There is **no need to reapply each term** or submit any proof of income. The discount is granted for the full duration of eligibility.

## How Long Does the Discount Last?

The Pioneer Discount applies:

- From the time of admission (SY 2022–2023)
- Until **graduation or the end of SY 2025–2026**, **whichever occurs earlier**

Students who need more time to complete their degree after SY 2025–2026—whether due to part-time study, LOA, or other delays—will automatically **transition to the Asenso Scholarship Discount Program**.

At that point, they will need to follow the [Asenso Scholarship Discount Program](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37450066753805)'s requirements, including applying for additional aid (up to 36%) based on financial need.

## What Happens After SY 2025–2026?

If you are still completing your degree after the end of SY 2025–2026, you will:

- **No longer be covered** by the Pioneer Scholarship Discount Program
- **Be automatically shifted** to the Asenso Scholarship Discount Program 2025  - Under the Asenso Scholarship Discount Program 2025, students are eligible to:
    - **20% automatic tuition discount**
    - **+16% additional discount** (subject to application and verified income)

* * *

## 🔔 Key Reminders

- The **36% discount** applies to **tuition fees only**
- It **does not cover** miscellaneous fees or other school charges
- Any **dropped or withdrawn subjects** are still counted toward the tuition fee computation
- The Pioneer Discount is **non-convertible, non-transferable, and non-deferrable**
- Program terms are effective until further notice. Eligibility, coverage, and validity are final and will remain in place until the next official update.

## How to Request a Transfer Credential (TC) Package – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37497953771149-How-to-Request-a-Transfer-Credential-TC-Package

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37497953771149-How-to-Request-a-Transfer-Credential-TC-Package#main-content)

_The Transfer Credential (TC) Package is for students (active or inactive) planning to transfer to another school. This article provides essential details on what documents are included in the package, the requirements, the step-by-step process, and the timelines you should follow to ensure a smooth transfer._

This article includes:

- [List of Documents Included in the Transfer Credentials (TC) Package](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37497953771149-How-to-Request-a-Transfer-Credential-TC-Package#h_01JY5MC3DNM0MH27WT70H55SC3)
- [Requirements for Requesting the TC Package](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37497953771149-How-to-Request-a-Transfer-Credential-TC-Package#h_01JY5MQQVBYQE5YK2B5Q94H7AZ)
- [Step-by-Step Process for Requesting the TC Package](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37497953771149-How-to-Request-a-Transfer-Credential-TC-Package#h_01JY5MYXQK8GTS5819Q7JQZGYN)
- [Student Clearance Guidelines](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37497953771149-How-to-Request-a-Transfer-Credential-TC-Package#h_01JY5NTW947FKQ7J2DXMHQDFSS)
- [Frequently Asked Questions](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37497953771149-How-to-Request-a-Transfer-Credential-TC-Package#h_01JY5P3W2DBM6V1RXDEHGM59BK)


## Documents Included in the Transfer Credentials (TC) Package

● **Certificate of Transfer Credential / Honorable Dismissal**

● **Grade Certification**

● **Good Moral Certificate**

As a final step, the final **Transcript of Records (TOR)** will be issued to the new school once MMDC receives the Return Slip originally attached to the Certificate of Transfer Credential/ Honorable Dismissal. The Return Slip should be duly signed by the Registrar of the next school to confirm the student's transfer to that institution.

## Requirements for Requesting the TC Package

● Completed Application for Transfer Credentials Form: [REVISED MMCL OCR 011A -](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1LlGsK8wmiHU7NKWvfpM_XLcpDaX262b5/view?usp=sharing)

[APPLICATION FOR TRANSFER CREDENTIALS\_FILLABLE FORM (1).pdf](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1LlGsK8wmiHU7NKWvfpM_XLcpDaX262b5/view?usp=sharing)

● Proof of processing fee payment amounting to ₱1,040 _(For payment instructions, click here:_ [_How to Pay for Processing Fees for Requests and Services – MMDC_](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34560176570637-How-to-Pay-for-Processing-Fees-for-Requests-and-Services) _)_

## Step-by-Step Process

#### Step 1: Fill Out the Application Form

● Download the Application for Transfer Credentials Form

● Fill it out completely and accurately

● Affix your signature on the form

#### Step 2: Pay the Processing Fee

● Amount: ₱1,040

● When paying, do not use your student number. Use 2020654321 or 2020123456 as the

assigned processing code.

● For payment instructions, click here: [How to Pay for Processing Fees for Requests and](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34560176570637-How-to-Pay-for-Processing-Fees-for-Requests-and-Services)

[Services – MMDC](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34560176570637-How-to-Pay-for-Processing-Fees-for-Requests-and-Services)

#### Step 3: Submit Your Request

● [**Send the accomplished form and proof of payment here.**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/requests/new)

## Student Clearance Guidelines

#### 1\. Clearance Signing

Your request will go through five (5) offices for clearance:

- Center for Learning and Information Resources (CLIR)
- Center for Guidance and Counseling (CGC)
- Student Affairs Office (SAO)
- Registrar’s Office
- Treasury Office

Your documents will be prepared and released only after **all offices** have signed off on your

clearance.

#### 2\. Pending Admission Documents (Physical Copies)

The physical copies of your admission documents must be submitted within your initial term at MMDC. If you have not yet submitted the physical copies of your admission requirements, this may cause delays in the clearance processing. Make sure to complete your physical documents submissions as part of your clearance.

#### 3\. INC Grades

- If you **failed to request** a course completion of your INC grade during the applicable term, the course/subject will be marked as 5.00.
- If you **submitted a course completion request**, your grade will be updated to 3.00 after one (1)

term.

_For more information about the **Course Completion Process**, please refer to this guide:_ [_Course Completion for INC Grades_](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/32265959292557-Course-Completion-for-INC-Grades)

#### 4\. Outstanding Balances

Clearance cannot proceed if you have unpaid balances related to tuition and/or your lease-to-own laptop account if you availed of this program. Please settle any balances before submitting your request.

_For more information about the **laptop device payments**, please refer to this guide:_ [_How to pay for laptop devices under the lease-to-own program_](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34386842189197-How-to-pay-for-Laptops-under-the-Computer-Lease-to-Own-Program-SY22-and-SY23)

_For more information about the available **payment channels for tuition fee payments**, please refer to this guide:_ [_Tuition Fee Payment Channels_](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17707754312845/live_preview/01JY5QAXB3YYWGJAK3VAEA282D)

#### Processing Timeline

Please allow **6–7 weeks** for processing. This timeline covers all internal procedures, clearance verification, and administrative validation of your records and accounts.

## Frequently Asked Questions

#### 1. **Where does my clearance go?**

Your clearance form will be routed through **five offices**:

- Center for Learning and Information Resources (CLIR)
- Center for Guidance and Counseling (CGC)
- Student Affairs Office (SAO)
- Registrar’s Office
- Treasury Office

#### 2. **When will my transfer credentials package be released?**

Your transfer credentials package will only be prepared **after all offices have signed** your clearance. If you do not have any pending obligations, your transfer credentials will be released after 6-7 weeks.

#### 3. **What if I haven’t submitted my admission documents yet?**

If you haven’t submitted the **complete physical copies** of your admission requirements, your clearance might be delayed. Submit them as part of your clearance process.

#### 4. **What happens to my INC grades?**

- If you **didn’t request completion** of your INC grade during the term, it will be marked as **5.00**.
- If you **did request completion**, your grade will be updated to **3.00** after one term.

#### 5. **Can I get clearance if I have unpaid balances?**

No. If you have **outstanding tuition or laptop account balances**, your clearance will be **on hold**. Please settle all payments first.

## Integrative Courses for Year 3 and 4 Students – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37500161123597-Integrative-Courses-for-Year-3-and-4-Students

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37500161123597-Integrative-Courses-for-Year-3-and-4-Students#main-content)

1. [_What Are Integrative Courses?_](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37500161123597-Integrative-Courses-for-Year-3-and-4-Students#h_01JZRY9RYYRW9EVFG10YC2TWXY)

2. [_Project Timeline & Milestones_](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37500161123597-Integrative-Courses-for-Year-3-and-4-Students#h_01JY6885KEV2DMK08ZZ0PJ6Q6T)
3. [_Integrative Courses by Program_](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37500161123597-Integrative-Courses-for-Year-3-and-4-Students#h_01JY6885KMPQN59DEB8Y6C2RST)
4. [_Integrative Fee_](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37500161123597-Integrative-Courses-for-Year-3-and-4-Students#h_01JY6885KXR9F0GK0FCFEJGSGF)
5. [_Re-Defense Policy and Fee_](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37500161123597-Integrative-Courses-for-Year-3-and-4-Students#h_01JZQ9JWWN7RMAS7A4GY45C0AS)

### What Are Integrative Courses?

Integrative Courses are **culminating, performance-based subjects** you complete in **Year 3 and Year 4**. They consolidate everything you’ve learned into a major project that tackles real-world problems in society, industry, or the environment.

They are designed to:

|     |     |
| --- | --- |
| **Purpose** | **What It Means for You** |
| **Assess Program Outcomes** | MMDC verify that graduates are academically knowledgeable, professionally competent, and ethically responsible. |
| **Bridge Classroom & Industry** | You apply theories and methods to projects, ensuring industry relevance and up-to-date practice. |

Typical activities include written proposals, problem justifications, manuscript preparation, and **oral defenses** before a  panel.

### Project Timeline & Milestones

The schedule below shows the **typical weeks** during the term when key milestones are expected. Oral defenses are **generally scheduled** within these timeframes and may vary slightly depending on your program or mentor’s timeline.

|     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Week** | **Milestone** | **What Happens** |
| **5–8** | Proposal/ Problem Justification & Oral Defense | Present your concept, get feedback, refine scope. |
| **10–12** | Final Oral Defense | Defend the near-final output, address panel comments. |
| **12** | Final Manuscript Submission | Submit polished work for final grading and archive. |

### Integrative Courses by Program

#### Bachelor of Arts in Marketing

|     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Course Code** | **Course Title** | **General Description** |
| **MO-MKT2002** | Thesis / Feasibility Study | Generally, a scholarly thesis or a business feasibility plan. You independently research a business-related problem or opportunity, prove its technical and financial viability, and present a professional-grade proposal that could attract investors or stakeholders. |

_Note: For Term 3-SY24-25, the focus is on building a business feasibility plan._

#### Bachelor of Science in Information Technology

|     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Course Code** | **Course Title** | **General Description** |
| **MO-IT200D1** | Capstone Project 1 | First phase of a multi-term capstone. Conduct background analysis, define requirements, and produce a detailed project proposal that solves a specific business or scientific problem. |
| **MO-IT200D2** | Capstone Project 2 | Implementation and evaluation phase. Develop the product or system, test it, and document results. Culminates in a final defense and manuscript. |

**Capstone Projects** emphasize applied problem-solving. Although they may not introduce entirely new research, they require rigorous analysis and a tangible solution that addresses an identified need.

### Integrative Fee

- **Amount:** **₱1,600** per **studen** t per **integrative course** per **term**
- **Billing:** Appears as a separate line item on your Statement of Account; it is **not** part of tuition or miscellaneous fees.

This fee covers for the extra administrative, review, evaluation and defense processes and ensures you receive the guidance, tools, and evaluation needed to produce high-quality integrative outputs.

For guidance on how to pay for the integrative fee, please refer to the [How to Pay for Processing Fees for Other Charges, Requests and Services Help Guide](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/34560176570637)

* * *

### Re-Defense Policy and Fee

If the event that a group will be required to undergo a re-defense after their final defense for their Feasibility Study or Capstone, a **Re-Defense Fee of ₱2,200** will apply. This fee must be **shared and settled by the group** and **paid in full before the scheduled re-defense**.

Re-defense is typically due to significant gaps in the project’s quality, completeness, or alignment with course outcomes. The fee helps cover additional administrative, review, and panel evaluation efforts involved in re-assessing your work.

We strongly encourage all groups to prepare thoroughly, plan ahead, collaborate effectively, and take feedback seriously throughout the process. Submitting a strong proposal, consulting regularly with your mentor, and rehearsing your defense can go a long way in helping you pass the first time—saving you time, effort, and added costs.

You've got this—prepare well, trust your process, and aim to finish strong!

We’re here to support you as you take these final steps toward graduation. Good luck with your Integrative Course journey!

## How to Pay via the GGives Study Now Pay Later Program – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37898480653453-How-to-Pay-via-the-GGives-Study-Now-Pay-Later-Program

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37898480653453-How-to-Pay-via-the-GGives-Study-Now-Pay-Later-Program#main-content)

At MMDC, we understand that finances can be a challenge—especially for working students and their families. To help ease the burden, we’ve partnered with GGives by GCash to offer the **Study Now, Pay Later Program**.

This program allows you to pay for your tuition and school fees upfront and settle the amount in monthly installments over a flexible period of **6 to 15 months**.

### Who Can Avail of This Program?

This loan option is open to:

- New MMDC students
- Currently enrolled students
- Returning students
- Student applicants who are working or supported by working parents or guardians

### How to Apply

Before you can use the GGives SNPL Program to pay for your MMDC tuition and fees, you must first apply and receive approval from GCash and Fuse Lending. Once approved, only then can you activate and proceed with the tuition payment.

1. **Scan the official QR code** to access the GGives application form or you may also access the form via this link: 🔗 [**Application Form**](https://bit.ly/ggivesstudynowpaylater)

[![GGives.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/41802814953613)](https://bit.ly/ggivesstudynowpaylater)

1. **Fill out the form completely and accurately.** You will not be able to edit the form after submission.
2. **Wait for the review.** All applications will be reviewed by GCash and Fuse Lending. Please note that approval is not guaranteed.
3. **Get notified.** You will receive updates through official GCash channels once results are available.
4. **Activate GGives.** If approved, you may activate GGives on the GCash app by tapping **Borrow > GGives**.

### What to Prepare Before Applying

Please have the following information ready:

- Student's year level and course
- Term(s) with outstanding balance
- Total tuition amount to be paid

You will also need to submit the following documents:

- Student’s most recent student ID
- Most recent enrollment form, certificate of matriculation, or statement of account
- Loan applicant’s valid government-issued ID
- Loan applicant’s updated proof of income (issued within the last 3 months; up to 2 documents allowed)
- _(Optional)_ Student’s most recent report card

### How to Pay Your Tuition Using GGives

1. Log in to your **GCash** account.
2. Tap **Bills** and select the **Schools** category.
3. Choose **Mapúa Malayan Digital College** or the school listed in the GGives menu.
4. Fill in the required payment details.
5. Select **GGives** as your payment method.
6. Choose your preferred installment plan.
7. Review and sign the disclosure statement.
8. Your tuition is now paid!

### How to Repay Your GGives Loan

Your repayment will begin exactly **one month after your tuition payment** via GGives.

To learn more about repayment, visit GCash’s official guide:

[How can I pay for my GGives dues?](https://help.gcash.com/hc/en-us/articles/4405187569817-How-can-I-pay-for-my-GGives-dues)

### **Don’t Miss Out!**

This is a pilot run and on a **limited-time offer** until the next update.

## Frustrations, Ideas and Shoutouts – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37869523175053-Frustrations-Ideas-and-Shoutouts

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/37869523175053-Frustrations-Ideas-and-Shoutouts#main-content)

At MMDC, your experience matters. We understand that not everything goes as planned—and sometimes, you just need a place to speak your mind, share an idea, or appreciate someone who made your day a little better.

That’s why we created [**Frustrations, Ideas, and Shoutouts**](https://forms.gle/r9Uh6VFQjg6SPqsZ6)—a space where you can express yourself freely and honestly.

## What Is This For?

This is a simple form where you can:

- 😤 Vent about a frustration (academic, peer-related, or personal)
- 💡 Share an idea or suggestion for how we can make your experience better
- 🙌 Give a shoutout or appreciation to someone who deserves it

You can share anything—from small wins to big feelings. You may choose to submit anonymously or leave your name if you’d like us to follow up.

> This is your space. Whether you're feeling inspired, overwhelmed, or thankful—your voice belongs here.

## What Happens After You Submit?

We review every message submitted with care. Here's how we handle the feedback:

| If You Chose To… | What Happens |
| --- | --- |
| **Stay Anonymous** | Your message is still read and included in our weekly review. No names are shared. |
| **Leave Your Name & Email** | If your message needs follow-up, we’ll reach out to you directly via your email. |
| **Submit a Shoutout** | With your submission, we may include your appreciation post in a **Student Shoutouts board**. |

## The Feedback Loop: How You’ll Hear Back

We believe in **closing the loop** on feedback.

- ✅ If you provided your email and asked for a response, expect an update once your concern has been routed or addressed.
- 📄 If you submitted anonymously, stay tuned to the **monthly “You Spoke, We Heard” bulletin**, where we summarize key themes and share actions being taken—no names, just shared insights.

> This bulletin will also be posted here on the Help Center for full transparency.

## Ready to Share?

Click the link below to submit your entry:

👉 [Submit to Frustrations, Ideas, and Shoutouts GForm](https://forms.gle/xpiryY9bAfHfGv7D8)

## A Note on Respect and Community

We encourage honest expression—but please remember:

- This space is **not for harassment, threats, or personal attacks**.

If you have other questions or concerns, feel free to visit our other help articles in the [**Support Center**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us) or [**raise a ticket here.**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/requests/new)

We're here to support you.

## 📝 MMDC Practicum Guide – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38008357644301--MMDC-Practicum-Guide

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38008357644301--MMDC-Practicum-Guide#main-content)

At MMDC, the Practicum is more than a graduation requirement—it’s a strategic opportunity for **real-world learning, career enhancement, and professional growth**.

Whether you're a fresh graduate, a working student, or a career shifter, the Practicum Program is designed to help you:

- Apply what you've learned in actual industry environments
- Strengthen your professional competencies
- Expand your network and portfolio
- Align your academic work with your career direction

As defined in **CHED Memorandum Order No. 17, s. 2021**, the internship program aims to:

“Provide students with an opportunity to complement their formal learning with practical knowledge, skills, and desirable attitudes, and to gain hands-on experience in a recognized Host Training Establishment (HTE).”

### **🎓 Who is Eligible?**

You may enroll in the Practicum course once you have completed and passed:

- All **major and specialization courses** as indicated in your program’s Curriculum Plan: 🔗 [BA](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/sections/28639222873229-MMDC-s-Business-Administration-Program) & 🔗 [IT](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/sections/28639223603469-MMDC-s-Information-Technology-Program).
- Your **Feasibility Study** (for BSBA students) or **Capstone Courses**(for BSIT students)

### **✅ What to Prepare Before You Begin**

To ensure a smooth practicum experience, complete these steps **beginning the term before your intended Practicum term**:

|     |
| --- |
| #### **1\. Signify your intent and prepare your credentials:**<br>- 🔗 [**Practicum Form 01: Practicum Intent Form**](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1j7SQbSrHM0Kmu96EnLv6ixkU5uOI_-VJOJuPJMl-pAU/edit?gid=181712368#gid=181712368) \- Make a copy of the form, completely fill it out and prepare it for submission to your Program Head.<br>- Updated **curriculum vitae** with a recent photo |
| #### **2\. Secure psychological and medical clearance:**<br>- **Secure a Medical certificate** from a DOH-accredited clinic or hospital<br>  <br>  (both physical and psychological assessments)<br>- Submit the results of the **Medical Assessment/ Medical Certificate** to the Center for Health Services and Wellness (CHSW) and **Psychological Assessments** to the Center for Guidance and Counseling (CGC)<br>**Note**: We will publish a separate article for more information on the process of securing a medical and psychological clearance from MMCL’s CHSW and CGC. <br>**Also,** take advantage of the ongoing APE Services available this month of July. This can serve as your physical assessment. For more information, see  🔗 [Help Article: APE for MMDC Students](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28216296339469)<br>- Additional medical requirements may be required by your preferred HTE |
| #### **3\. Identify preferred HTEs:**<br>- Shortlist **up to three (3) HTEs** of your choice. See the list of MMDC partner HTEs here: 🔗 [MMDC Practicum Partners SY2526](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38033354345229) |
| #### **4\. Prepare for enrollment:**<br>- Officially enroll in the Practicum course. Refer to the term calendar to be informed of the upcoming enrollment dates: 🔗 [Help Article: Term Calendar](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/sections/28318507978637-MMDC-s-Calendar-of-Activities)<br>- Upon enrollment, settle the **OJT Fee**: PHP **4,220**<br>  <br>  This is charged **on top of your usual tuition and miscellaneous fees** and helps cover the administration, coordination, and support of the practicum program.<br>- If you have already identified your preferred HTEs, the Program head and Practicum Coordinator will endorse you and assist in processing your application with your chosen HTE. |
| #### **5\. After enrollment, process your placement with an HTE**<br>- If you have already identified your preferred HTEs, the Program head and Practicum Coordinator will endorse you and assist in processing your application with your chosen HTE. |
| #### **6\. Once accepted by an HTE:**<br>- Submit 🔗 [**Practicum Form 02: Confirmation and Acceptance**](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1Yzd7LENOGSsu8ojQyxodNUqcx6R7S8xx8LLZQq6R1V0/copy)<br>- Sign the **Training Plan** issued by your Practicum Advisor<br>- Notarize 🔗 [**Practicum Form 00: Liability Waiver**](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/16Uu-7q-CLHLkU3fCK2WcpSJ5VlTrQE3JIik9812Xqik/copy)<br>- Submit any remaining required documents |

### **🗂 Explore MMDC’s Employer Partners**

MMDC has a network of reputable Host Training Establishments (HTEs) that welcome students from various backgrounds, including working professionals.

- Refer to the list of partner HTEs:  🔗 [MMDC Practicum Partners SY2526](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38033354345229)
- Review your options and begin shortlisting based on your interests, preference, location, and goals

💡 _Already working? You may propose your current employer as your HTE—provided that the nominated company meets CHED’s standards for reputable training establishments, complies fully with MMCL’s accreditation procedures, and aligns with the core objectives of the internship program as defined in CHED CMO No. 17 and MMDC’s Practicum Guidelines. Any deviation from these may compromise the approval of the partnership._

### **⏱ Required Hours**

| **Program** | **Hours Required** | **Notes** |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **BSBA** | 600 hours | BSBA students are required to complete a total of **600 hours** to fulfill their Practicum. While some Host Training Establishments (HTEs) can accommodate the full 600 hours, others may offer up to 480 hours of actual industry engagement. In such cases, the remaining 120 hours will be completed through asynchronous professional readiness courses via Coursera, facilitated by MMDC. |
| **BSIT** | 486 hours | BSIT students must complete a total of **486 hours** to satisfy their Practicum requirement. These hours may be distributed according to the agreement with the Host Training Establishment and the structure set by MMDC. |

## **❓ Frequently Asked Questions (FAQs)**

**Can I take other courses while doing Practicum?**

Yes. You may take up to **6 additional units**, with approval from your Program Head, to ensure your academic load stays manageable.

\\_\\_\\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_

**What if I don’t finish my internship?**

You must notify your Program Coordinator and submit a letter of intent at least **3 working days** before your last day.

\\_\\_\\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_

**Will internships be conducted online or onsite?**

Onsite, online, and hybrid **internships** are available. MMDC has a mix of HTEs offering flexible modalities. For **working students**, remote and asynchronous setups are available through select partner companies.

\\_\\_\\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_

**Can I propose my own Host Training Establishment (HTE)?**

Yes—as long as it meets CHED’s standards, passes MMDC’s accreditation process, and supports your learning objectives. This includes your current employer if relevant to your field of study.

Please take into account that the HTE accreditation process typically runs for at least a month before a partnership and agreements are established between MMCL/MMDC and the employer partner.

\\_\\_\\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_

**Can my current job count as my internship?**

If your current job is **directly aligned** with your MMDC program, it **may be considered** for practicum credit. You must:

- Be **actively performing tasks** relevant to your field of study. You may refer to the training plan of your specialization which will be published by the Program Heads.
- Submit proof of work scope and responsibilities
- Go through the same endorsement and documentation process as regular HTEs
- The HTE to go through the accreditation process and supportive of the practicum objectives

**Final approval will depend on CHED and MMDC guidelines and the fulfillment of the accreditation process.**

\\_\\_\\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_

**I’ve been employed doing relevant work for years—do I still need to do an internship?**

If you have already been employed in work that is directly aligned with your MMDC program, you may qualify for the **Portfolio Track** instead of completing a traditional internship. This track is designed for students who have already demonstrated, through years of experience, the foundational knowledge and skills that the practicum aims to develop. You must:

- Be actively performing or have performed tasks relevant to your field of study, as reflected in the training plan per specialization to be published by the Program Heads

- Submit proof of your work scope and responsibilities

- Provide evidence of work and experience verified by an authority in your workplace, showing that you have already gained the essential practicum competencies


The Portfolio Track recognizes your prior professional experience and allows you to meet the practicum requirement by showing that you have already achieved the outcomes expected from internship training.

\\_\\_\\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_

**Can I count unrelated work experience as my internship?**

No. If your job is **not related** to your program specialization, it **cannot be credited** as your practicum. You must still complete a qualifying internship aligned with your academic track.

\\_\\_\\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_

**Can I do an internship in advance and have it credited later?**

MMDC only credits internships done **within the approved Practicum term** and under an official enrollment. Voluntary or early internships done outside the required term are **not credited retroactively** unless pre-approved and officially processed through MMDC.

\\_\\_\\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_

**How will the internship work if I am currently based outside the Philippines?**

If you're currently based abroad, you can still complete your Practicum remotely. MMDC works with partner HTEs that offer **fully online internships**, making it possible for students outside the Philippines to participate without needing to report onsite.

When selecting or proposing an HTE, ensure that:

- The internship can be done **completely online**
- The company can provide **regular supervision and feedback**
- You can complete all **MMDC documentation, reporting and evaluation requirements**
- The HTE aligns with **CHED and MMDC standards**

Internship is a required academic component and must be completed during your enrolled Practicum term, regardless of your location.

## Additional MMDC Practicum Partners for BA Students – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38033354345229-Additional-MMDC-Practicum-Partners-for-BA-Students

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38033354345229-Additional-MMDC-Practicum-Partners-for-BA-Students#main-content)

## **Overview**

This article introduces the **additional practicum partner organizations** available for students under the **BSBA** **specializations** **(HRM, MM, OM)** **at Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC) for Term 2 of School Year 2025-2026**.

It lists each partner, their modality (remote / onsite / hybrid), available slots, and the application process. Use this guide to explore options, prepare your practicum application, and select a partner that supports your learning goals, schedule, and preferred working environment.

This list will be updated regularly as we gain more employer partners.

## Medical and Psychological Clearance for Practicum – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38461453698957-Medical-and-Psychological-Clearance-for-Practicum

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38461453698957-Medical-and-Psychological-Clearance-for-Practicum#main-content)

As part of the pre-practicum requirements, students must secure a certification to be in **good physical and emotional/ psychological health** before they are endorsed for internship. This is to ensure that all students are physically fit to take on real-world responsibilities in their Host Training Establishments (HTEs), and are emotionally prepared to navigate workplace dynamics.

This requirement aligns with **CHED Memorandum Order No. 104, s. 2017**, which mandates that student interns undergo both a physical and psychological examination conducted or certified by a DOH-accredited clinic or hospital.

### **Required Health Clearances**

The following health assessments must be completed before enrollment in the Practicum course:

**1\. Physical Examination**

- Student is encouraged to have this done by their preferred laboratory/ diagnostic center. The examination must be conducted or certified by a DOH-accredited clinic or hospital.
- This may also be completed through MMDC’s Annual Physical Exam (APE) program. This service is part of the student’s health benefit and comes at no additional cost. For more information, please see the **help article:** 🔗 [Annual Physical Exam (APE) for MMDC Students](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/28216296339469-Annual-Physical-Exam-APE-for-MMDC-Students). This service is available every July to August of the year.
- Physical Evaluations are only valid for 6 months from the date of assessment.

**2\. Psychological Assessment**

- Must also be conducted or certified by a qualified psychological service provider
- The cost of this assessment is to be shouldered by the student
- The student may choose a preferred provider that meets MMDC guidelines
- Psychological Evaluations are only valid for 6 months from the date of assessment.

### **Requesting a Referral Form**

Students may request a referral form to present to a clinic or psychological center, if needed, for the purpose of obtaining the required physical or psychological evaluation..

- Request may be made through this **GForm**: 🔗 [MMDC \| Request for Referral Form (Practicum Medical or Psychological Assessment)](https://forms.gle/vAz4g3hDMDbBntX77)
- Specify whether the referral is for:
  - Physical exam (Center for Health Services and Wellness - CHSW)
  - Psychological assessment (Center for Guidance and Counseling - CGC)
- Please allow 1-2 business days after the request is made for the referral form to be completed and sent back to your email address.

The student may use and present the referral form at a preferred provider.

### **Submitting Results for Endorsement (Pre-Internship)**

Once the exams are completed, the results must be submitted along with the 🔗 [Practicum Form 01: Practicum Intent Form](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1cnaB4SKRQ52bSYVbb6F_yc4FkEzgkmOxSMU58iMF60w/copy) as follows:

| **Requirement** | **Submit To** | **Submission Method** | **What Happens Next:** |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Physical Exam Results | CHSW | Via **email** to: [MCLCHSW@mcl.edu.ph](mailto:MCLCHSW@mcl.edu.ph)<br>Attachments: (1) Medical Results & Supporting documents, if any, (2) Practicum Intent Form 01 | CHSW reviews and returns signed Form 01 within 1-3 business days |
| Psychological Assessment | CGC | via **GForm** upload: 🔗 [GForm: MMDC \| Psychological Clearance for Practicum](https://forms.gle/QiA2AL8e1pnVjoST8)<br>**Attachments:** (1) Psychological Assessment Results & Supporting documents, if any, (2) Practicum Intent Form 01<br>**Note:** Depending on the results of the psychological evaluation, the CGC may require an interview with the student before official endorsement. The CGC will reach out to the student directly via their learner email and set an appointment for interview. | CGC evaluates and returns signed Form 01 within 1-3 business days |

**Additional Notes:**

1. **Please make sure that both CHSW and CGC sign on the same copy of your Practicum Intent Form.**

To do this, submit your results **one after the other**—not at the same time—to ensure that each office can review and signify their endorsement (signature) on the same document.
2. If the results indicate medical or psychological conditions that require clarification, the student may submit additional documentation confirming fitness to engage in practicum.
3. Physical and Psychological Evaluations are only valid for 6 months.
4. In cases where there are observed mental health issues or challenges reflected in the results of the psychological evaluation of the student, a psychological interview with the CGC will be conducted virtually with the concerned student before issuing endorsement.

### **Reminders:**

- All health documents must be submitted, clearance and endorsement obtained before the start of practicum.
- Only students with endorsed Practicum Intent Forms from both CHSW and CGC will be cleared for practicum placement.
- Upon completion of endorsement from CHSW and CGC, the student may proceed with the submission of their Practicum Intent Forms to their Program Heads or Practicum Coordinators.

### **Suggested Psychological Centers**

The following are recommended psychological service providers compiled by MMCL’s Center for Guidance and Counseling (CGC). These clinics are known to offer psychological assessments suitable for internship clearance.

**Note:** This is not an official or exclusive list. Students may also choose to undergo their psychological assessment at any DOH-accredited clinic or hospital that offers psychological evaluation services.

In most cases, the clinics listed below do not require a referral letter, but students are encouraged to check with the provider directly for any requirements.

1. **A-max Psychological Services**

Unit A5, Ozzie Place Building, Block 1, Lot 19, Sitio Mandaluyong, Barangay Biclatan, General Trias Cavite
2. **Neuro Psychological Testing Center (Online Testing)**

Brgy. Batasan Hills, Quezon City 09617838287 [exam@neuropsychologicaltesting.center](mailto:exam@neuropsychologicaltesting.center)
3. **Unciano Colleges & Gen. Hospital, Inc. (Online Testing)**

Circumferential Road, Antipolo City, Philippines Telephone Nos (02) 6507096; 02 6970170; 09052845890; 09435520907; telefax 6972447

Facebook: [https://m.facebook.com/Psychological-Test-Nueropsychological-Assessment-Services-101737958626270/?\_rdr](https://m.facebook.com/Psychological-Test-Nueropsychological-Assessment-Services-101737958626270/?_rdr)

E-mail: [sbehavioralhealthclinic@gmail.com](mailto:sbehavioralhealthclinic@gmail.com)

## Petition to Open a Petition/ Special Class – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38541627793421-Petition-to-Open-a-Petition-Special-Class

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38541627793421-Petition-to-Open-a-Petition-Special-Class#main-content)

In certain cases, students may request the opening of a **Special Class** to help ensure timely academic progression. A special class refers to a course that is not offered during the current term, either because it is not a regular offering, seasonal, phased out, or has been abolished due to low enrollment (i.e., the number of students falls below the minimum required).

Special Classes may be requested when the following academic circumstances apply:

- The student will be further delayed due to phased out courses or seasonally offered courses, especially for the BSBA program.
- The student is in their penultimate term or is a candidate for graduation

A request may only proceed if:

1. A formal petition is submitted by the student,
2. An eligible faculty member is available to handle the course, and
3. MMDC’s online platforms and resources can support the course delivery.

**Note:** Integrative courses are not eligible for offering as special or petition classes.

## **How to Submit a Petition for a Special Class**

### **Step 1: Submit a Petition**

1. **Download and fill out the form:** 🔗 [Petition to Open a Special Class (PDF)](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1IoQrkz2_USzSaeNQoBBcDFI54AkTBEXf/view?usp=sharing)    1. The PDF petition form must include your signature and your parent’s/guardian’s consent (if applicable), indicating agreement to the terms and conditions for enrolling in a petition/ special class.
2. **Submit the completed petition form via the request submission GForm:** 🔗 [Submission of the Petition to Open a Special Class (GForm).](https://forms.gle/S7ffLGL5SUfZ5Vks8)
3. **Attend academic advising, if required:**

The Program Head may call for an advising session before deciding. Attendance is mandatory.

### **Step 2: Wait for Evaluation and Approval**

- The petition will be reviewed by the **Program Head.**
- You will receive an **email notification** regarding the outcome of your petition as well as the estimated cost of the course, which is based on the number of students who submitted a request for the said petition course. This information should help the student decide on whether they will proceed their enrollment to the petition course, or not.

### **Step 3: Enrollment Finalization of Approved Petition Course**

After receiving the email notification of the Approved Petition Courses to be offered for the term and after being informed of the estimated cost of the petition course, the student needs to signify their comitment to proceed with enrollment by filling out the  🔗 [**Enrollment Finalization for Approved Petitioned Special Courses T3-SY2526**](https://forms.gle/cv7XJGUeb1gf8xP58)

1. **Fill out the** 🔗 [**Enrollment Finalization for Approved Petitioned Special Courses T3-SY2526**](https://forms.gle/cv7XJGUeb1gf8xP58) **completely.**
2. **Signify agreement and commitment to the Terms and Conditions for enrolling to a Petition Course**
3. Once finalization is received, the student will automatically be manually enrolled by the **Enrollment Officer** and billed accordingly.

Note: You may refer to this help article for the term to term listing of approved petition courses: [**Approved Petition/ Special Classes and Next Steps (T3-SY25-26)**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/44691384944141)

* * *

## **Assessment of Fees for Petition/ Special Courses:**

If approved, fees will be assessed based on the number of students enrolled in the class. The formula for computation is as follows:

- **For Special Classes with 1-7 students:**  - Special Class **FEE PER STUDENT** = \[Tuition and Laboratory Fee per unit\* x No. of units of the course x 8\*\*\] ÷ No. of students

Sample Computation: ![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/39747720407565)

- For Special Classes with **8-14 students**:  - Special Class **FEE PER STUDENT** = \[Tuition and Laboratory Fee per unit\* x no. of units of the course x 15\*\*\] / no. of students

Sample Computation: ![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/39747677722637)

\\* The per-unit cost is subject to the approved rate per school year and may be adjusted accordingly in succeeding academic years. Subsequent enrollments will follow the prevailing per-unit rate as approved for that school year. This is also dependent on the payment scheme preferred by the student.

\\*\\* 8 and 15 are standard formula multiplier depending on the number of students enrolled to the petition course.

* * *

## **Important Terms and Guidelines**

- **Submission Deadline:**

All petitions must be submitted **on or before the deadline set by the Registrar’s Office**. Late requests will not be considered. Please refer to the term calendar.
- **No Enrollment Beyond Schedule:**

Students who do not proceed with enrollment within the approved period **will not be allowed to enroll later**.
- **Disciplinary Action for Non-Compliance:**

Students who fail to enroll after petition approval will be subject to **disciplinary action** as initiated by the Enrollment Officer under the authority of the Registrar’s Office.
- **No Revisions Allowed:**

Once enrolled, **revisions or changes** to the special class petition or enrollment will **not be accommodated**.
- **Exclusions:**

**Integrative courses cannot be petitioned** as special classes.

## BA Training Plan for Practicum – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38602815200013-BA-Training-Plan-for-Practicum

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38602815200013-BA-Training-Plan-for-Practicum#main-content)

When you begin your practicum, the tasks and responsibilities you are assigned at your Host Training Establishment (HTE) must align with the official **Training Plan** of your program. This plan outlines the expected learning objectives and activities for your internship and ensures that your work contributes meaningfully to your academic and professional development.

Under **CHED Memorandum Order No. 104, s. 2017**, all internships must have clearly defined and structured learning outcomes that are relevant to your degree program. These are documented in the HTE's Training Plan, which is reviewed and approved as part of the accreditation process.

**Important:**

When proposing an HTE or selecting your preferred company for internship, you must **verify that the internship role or scope of work they are offering aligns with the Training Plan** for your program. Work that is purely clerical, unrelated to your field, or does not meet the learning outcomes will not be approved.

If the tasks assigned to you during the internship do not match the approved Training Plan, inform your **Practicum Advisor** immediately so appropriate adjustments can be made.

You can review the standard Training Plans below:

1. **Marketing Management Internship Tasks**
2. **Operations Management Internship Tasks**
3. **Human Resource Management Internship Tasks**

| ### **Marketing Management Internship Tasks** |
| --- |
| **Marketing Project Documentation and Reporting**<br>- Draft and organize project documents such as campaign briefs, timelines, and progress reports<br>- Maintain and update marketing project trackers and shared documentation systems<br>- Support project planning by aligning documentation with campaign goals and milestones<br>- Ensure clarity, accuracy, and consistency across project reports and deliverables<br>  <br>**Market Research and Analysis**<br>- Conduct competitor analysis and track industry trends relevant to the company<br>- Gather data on audience behavior, preferences, and emerging marketing strategies<br>- Support content direction by researching effective formats and messages<br>- Create customer personas and translate insights into strategic recommendations<br>- Identify business owners, collaborators, or brands for potential tie-ups<br>  <br>**Social Media and Content Management**<br>- Manage and schedule posts on Facebook, Instagram, ## BSIT Curriculum Plan - SY2025-2026 – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38606013434381-BSIT-Curriculum-Plan-SY2025-2026

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38606013434381-BSIT-Curriculum-Plan-SY2025-2026#main-content)

MMDC offers a flexible, industry-aligned **Bachelor of Science in Information Technology (BSIT)** program taught through the **Projects, Problems, and Cases (PPC)** learning model. This hands‑on, real-world approach enables you to work on meaningful assignments and practical scenarios that reflect the challenges you’ll face in the workplace.

The four-year program is divided into two main paths:

- **Development‑focused** specializations:
  - **Software Development** – Master programming languages like Java, Python, JavaScript, and Ruby, along with software design, testing, debugging, and deployment.

  - **Network & Cybersecurity** – Learn network standards, cybersecurity protocols, system security frameworks, and prepare for certification like CCNA
- **Business‑focused** specializations:
  - **Data Analytics** – Learn how to clean, analyze, and visualize data using tools to build reports and dashboards for business insights (courses include Machine Learning, Data Mining, etc.).

  - **Marketing Technology** – Explore tech-driven marketing tools and analytics platforms to optimize brand engagement and campaigns.

  - **Entrepreneurship Technology** – Combine e‑commerce platforms, SaaS tools, and tech strategies to launch and grow businesses.

The Curriculum Plans linked below enumerates the sequence of courses and is structured to include prerequisites and co-requisites, ensuring that you follow the optimal progression toward your specialization. The plan also highlights how term loads align with MMDC’s trimester model and maximum unit limits per term under academic policies

Additionally, the curriculum plan—term by term—helps you visualize your path to graduation, from general IT foundations to specialization courses, culminating in a capstone project and internship experience.

1. **BSIT major in Software Development**



_If you dream of building your own app, our Software Development major will be perfect  for you. Once you graduate, you’ll be proficient in different programming languages and software development, testing, debugging, and software deployment._



[_![Curriculum Plan.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/38605982976781)_](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1xb10GA4OeJ3_OVGIzGcZoNniOUKdhwioyho1pUQArzA/edit?gid=934151035#gid=934151035)

2. **BSIT major in Network and Cybersecurity**

_Imagine yourself being a company’s first line of defense in tech. Our Network & Cybersecurity specialization provides students with an in-depth understanding and skills on cyber security standards, protocols, and frameworks. Learn the technical skills needed to support network operations administration, and monitoring and maintenance of cybersecurity systems and applications._



[_![Curriculum Plan.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/38605982976781)_](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1xb10GA4OeJ3_OVGIzGcZoNniOUKdhwioyho1pUQArzA/edit?gid=2068093852#gid=2068093852)

3. **BSIT major in Data Analytics**



_Are you detail-oriented with a passion for tech, numbers, and data? Then, specialize in Data Analytics! Develop skills in basic data cleaning and transformation, and data analysis that are necessary in supporting business and product decisions. Graduates from this specialization will be trained in using development tools to generate reports, dashboards, and analytical solutions, according to business rules and specifications._





[_![Curriculum Plan.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/38605982976781)_](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1xb10GA4OeJ3_OVGIzGcZoNniOUKdhwioyho1pUQArzA/edit?gid=1470715077#gid=1470715077)

4. **BSIT major in Marketing Technology**


_In Marketing Technology, you'll harness the power of cutting-edge tools to supercharge your marketing efforts. From analytics to targeted advertising, to the latest online platforms, you'll learn how to reach your audience effectively. Elevate your brand, and gain the edge you need to succeed in today's competitive landscape. Graduating from this program will possibly open more senior positions for you in various industries._

[_![Curriculum Plan.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/38605982976781)_](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1xb10GA4OeJ3_OVGIzGcZoNniOUKdhwioyho1pUQArzA/edit?gid=700987941#gid=700987941)

**5.****BSIT major in Entrepreneurship Technology**

_In Entrepreneurship Technology, you'll learn how to leverage the most common technology platforms entrepreneurs use to drive success. Dive into key tools for e-commerce and marketing, and explore the principles related to the entrepreneurial process, particularly with the field of IT. If you already own a business or are thinking of starting one, you can reach next level success once you graduate with this specialization._

[_![Curriculum Plan.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/38605982976781)_](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1xb10GA4OeJ3_OVGIzGcZoNniOUKdhwioyho1pUQArzA/edit?gid=1102328845#gid=1102328845)

## HTE Accreditation & MOA Process for Practicum – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38665476654605-HTE-Accreditation-MOA-Process-for-Practicum

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38665476654605-HTE-Accreditation-MOA-Process-for-Practicum#main-content)

As part of your practicum requirements at MMDC, you must be placed in a **Host Training Establishment (HTE)**—a company or organization where you’ll undergo supervised, real-world training related to your degree program.

Before your practicum can begin, MMDC must first **accredit your proposed HTE** and establish a **Memorandum of Agreement (MOA)** with them. This process is required by the Commission on Higher Education (CHED) to ensure the **safety, relevance, and academic integrity of your internship experience.**

**Table of Contents:**

1. [Why Does the HTE Need to be Accredited?](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38665476654605-HTE-Accreditation-MOA-Process-for-Practicum#h_01K247BFMGDEATRX3G4XDS8TCD)
2. [Who Is Involved in the Accreditation Process?](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38665476654605-HTE-Accreditation-MOA-Process-for-Practicum#h_01K247BFMNQWK8XAVENK1QBK8A)
3. [Requirements for an HTE to be Accredited](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38665476654605-HTE-Accreditation-MOA-Process-for-Practicum#h_01K247BFNBFFESAAXCDHRCT5XH)
4. [MMDC Accreditation and MOA Process](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38665476654605-HTE-Accreditation-MOA-Process-for-Practicum#h_01K247BFNGZK1WD3D9S9QZE85W)

### **Why Does the HTE Need to Be Accredited?**

CHED requires that all HTEs be evaluated and approved by the Higher Education Institution (HEI), in this case MMDC/MMCL, through a formal accreditation process and a signed MOA.

This ensures that:

- The HTE is legally registered and reputable
- The training aligns with the learning outcomes of your program
- The HTE can provide a safe and structured learning environment
- Clear roles and responsibilities are defined for all parties
- Student rights, data privacy, and safety protocols are upheld

These are mandated under **CHED Memorandum Order (CMO) No. 104, s. 2017**, which provides the national guidelines for **Student Internship Programs in the Philippines (SIPP)** across all degree programs with practicum components.

### **Who Is Involved in the Accreditation Process?**

For HTE’s preferred by students which are not yet part of the current line up of partners of MMDC, the accreditation process is initiated

| **Party** | **Responsibilities** |
| --- | --- |
| **Student** | Proposes the HTE, secures required documents, and submits for review and approval. |
| **Program Head (PH)** | Reviews the HTE proposal and documents submitted by the student. Endorses the request to the Career Development Office (CDO). |
| **MMDC’s Career Development Office (CDO)** | Verifies completeness and compliance of submissions and facilitates the accreditation process together with the OSPAGE. |
| **MMCL’s OSPAGE (Office for Strategic Partnerships and Global Engagement)** | Facilitates official HTE coordinations and MOA finalization. |
| **HTE (Host Training Establishment)** | Submits necessary accreditation documents, agrees to train students under specified conditions, and signs the MOA. |
| **Higher Education Institution (HEI): MMDC under MMCL** | Maintains official HTE registry, ensures CHED compliance, and oversees the execution of the MOA. |

### **Requirements for an HTE to be Accredited:**

Under CHED CMO No. 104, the following are required before any internship can proceed:

- **Valid SEC or DTI Registration** and **Business Permit** of the HTE
- Logo
- Company Profile
  - Agreement or Letter of Intent to signify HTEs interest to host interns from MMDC

It is also important that the HTE agrees to:

- Assign interns to tasks that align with the program’s **internship/training plan** relevant to the student’s field
- **Nominate a designated supervisor or mentor** for the student
- **Promotes a safe and ethical work environment**
- Enter into a **MOA** between the **HEI** and the **HTE**
- Complies with **labor standards, data privacy laws,** and **safety protocols**

The proposed HTE of the student must also first be presented to the Program Head or Practicum Coordinator for assessment and approval.

### **MMDC HTE Accreditation and MOA Process**

This process may be initiated as early as one full term (3 months) before your intended practicum term.

1. **Secure your proposed HTE's documents:**   - Business Permit or SEC/DTI Registration
   - Company Profile
   - Company Logo
   - Letter of Intent addressed to MMDC stating the company’s willingness to serve as an HTE
     - Mr. James Ronald O. Mesina

       Assistant Vice President, **Office Of External Relations and Global Linkages** AND Ms. Pearl Stephanie DL. Ulep

       Director, **Office for Strategic Partnerships and Global Engagement**
   - |     |
     | --- |
     | ### **📌 Note:**<br>**Requesting a Letter of Intent (LOI) for Your HTE Application**<br>     - Some Host Training Establishments (HTEs) prefer a **Letter of Intent (LOI)** from MMDC before they accept your practicum application.<br>       <br>       If the HTE you are applying to requests an LOI, you may **request one from MMDC** by sending an email to **cdo@mmdc.mcl.edu.ph**. Please include the following details in your email so the Career Development Officer can prepare the letter correctly:<br>       - **Name of the company / HTE**<br>         <br>       - **Name of the contact person**, if available<br>         <br>       - **Designation or department of the contact person**, if available<br>         <br>       - **Email address** or official contact information of the recipient, if available<br>         <br>       - You may also provide a link to their online website or other available online pages.<br>Our Career Development Officer will prepare the LOI and send it to you, which you can then forward to the HTE as part of your application. |

**2\. It is recommended that the student verifies if they may be given an internship scope that aligns with their program's training plan.**

- See training plans:

🔗 [BA Training Plan for Practicum](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38602815200013)

🔗 [IT Training Plan for Practicum](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/40345072724749)


**3\. Upload all documents to your Google Drive. Make sure the sharing settings allow anyone with the link to view.**

**4\. Submit the link via the official Google Form** provided. See GForm: 🔗 [https://forms.gle/rFgVwDb1dyHJzwW39](https://forms.gle/rFgVwDb1dyHJzwW39)

**5\. Program Head reviews and endorses your proposal to the Career Development Office (CDO)**.

**6\. CDO, together with the OSPAGE processes the accreditation and MOA signing with the nominated HTE**.

7\. Once done, **you will be notified once your HTE is accredited and ready for deployment.**

Additional Reminders

- The internship proper may not commence until the HTE is officially accredited and a MOA is signed.
- Only complete submissions will be processed. Missing or invalid documents will delay approval.
- The MOA is a formal requirement and must be in place before any internship service is rendered.
- You are encouraged to start the process early to avoid delays in your practicum schedule.

If you have further questions, please contact your Program Head or the Career Development Office via cdo@mmdc.mcl.edu.ph.

## Coursera - Student Guides – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38905579928077-Coursera-Student-Guides

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38905579928077-Coursera-Student-Guides#main-content)

**Welcome to Coursera at MMDC**

Starting Term 1 of School Year 2025–2026, MMDC will be introducing **Coursera** as the Learning Management System (LMS) for selected courses. Coursera is a trusted global platform that partners with top universities and organizations to provide high-quality online learning experiences.

If you are enrolled in any of the following courses that will use Coursera this term, you will access your classes, lectures, and learning materials directly through the Coursera platform.

- Language and Communication
- College Logic and Math
- Philippine Popular Culture
- Understanding the Self
- The Contemporary World
- PE1

**To help you get started, we’ve prepared a step-by-step guide:**

_(Note: Please use your MMDC email account to be able to access the guides.)_

👉 [Download the Coursera Student Guide for Freshies](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1QU0MO2mV2kCfLFJclGl3P8y9AyvBD7HX/view)

👉 [Download the Coursera Student Guide for Re-Enrollees](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1X8UxVV0cejc9jAAE1EOH8RIZyekpNRJJ/view)

## Getting Started with your Coursera Account – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/39089679703565-Getting-Started-with-your-Coursera-Account

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/39089679703565-Getting-Started-with-your-Coursera-Account#main-content)

This help guide contains the following topics:

1. [Joining the Welcome to MMDC! Learning Program](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/39089679703565-Getting-Started-with-your-Coursera-Account#h_01K3J75MCPD43DBRMB4KD5PBTF)
2. [Viewing Your Enrolled Courses in Coursera](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/39089679703565-Getting-Started-with-your-Coursera-Account#h_01K3J1GAN15AS3BF5CC8DCFY44)
3. [Enrolling in a Course](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/39089679703565-Getting-Started-with-your-Coursera-Account#h_01K3J1GAN15AS3BF5CC8DCFY44)
4. [Unenrolling in a Course](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/39089679703565-Getting-Started-with-your-Coursera-Account#h_01K3J28CY2ZJM27FD1X2FY4FKA)
5. [Frequently Asked Questions](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/39089679703565-Getting-Started-with-your-Coursera-Account#h_01K3J635PJ5VJ63115GQ2FFCVR)

## Joining the Welcome to MMDC! Learning Program

1. Within 1-2 business days after receiving your Camu and Google login credentials, you should receive an email from [no-reply@t.mail.coursera.org](mailto:no-reply@t.mail.coursera.org) welcoming you to the Welcome to MMDC! Learning Program.
2. Click **Join now.** You should be redirected to Coursera. ![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/39089679701389)
3. In Coursera, a "Join the learning program" pop-up will appear. Click **Join program**. ![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/39089714030733)
4. After joining the program, you will automatically be moved from the Welcome to MMDC! Learning Program to the program that houses your courses within 5 minutes. You will also be automatically enrolled in your courses for the term.
1. Additionally, you will be automatically enrolled in orientation courses or external courses as part of your learning journey. (e.g., Google Sheets)
5. You may also receive a notification stating that you have been removed from the program. **Please disregard this message**—it is part of the system process. Rest assured, you will still be able to access your courses on Coursera without any issues.

![coursera removed.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/39089714031501)


## Viewing Your Enrolled Courses in Coursera

To view your enrolled courses in Coursera, go to _**My Learning**_ **.** Only the courses listed here are considered part of your official Coursera enrollments. Always check if your enrolled courses in Coursera are aligned with your course load in Camu.

⚠️ **Important Notes**

- If you have courses in **Coursera but not in CAMU**, you will **not earn academic credits** for them.

- If you have courses in **CAMU but are not enrolled in Coursera**, you must enroll in them. Otherwise, you risk incurring a **grade of 5.00 (Failed)** if you are unable to submit the required outputs on both platforms.


![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/39089679702669)

## Enrolling in a Course

In instances where you were not automatically enrolled in your courses, you may enroll in the course manually.

1. Look for the **"Assigned to you"** section in the learning program. ![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/39089714033933)
2. Click the course you're enrolled in. On this page, you will see a preview of the course, including its description, module coverage, and instructor information.
3. Read the content of the page. Then, click **Enroll**. ![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/39089714034061)

## Unenrolling in a Course

If you have accidentally enrolled in a course that you are not supposed to take, you may **unenroll from the course.**

Always refer to your enrolled courses in **Camu**. The courses you see in Coursera should match the courses in your Camu course load. **Note: Only the courses in your Camu course load will be eligible for academic credits.**

1. To check your enrolled courses in Coursera, go to " **My Learning**".

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/39089679702669)

2\. Click the meatball menu "![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/39089714034957)" and click " **Unenroll from Course**".

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/39089679702925)

## Frequently Asked Questions (FAQs)

#### **Question: What should I do if I have not yet received my Coursera login credentials, even if I already have my Camu and Google login credentials?**

**Answer**: You should be able to receive your Coursera invitation within 1-2 business days after receiving your Camu and Google login credentials. If not, try to log in to Coursera via Google Single Sign-On (SSO) or by clicking the " **Continue with Google"** and using your MMDC-issued Learner's Google Email account.

You should be able to click " **Log in with Mapua Malayan Digital College".**![unable to login.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/39089679703053)

However, if you are unable to proceed due to an error or issue, please contact your IAs by [raising a ticket here](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/requests/new).

#### **Question: What if I have Coursera courses but don’t see them in CAMU?**

**Answer**: You will not earn academic credits for courses that appear only in Coursera but not in CAMU.

#### **Question: What if I have CAMU courses that I haven’t enrolled in on Coursera?**

**Answer**: You must also enroll in Coursera for those courses. If not, you risk receiving a **grade of 5.00 (Failed)** because submissions are required on both CAMU and Coursera.

#### **Question: I did not enroll in some of the courses I see in my Coursera, how can I remove them?**

**Answer**: First, check if you are looking at the right section of your Coursera. If this is what you're seeing, you are looking at the Year 1 Course Catalog. This lists **all the available courses for Year 1**, and not necessarily enrolled to you.

![Course Catalog.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/39091831723149)

To check the courses enrolled in your Coursera, click on the **"My Learning"** button.

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/39089679702669)

If the course is in "My Learning", click the meatball menu "![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/39089714034957)" and click " **Unenroll from Course**".
