## Activities and Club Drive - Term 1-SY2526 – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/39426974902029-Activities-and-Club-Drive-Term-1-SY2526

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/39426974902029-Activities-and-Club-Drive-Term-1-SY2526#main-content)

## **Say Yes to What Moves You:**

## **Choose Your Own Adventure, MMDC-style!**

Fresh term, fresh start.

This term, we’re inviting you to **take part** — to engage, to connect, and to get involved in ways that are meaningful to you. We know that you're not just here to get through school. You're here to grow — in your career, in your confidence, in your community.

* * *

We’ve heard you say:

_“If it helps me grow, if it counts as upskilling, if I can put it on my resume, or if I get to work on something meaningful — I’m in.”_

* * *

So we’ve made space for exactly that. Whether you want to lead, support, or simply stay connected — you get to **choose your own path**, at your own pace.

It could be:

- A club you’ve always wanted to join — or start
- A project idea, activity or event you’ve been meaning to launch
- A chance to meet others who just _get it_
- A leadership role that fits your bandwidth and interest

You don’t have to do everything. You just have to **choose what fits you, now** — and we’ll help you take it from there.

This is your adventure, MMDC-style! Whatever it is, **YOU get to choose** — what you do, how far you go, and how you show up.

* * *

### **The 4 Ways to Get Involved**

At MMDC, we understand that life doesn’t pause for school. Many of you are working, caregiving, or managing other responsibilities. That’s why **student engagement at MMDC** is now built with **your time, your goals, and your energy** in mind.

This term, we’re inviting you to **take a step** — just one — toward building something that’s not just for today, but for your future.

We’ve created opportunities that are:

- ✅ **Flexible** – Join for one term or for one activity, no pressure!
- ✅ **Meaningful** – Your time and effort are recognized
- ✅ **Career-relevant** – Add real experience to your resume or portfolio

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/39426974901261)![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/39427094229517)

* * *

### **What’s In It for You?**

**✅ Build your resume –** Titles, badges, and projects you can actually talk about

**✅ Grow your network –** Meet other students across programs and life stages

**✅ Work on what matters to you –** No fluff, just meaningful experiences

**✅ Get recognized –** We track your contributions and recognize your impact

**✅ On your terms –** No year-long commitment. Just 1 term. Or even 1 project.

* * *

### **Ready to Start?**

**Choose your adventure and tell us what role speaks to you.**

👉 **Fill out the Google Form:** [Choose Your Own Adventure, MMDC-Style!](https://forms.gle/wyDURaaYQof7dCyr8)

🗓 **Sign-up deadline:** Please make sure to signify your interest by Monday, September 15, 2025.

**📣 Student Activities and Club Drive - Consultations:**

- If you have questions or just want to chat about your plans,

- let’s meet on **Friday, September 12 at 3pm**

- GMeet Joining Info: https://meet.google.com/udy-ndez-afq


* * *

### **What’s Next**

Thanks in advance for signing up! In the coming days, we’ll get in touch with the next steps for your chosen role — including orientation invites and how to get started.

Get ready to connect, lead, build, or explore — your adventure at MMDC is just beginning.

* * *

## MMDC Student Clubs – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/39572045936909-MMDC-Student-Clubs

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/39572045936909-MMDC-Student-Clubs#main-content)

At MMDC, we believe that college life is more than just academics—it’s also about **building connections, discovering passions, and finding your community**.

**MMDC Clubs are for the students and by the students—they exist to bring your interests and passions to life.** They offer a vibrant and diverse space where you can connect, grow, collaborate and achieve. They’re not handed down from administrators; they’re built by students like you. That means you shape what happens, what projects to launch, and what community to grow. Clubs give you a platform where your voice matters, your creativity is welcomed, and your leadership can shine.

Whether you love writing, music, gaming, design, or guiding your peers, there’s a place for you here. However, if your passion isn’t represented yet, you’re empowered to start a club of your own and bring together others who share your interests. _(See our \[How to Start a Club\] article for details.)_

MMDC currently hosts a growing number of **student-initiated and student-led clubs**. Each one reflects the passions, talents, and creativity of our students, offering diverse opportunities for connection, learning, and self-expression.

### **The Digital Fort**

The official publication and journalism club of MMDC. They deliver current, accurate, and relevant information to students through newsletters, social media, and other media platforms.

### **PlayerOne**

MMDC’s official e-sports club. PlayerOne aims to build a supportive gaming community where students can improve their skills, connect with fellow players, and enjoy game-based activities.

### **Musicalidad De Harmonia**

The official music club of MMDC. It serves as a stage for students to showcase, share and develop their musical talents—whether vocal or instrumental.

### **Disenyo Malaya**

The home for MMDC’s aspiring designers and creatives. Disenyo Malaya is for students who want to explore and express their creativity in visual arts, design, and multimedia—whether as a hobby, a passion, or a potential career path.

### **SIKLAB**

The peer facilitators club of MMDC. Siklab is for students who are passionate about building community, supporting their peers, and creating a safe and inclusive space where everyone feels heard and connected.

### **Hustle & Thrive**

The club for MMDC’s working students. Hustle & Thrive is a supportive space where students balancing work and academics can share experiences, exchange tips, and encourage each other to succeed in both areas of life.

### **Scholars Club**

A community for MMDC scholars to connect, support, and inspire one another. The Scholars Club provides a venue for collaboration, leadership development, and peer mentorship, celebrating academic achievement while creating a strong support network.

* * *

## **Join the Club!**

Joining a club is one of the best ways to make the most out of your college experience. Here, you'll **find your people, pursue your passions, and make your mark**.

When you join, you’ll:

- **Find Friendship & Belonging** – Meet like-minded peers, build valuable friendships, and create your community.

- **Grow Your Skills** – Explore your interests, learn new skills, and gain leadership and organizational experience.

- **Boost Personal Growth** – Strengthen your confidence, creativity, and problem-solving abilities.

- **Gain Career Advantages** – Add leadership roles and accomplishments to your résumé while sharpening teamwork and time management skills.

- **Create Memories** – From projects to events, you’ll collect stories and experiences you’ll carry with you beyond college.


At the same time, clubs thrive on the creativity and commitment of their members—and that includes you. By joining, you’ll have the chance to:

- Take part in events, projects, and activities.

- Share your voice, ideas, and talents.

- Even step up as a leader and help shape the direction of your club.


Whether you’re writing for **The Digital Fort**, planning a tournament with **PlayerOne**, performing with **Musicalidad De Harmonia**, or finding balance with **Hustle & Thrive**, your contributions matter. _You don’t just join a club—you help bring it to life._

_Don’t just study at MMDC—live the experience. Find your community, share your passions, and help shape the vibrant student life that makes MMDC unique._

👉 [Join the Club Now!](https://forms.gle/ky5zhhiVWcdBstM28)

* * *

## **Start Your Own Club**

Don’t see your passion on the list yet and have an idea, interest, or cause you care about, you can start a new club and build a community around it.

From entrepreneurship to fitness, cultural exchange to niche hobbies, your club can become the space where others connect, grow, and share in what inspires you.

👉 Ready to lead the way? Check out our \[How to Start a Club\] article for the easy steps to get started.

## Club Registration & Recognition – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/39646419621645-Club-Registration-Recognition

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/39646419621645-Club-Registration-Recognition#main-content)

Every student brings unique passions, talents, and perspectives. At MMDC, Clubs are where those come together. They exist because students choose to create them, and they thrive because students lead them. Each club becomes a reflection of its members—a space to connect, collaborate, and shape the MMDC experience in ways that matter.

Here, Clubs are not top-down organizations handed-down to students; they are communities built by students themselves. This makes them powerful spaces for self-expression, leadership, and innovation. By joining or founding a club, students take ownership of their college experience, transforming it into something that is not only memorable but also meaningful for their personal growth and future careers.

This help article provides the complete framework for how MMDC clubs are formed, recognized, and sustained. It defines the roles of founders and leaders or officers, outlines the proposal submission and club recognition process, and sets clear guidelines for governance, succession, and accountability. It is both a reference and a guide—for students who want to start something new, for officers who want to lead well, and for members who want to actively contribute to their community.

### **Club Registration Guidelines**

In keeping with the spirit of student-initiated clubs, MMDC recognizes that the best organizations grow out of student passions. If you have an idea, an interest, or a cause you want to share, starting a club is your opportunity to turn that passion into a community.

Clubs begin with students who step forward as founders—those willing to take the lead in shaping a space where others can connect, grow, and create. The guidelines below outline the requirements and processes that founders and or the founding team must follow to transform an idea into a recognized MMDC club.

These standards are not meant to limit creativity, but to ensure that every club:

- Has a strong foundation and committed membership.
- Operates inclusively and responsibly.
- Reflects MMDC’s values of integrity, professionalism, and innovation.

By following these steps, founders can establish clubs that are not only recognized by the institution but also respected, sustainable, and impactful for the whole community.

#### **1\. Role of the Founder or Founding Team**

The process of registering a student club begins with the Founder or its Founding Team. These are the students who:

- Define the purpose and direction of the club.
- Take responsibility for completing the registration requirements - from proposal to recognition, sealing the deal with the conduct of at least 1 meaningful activity during the initial term.
- Serve as the first set of officers during the founding term

To qualify as founders, students must:

- Be enrolled in MMDC during the current term.
- Be in good academic standing with no failing mark. This signifies that the student has the capacity to handle the academics alongside extra-curricular activities.
- Have no active disciplinary cases or disciplinary records.
- Be willing to act as role models who reflect MMDC’s values of professionalism, inclusivity, and innovation.


#### **2\. Minimum Membership Requirement**

- A proposed club must have at least **ten (10) committed members at the time of registration**, **inclusive of the founder or founding team**. This ensures that every club begins with both leadership and a core group of students who are genuinely interested in its purpose.

#### **3\. Defining the Club: The Club Charter**

The **Founder or Founding Team** play the key role in creating a **Club Charter**— a clear and concise document that defines the essence of the club and serves as its long-term guide. This document becomes the club’s **foundational framework**, ensuring continuity and consistency as leadership and membership change over time.

**The Club Charter must include the following elements:**

1. **Club Identity**   - **Name of the Club** (unique, inclusive, and aligned with MMDC values).
   - **Logo** (or initial ideas for the logo).
2. **Purpose & Mission**   - Why the club exists.
   - What it seeks to contribute to MMDC and its members.
3. **Vision**   - What the club aspires to become or achieve in the long run.
   - The “big picture” of the community it wants to create.
4. **Objectives**   - Clear, measurable goals the club will or must pursue each term or year.
   - Examples: host one workshop per term, publish a monthly newsletter, run an annual advocacy campaign, etc.
5. **Core Values & Principles**   - The guiding behaviors and standards that members and leaders are expected to uphold.
   - This must ensure alignment with and uphold the guidelines set by MMDC’s Student Handbook and Code of Conduct.
6. **Governance & Leadership Structure**    - Define officer roles and responsibilities
7. **Membership Guidelines**   - Who can join. Criteria for joining, if any.
   - Expectations for active members (participation, respect, conduct).
8. **Club Activities Framework**   - The types of activities the club will run (events, projects, campaigns, performances, etc.).
   - Minimum expectation: at least **one meaningful activity per term**.

### **Club Leadership Structure**

Student clubs exist to build community and shared interests, but they are also **training grounds for leadership, professional skills, and life after college**. Serving as an officer allows students to practice collaboration, communication, accountability, and project management—skills that go beyond academics and prepare them for future careers.

It is the role of the **Founder or Founding Team** to design the club’s leadership structure as part of the **Club Charter**. Founders may define which roles the club needs, how responsibilities are distributed, and may even create additional positions if necessary.

#### **Guidelines for Designing the Club Leadership Structure**

- The leadership structure is outlined in the club charter, dependent on the need and purpose of the club. eEvery club must have a **minimum of three leadership roles** filled at the time of registration.
- Founders may **choose from the six suggested officer roles below**.
- Clubs may further **define the focus of each role** to fit their unique mission and activities.
- Clubs may also **add new leadership roles** not listed here, if aligned with their needs.

**Suggested Leadership Roles (with Traditional Comparison)**

|     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Traditional Student Role** | **MMDC Club Leaders** | **Primary Responsibilities** |
| President | Chief Executive Officer (CEO) | Provides vision, direction, and overall leadership; represents the club in official functions. |
| Vice President | Chief Operating Officer (COO) | Oversees operations and ensures activities and projects are executed effectively. |
| Secretary | Chief Documentation Officer (CDO) | Maintains records, documentation, minutes, and official communications. |
| Treasurer | Chief Finance Officer (CFO) | Manages finances, prepares budgets, and ensures accountability and transparency of funds. |
| Auditor | Chief Audit Officer (CAO) | Reviews reports and records, ensuring fairness and integrity in operations and finances. |
| Public Relations Officer (PRO) | Chief Communications Officer (CCO) | Leads communications, publicity, promotions, and member engagement. |

### **Club Proposal & Recognition Process**

To be officially recognized, a club must complete the following process:

#### **Step 1: Proposal Submission via Google Form**

The Founder or Founding Team prepares and submits the proposal through the official Club Registration Google Form provided by the Office of Student Affairs. The proposal must include:

- Club Charter: mission, vision, values, objectives, and core framework.
- Minimum Membership List: at least ten (10) committed members, inclusive of the founder or founding team.
- Leadership Structure: at least three (3) leadership roles defined (from the suggested officer roles), with room for expansion as the club grows.
- Gform: [https://forms.gle/fGd1wbHx1YV2V7gq6](https://forms.gle/fGd1wbHx1YV2V7gq6)

**Step 2: Review & Endorsement**

- The Office of Student Affairs screens the submission for completeness and compliance with policies.
- The proposal will be evaluated for viability and alignment with MMDC’s values.

**Step 3: Formal Recognition**

Once approved, the club receives a Certificate of Recognition and is officially registered as an MMDC student club. Recognized clubs are granted:

- Official listing in the MMDC Club Directory.
- Access to MMDC digital platforms and resources for activities.
- Permission to recruit members and organize events.
- Advisory support from the Office of Student Affairs.

## MasterList of HTE Partners (MMCL/MMDC) – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/39693731509645-MasterList-of-HTE-Partners-MMCL-MMDC

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/39693731509645-MasterList-of-HTE-Partners-MMCL-MMDC#main-content)

We are pleased to share the updated list of Host Training Establishments (HTEs) partnered with Mapúa Malayan Colleges Laguna – Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMCL–MMDC). These organizations are recognized partners where our students can complete their required practicum or internship.

👉 [Download the full list of current HTE partners (PDF)](https://mcl.edu.ph/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/List-of-Industry-Partners-with-Active-Memorandum-of-Agreement-as-of-July-2025.pdf)

[![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/39693747009677)](https://mcl.edu.ph/wp-content/uploads/2025/07/List-of-Industry-Partners-with-Active-Memorandum-of-Agreement-as-of-July-2025.pdf)

* * *

## **How to Use This List**

This list is meant to help you **explore and plan** your practicum journey. Here’s what you can do:

- **Review and shortlist** the companies or organizations you are most interested in.

- **Check their websites** to learn more about their work, culture, and internship opportunities.

- **Start reaching out** to inquire whether they are currently accepting interns, and if so, what roles or positions are available. Remember, your practicum role should be aligned with what your program specifically requires.

- Once you're ready to apply, you may do so and **apply directly** to the partner HTEs. When you reach out, kindly inform them that you are a student of **MMCL under the Mapua Malayan Digital College, a college under MMCL.**


* * *

✅ Tip: Being proactive in researching and reaching out will not only help you secure an internship faster but also give you valuable practice in professional communication and job applications.

* * *

### **FAQ**

**What if my chosen HTE isn’t accepting interns right now?**

You may keep the company on your shortlist and follow up later. In the meantime, you can apply to other HTEs on the list to ensure you stay on track with your practicum requirements and timeline.

**Can I apply to more than one HTE?**

Yes. You may strategize and send applications to multiple HTEs to increase your chances of securing a placement.

**What if I find an organization I want to intern with that is not on the list?**

You may suggest new HTEs but also be willing to facilitate the accreditation process. These companies will undergo evaluation and accreditation before they can be considered official partners. **See:**[HTE Accreditation & MOA Process for Practicum](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38665476654605)

**Do I need to inform MMDC when I apply?**

Yes. While you apply directly to the HTEs, please keep MMDC informed of your applications and outcomes, specifically your Practicum Coordinator or Program Heads. They will also need to endorse your placement to the HTE before you may formally begin your internship hours.

## Additional MMDC Practicum Partners for IT Students – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/39843942858765-Additional-MMDC-Practicum-Partners-for-IT-Students

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/39843942858765-Additional-MMDC-Practicum-Partners-for-IT-Students#main-content)

## **Overview**

This article introduces the **additional practicum partner organizations** available for students under the **IT specializations at Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC) for Term 2 of School Year 2025-2026**.

It lists each partner, their modality (remote / onsite / hybrid), available slots, and the application process. Use this guide to explore options, prepare your practicum application, and select a partner that supports your learning goals, schedule, and preferred working environment.

## IT Training Plan for Practicum – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/40345072724749-IT-Training-Plan-for-Practicum

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/40345072724749-IT-Training-Plan-for-Practicum#main-content)

When you begin your practicum, the tasks and responsibilities you are assigned at your Host Training Establishment (HTE) must align with the official **Training Plan** of your program. This plan outlines the expected learning objectives and activities for your internship and ensures that your work contributes meaningfully to your academic and professional development.

Under **CHED Memorandum Order No. 104, s. 2017**, all internships must have clearly defined and structured learning outcomes that are relevant to your degree program. These are documented in the HTE's Training Plan, which is reviewed and approved as part of the accreditation process.

**Important:**

When proposing an HTE or selecting your preferred company for internship, you must **verify that the internship role or scope of work they are offering aligns with the Training Plan** for your program. Work that is purely clerical, unrelated to your field, or does not meet the learning outcomes will not be approved.

If the tasks assigned to you during the internship do not match the approved Training Plan, inform your **Practicum Advisor** immediately so appropriate adjustments can be made.

You can review the standard Training Plans below and use this as reference to ensure that you will be assigned work that will check if some, if not all the items in this list.

| **Network and Cybersecurity** |
| --- |
| **Network Monitoring and Maintenance**<br>- Assist in observing network traffic and identifying irregular activity<br>- Help maintain stable connectivity across systems<br>- Support basic troubleshooting and documentation of network concerns<br>**System Security Checks**<br>- Conduct routine vulnerability scans under supervision<br>- Support firewall testing and verification<br>- Ensure antivirus systems are updated regularly<br>**Incident Reporting and Documentation**<br>- Draft initial reports on potential security incidents<br>- Organize and file logs for tracking purposes<br>- Escalate critical concerns to senior IT/security staff<br>**User Access Management**<br>- Assist in creating and updating user accounts<br>- Process password resets and permission adjustments<br>- Verify compliance with access control policies<br>**Asset and Configuration Tracking**<br>- Maintain updated records of hardware and software assets<br>- Assist with inventory tagging and logging<br>- Document network configurations to support audits and troubleshooting<br>**Security Awareness Support**<br>- Help organize cybersecurity training and awareness campaigns<br>- Prepare materials such as guides, posters, or digital reminders<br>- Promote best practices for secure system use among employees |

| **Software Development** |
| --- |
| **Web Scraping Execution**<br>- Run automated scripts to extract data from online sources<br>- Collaborate with business teams to monitor and validate extracted data<br>- Assist in maintaining scraping tools and updating data collection routines<br>**Automation Tool Development**<br>- Build simple programs to streamline data collection and research<br>- Apply appropriate programming languages (e.g., Python, JavaScript)<br>- Test and refine automation tools for reliability and efficiency<br>**Standards Compliance**<br>- Follow coding best practices and internal documentation protocols<br>- Ensure consistency and maintainability in code contributions<br>- Adhere to version control and project management guidelines<br>**System Integration**<br>- Assist in connecting new applications with existing platforms<br>- Support troubleshooting of integration issues to ensure seamless data flow<br>- Contribute to testing integrated systems for performance and stability<br>**Technical Documentation**<br>- Prepare clear and concise source code comments<br>- Draft configuration manuals and installation guides<br>- Maintain structured documentation for handover and future reference<br>**Application Coding and Debugging**<br>- Write software components in multiple programming languages<br>- Test applications to identify and resolve bugs<br>- Support stable deployment by refining code through iterative debugging |

| **Data Analytics** |
| --- |
| **Data Collection and Cleaning**<br>- Gather data from multiple internal and external sources<br>- Perform basic cleaning and preprocessing to prepare datasets for analysis<br>- Ensure accuracy and completeness of collected data<br>**Exploratory Data Analysis**<br>- Use Excel, Python, or SQL to summarize datasets<br>- Create visualizations to detect patterns, trends, and outliers<br>- Support preliminary analysis to guide deeper research<br>**Dashboard and Report Generation**<br>- Assist in creating visual reports and dashboards using Power BI, Tableau, or similar tools<br>- Update and maintain regular business reports<br>- Provide visuals that support data-driven decision-making<br>**Database Management Support**<br>- Support data entry, validation, and retrieval tasks<br>- Help ensure integrity of structured databases<br>- Assist in organizing datasets for easier access and usage<br>**Business Insight Assistance**<br>- Contribute to identifying key trends, correlations, or anomalies<br>- Assist in linking findings to business or marketing strategies<br>- Provide preliminary input to guide decision-makers<br>**Documentation and Presentation**<br>- Document analysis procedures and results<br>- Prepare slide decks and visual summaries of findings<br>- Assist in presenting insights to non-technical stakeholders in clear terms |

## Request for Credit Evaluation (RCEF) – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/40454620695693-Request-for-Credit-Evaluation-RCEF

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/40454620695693-Request-for-Credit-Evaluation-RCEF#main-content)

_This article outlines the course crediting evaluation process at Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC) for transferees and shifters, including the steps, requirements, and policies involved in requesting course credit for previously completed courses._

1. [_**What is the course credit evaluation process (RCEF)?**_](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/40454620695693-Request-for-Credit-Evaluation-RCEF#h_01K7YYXMHC6ZYK48K3ZJXZVB9G)

2. [_**Requirements for credit evaluation**_](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/40454620695693-Request-for-Credit-Evaluation-RCEF#h_01K7YY6PCWF029FMWZF2PNZ7RR)_– Documents and forms students must prepare and submit._

3. [_**Step-by-step Guide**_](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/40454620695693-Request-for-Credit-Evaluation-RCEF#h_01K7YY6PCY71HJDN3SJVH0216Z)_– How to fill out and submit the Request for Credit Evaluation Form (RCEForm)._

4. [_**File naming and submission guidelines**_](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/40454620695693-Request-for-Credit-Evaluation-RCEF#h_01K7Z0D4P1MNETQ8E6JX8H6D5V)_– Proper formatting and where to send documents._

5. [_**Important Guidelines**_](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/40454620695693-Request-for-Credit-Evaluation-RCEF#h_01K7YY6PDJP1GNY2575CVGKD61)_– Rules specific to transferees and shifters, including evaluation timelines._


## **What is the course credit evaluation process (Request for Credit Evaluation Form or RCEF)?**

The **Course Credit Evaluation** process for transferees and shifters is an essential step when entering an educational institution with previous school experience or shifting from a different program within the institution. It involves the careful review and evaluation of academic records to determine the equivalency and transferability of previously earned credits.

      This evaluation process ensures that students receive appropriate recognition, in the form of credited courses, for their prior coursework and have a clear understanding of how their educational history aligns with the requirements of the curriculum of the program they are enrolling in or shifting to. This aims to avoid unnecessary duplication of equivalent coursework and reduce the time and cost associated with completing a degree.

**Approval of courses taken from other higher educational institutions is the sole discretion of MAPUA MALAYAN DIGITAL COLLEGE. MMDC reserves the right to credit courses.**

**Transferees** are students who have previously attended another educational institution. The credit evaluation process should be completed within the**initial term**of the transferee. The initial term is the first term that the student is enrolled in MMDC.

**Shifters**, on the other hand, are students who intend to change their program and specialization from one to another within MMDC. The credit evaluation is an essential step in the shifting process to ensure the crediting of equivalent courses from their previous program towards the new one.

## **Requirements for Credit Evaluation**

**To proceed with the course credit evaluation process, please secure a****digital copy****of the following documents.**

1. RCEForm, duly filled out and signed by the student
2. Any of the following:    - Official Transcript of Records (TOR with grading system)
   - Copy of Grades (with grading system)
   - Grade Certification (with grading system)
   - Certified True Copy of the TOR (with grading system)

     _**Note**: Make sure that the document contains the grading system of your previous school._
3. Course Descriptions for each course/subject you are requesting credit for

_Note: The RCEForm is for transfer/shifter students who have earned credits from other higher educational institutions or a previous program._

## **Step-by-Step Guide**

**1\. Obtain the RCEForm:**

Log in to your EnrollMate Account and download the Request for Credit Evaluation Form (RCEF).

**2\. Read Guidelines and Agree:**

Thoroughly read the guidelines and terms and conditions on the form. If you agree, affix your signature and date on the designated space.![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/40454620693517)

**3\. Complete Personal Information.**

Under **"Personal Information,"** provide the following details:

- Last Name, First Name, Middle Name
- Student Number (or application number for not yet enrolled students)
- Program and Year (e.g., BSIT / 2023-2024)![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/40454651418765)

**4\. Fill in Units Earned.**

Based on your previous school records, identify the courses with the closest equivalency or similarity to the courses listed in the form.

Navigate to the section titled **"UNITS EARNED FROM OTHER HIGHER EDUCATIONAL INSTITUTION OR FROM PREVIOUS PROGRAM."**

Input the following details for each course you're requesting credit for:

- Course Code
- Unit
- Course Title
- Final Grade
- Year/Term Taken![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/40454620693901)

**5\. Repeat for Other Courses.**

If you're requesting credit for multiple courses, repeat step 4 for each course/subject.

**6\. Review Entries.**

Thoroughly review all entries to ensure accuracy.

## **File naming and submission guidelines**

Before you submit your documents, make sure to rename them using the specified format. Follow the instructions below:

- **RCEForm:**

**Format**: RCEF-PROGRAM-LAST NAME, FIRST NAME, MIDDLE INITIAL-SYXX-XX-TermX

**Example**:  RCEF-BSIT-DELA CRUZ, JUAN S-SY24-25-Term2

_**NOTE**:  Save the file in excel or sheets format._

- **Transcript of Records (TOR) and Course Descriptions:**

**Format**: RCEF-PROGRAM-DOCUMENT-LAST NAME, FIRST NAME, MIDDLE INITIAL-SYXX-XX-TermX

**Example:** RCEF-BSIT-TOR-DELA CRUZ, JUAN S-SY24-25-Term2

**1\. Gather Additional Requirements**

Please make sure you have your Transcript of Records (TOR) and course descriptions for each subject you are seeking credit for.

**NOTE**: Failure to submit the required documents will result in the non-processing of your request, as the evaluators will have no basis for the assessment of your previous coursework experience. This will result in “Not Credited” or “No Credit” evaluation results.

However, if you lack the course description only, you may still choose to proceed with the evaluation, provided you explicitly state your willingness to undergo the evaluation without the said document. This means that the evaluation will rely solely on the information available from your Transcript of Records (TOR), which provides limited information. Students accept that this **may result in no credit** being awarded due to limited information. Course descriptions provide detailed information about the content and scope of each course, which the evaluators use for assessing the equivalency and alignment with the curriculum of MMDC.

**2\. Submission**

Kindly submit the digital copies of the completed **RCEForm**, **TOR**, and **course descriptions** to your Admissions Advisor or, if the student is already enrolled, through email to records@mmdc.mcl.edu.ph.  Please ensure the subject of your email is formatted as follows:

**"Request for Credit Evaluation - Surname, First Name."**

## **Important Guidelines**

- For transferees, the crediting of courses shall be done after the approval of admission to MMDC.
- The crediting of courses shall be done in the initial term of studies at MMDC.
- For shifters, the crediting of courses shall be done after the approval of shifting by the college dean and shall be done not later than the date set by the college registrar.
- No other courses taken from other schools or from the previous MMDC program shall be credited after the initial term.
- Approval of courses taken from other higher educational institutions is the sole discretion of MAPUA MALAYAN DIGITAL COLLEGE. MMDC reserves the right to credit courses.
- Student fills out the form completely and submits to their Admissions Advisor or to the Records Officer (once enrolled). The Program Head, as the evaluator, grants or denies credit for the courses listed. The Office of the College Registrar encodes into the system the credited courses.

     By following these steps and guidelines, you ensure a smooth process for requesting a credit evaluation at Mapúa Malayan Digital College.

## From Enrollmate to Camu and Google: Transitioning to Official Student Platforms – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/40455172359309-From-Enrollmate-to-Camu-and-Google-Transitioning-to-Official-Student-Platforms

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/40455172359309-From-Enrollmate-to-Camu-and-Google-Transitioning-to-Official-Student-Platforms#main-content)

_This article serves as a guide on the importance of transitioning from Enrollmate to using official student platforms — **Camu** and the **MMDC Google Workspace email** — for a seamless academic experience. It outlines the key features and explains why these platforms are essential for academic and communication-related tasks._

## **From Enrollmate to Camu: Transitioning to Official Student Platforms**

While you may have used **Enrollmate** during the admissions process, this platform is **intended for admissions purposes only**. After the admission stage, your access to Enrollmate will be deactivated.

As an official student of **Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC)**, you must now **transition to using Camu and your MMDC Workspace email** for all academic, communication, and student-related activities.

## **What is MyCamu and MMDC Google Workspace Email?**

MyCamu and MMDC Google Workspace email are your main digital tools as a student of Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC). Here are the key features you should know:

#### **1\. Integrated Student Management**

Camu provides a centralized hub for your academic life. Through Camu, you can:

- Access your **course materials**
- View **grades** and **class schedules**
- Track academic progress and manage milestone requirements

#### **2\. Efficient Communication**

Your MMDC Google Workspace email is the **official channel for communication** between you, your mentors, IAs (Integrated Advisors), and coaches. It ensures:

- Timely updates on academic matters
- Clear correspondence about your milestones, activities, and support services

#### **3\. Collaborative Learning**

Camu supports interactive and collaborative learning through features that allow you to:

- Submit assignments
- Participate in discussions
- Collaborate with fellow learners on group tasks

#### **4\. Academic Support and Resources**

Many academic tools and support services are integrated within Camu, making it easier to:

- Get academic guidance
- Access learning resources
- Receive timely assistance when needed

## **Important Reminder**

To ensure a smooth and effective student experience at MMDC, **please begin using Camu and your MMDC Workspace email for all academic and communication-related tasks**. This will guarantee that you receive the most up-to-date information and remain well-connected with your academic community.

If you need help accessing Camu or setting up your MMDC email, feel free to visit these relevant help guides:

- [**Accessing Camu**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17498570466317-Accessing-Camu)
- [**See all Camu LMS categories**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17597079861645-See-all-Camu-LMS-categories)
- [**See All Google Workspace Tools**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/17704359025165-See-All-Google-Workspace-Tools)

Related to

- [Camu](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01H5V10RV3ES661TXFGK9APH6N&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")
- [Google](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01H5V4AMYV4K42ZDRD63QD80A7&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")
- [Google Account](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/search?content_tags=01H5V4BVY73TA72TZZFC2JGW9C&utf8=%E2%9C%93 "Search results")

## Document Requirements for Admission of New Freshman Students – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/40816512289805-Document-Requirements-for-Admission-of-New-Freshman-Students

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/40816512289805-Document-Requirements-for-Admission-of-New-Freshman-Students#main-content)

## **Overview**

This article lists the documents required for **freshman admission** to Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC), a college under Mapúa Malayan Colleges Laguna (MMCL); and explains how to submit them.

During your admission process, you may have already **uploaded digital copies** of your documents. However, **submitting the original physical copies** of these requirements is a **separate and essential step** to complete your official enrollment.

You will only be considered **officially enrolled** once MMDC has received and verified your complete physical documents. Students with pending requirements are considered **conditionally enrolled** until all credentials are submitted.

* * *

**📌 Note:**

A **freshman** refers to a student entering college for the first time — someone who has **not enrolled in any college or university before**.

* * *

## **Document Requirements**

Prepare the following major documents for freshman admission:

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/40816512289421)

**🔗** Please access this link for the full guide and the rest of the minor requirements.

[![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/40816525890829)](https://docs.google.com/presentation/d/1E4kiqIxg-kzpbluurr1qa_QuKAvcxFF8maUFFVmXllM/edit?usp=sharing)

## **How to Submit Your Physical Documents**

1. **Prepare your files.** Make sure all documents are clear, complete, and filled-out and signed where required.
2. **Drop off or send via your preferred courier service to**MMCL’s Registrar’s Office c/o:   - **Receiver:** Keilah Garcia
   - **Address:** Mapúa Malayan Colleges Laguna (MMCL), Pulo Diezmo Road, Southpoint, Cabuyao City, Laguna
   - **Contact No.:** 0960 598 8678
   - **Note to Courier/ Delivery Man:** Please leave the package with the guard at the MMCL main entrance.
3. **Monitor your learner email** for confirmation or feedback on missing requirements.

* * *

**📌 Note:**

All official documents—such as transcript of record, transfer credentials, or certifications—must be **addressed to** _**Mapúa Malayan Colleges Laguna (MMCL)**_ as the recognized legal and institutional name. **Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC)** operates as a college under **MMCL**, and therefore, all official documents should be addressed to MMCL.

* * *

## **Why do I need to submit my physical admission documents?**

Submitting your **physical admission documents** is required for MMDC to officially confirm your enrollment. Failure to submit your credentials may lead to the following:

- You **cannot be officially promoted** to the next level.
- You **cannot officially graduate** from the program.
- You **cannot be recognized for honors or awards**, even if qualified.
- You **cannot enroll in succeeding academic terms** without being cleared.
- You **will not be released any official records** (e.g., transcript, certifications, or permanent record).
- Your **enrollment may be cancelled** if documentary requirements remain incomplete beyond the deadline.

If your documents are still being processed by your previous school, coordinate immediately with your former registrar to ensure timely transmittal to MMDC/MMCL.

* * *

**📌 Note:**

These terms are detailed in the **Affidavit of Undertaking** you signed during admission. By signing the affidavit, you acknowledged your temporary or conditional enrollment status and agreed to submit all required credentials within the given timeline to maintain your official standing at MMDC.

* * *

## **Notes & Reminders**

- Digital submission during the application process **does not replace** the need for original physical copies.
- Submit all requirements on or before the set deadline to avoid interruption of enrollment or access to student services.


* * *

## How to Submit Your Physical Admission Documents to MMCL – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/40928241049229-How-to-Submit-Your-Physical-Admission-Documents-to-MMCL

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/40928241049229-How-to-Submit-Your-Physical-Admission-Documents-to-MMCL#main-content)

## Overview

This article explains **how to submit your** **original physical admission documents** to Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC), a college under Mapúa Malayan Colleges Laguna (MMCL).

Submitting physical copies is a required step separate from the digital upload done during your online application.

You will only be considered officially enrolled once your physical documents have been received and verified by MMDC.

## Step-by-Step Submission Guide

1. **Prepare your files.**
   - Make sure all documents are **clear, complete, fully filled-out and signed** where required.

   - Use an **envelope or folder** labeled with your **full name**, **student number (or App-Number)**, and **program**.
2. **Drop off or send via courier** to MMCL’s Registrar’s Office:
   - **Receiver:** Keilah Garcia

   - **Address:** Mapúa Malayan Colleges Laguna (MMCL), Pulo Diezmo Road, Southpoint, Cabuyao City, Laguna

   - **Contact No.:** 0960 598 8678

   - **Courier Note:** For LBC and similar services, please leave the package with the **guard at the MMCL main entrance**.
3. **Confirm receipt.**
   - Monitor your **MMDC learner email** for confirmation that your documents have been received.

   - If any requirement is missing or incomplete, the Records team will notify you for follow-up.

* * *

**📌 Note:**

All official documents—such as transcript of record, transfer credentials, or certifications—must be **addressed to** _**Mapúa Malayan Colleges Laguna (MMCL)**_ as the recognized legal and institutional name. **Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC)** operates as a college under **MMCL**, and therefore, all official documents should be addressed to MMCL.

* * *

## ⚠️ Reminders

- Double-check your documents before sending — incomplete submissions may cause **delays in enrollment confirmation**.

- Keep **digital or photocopy backups** of all submitted documents.

- Courier timelines vary; send your documents early to meet the submission deadline.


* * *

## Effective Communication – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41130555083021-Effective-Communication

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41130555083021-Effective-Communication#main-content)

Whether you're collaborating in person or working online, clear and effective communication is essential in today’s workplace. This section equips you with practical strategies and real-world insights to help you communicate confidently in any setting. From writing professional emails to practicing proper etiquette and navigating virtual meetings, these curated articles and videos are designed to boost your skills and build your confidence with every interaction. Start applying these strategies today—your future self (and your teammates) will thank you.

### **Mastering Professional Communication**

- **Article:** [**8 Ways You Can Improve Your Communication Skills**](https://professional.dce.harvard.edu/blog/8-ways-you-can-improve-your-communication-skills/)

_(This article from Harvard DCE provides practical tips to enhance your communication habits in the workplace.)_
- **Article:** [**Effective Communication at Work: Mastering Filipino Workplace Etiquette**](https://richestph.com/effective-communication-at-work-mastering-filipino-workplace-etiquette/)( _Richest PH provides insights into Filipino workplace communication styles and etiquette._)
- **Video:** [**The Art of Effective Communication \| Marcus Alexander Velazquez \| TEDx**](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=2Yw6dFQBklA)

_(A TEDx talk that explores methods to evaluate and improve your communication strategies.)_

**How to Write Professional Emails**

## Professionalism in the Workplace – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41130587192205-Professionalism-in-the-Workplace

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41130587192205-Professionalism-in-the-Workplace#main-content)

The modern workplace goes beyond dress codes and formal behavior—it’s about how you present yourself in any environment, whether in person, online, or somewhere in between. This section provides practical tips and real-world insights to help you maintain professionalism across remote, hybrid, and digital settings. With curated articles and videos, you’ll explore how to adapt to evolving workplace norms, manage your time effectively, and build a strong professional presence. Apply these strategies to stay focused, credible, and confident—wherever and however you work.

- **Maintaining Professionalism in Remote and Hybrid Work Environments**

  - **Article:** [**The Remote Work Advantage: Filipino Experts' Success in Remote Work**](https://www.kineticstaff.com/the-remote-work-advantage-how-filipino-experts-turn-challenges-into-career-success/)( _Kinetic Innovative Staffing explores how Filipino professionals turn remote work challenges into career success._)
  - **Article:** [**Work-from-Home and Hybrid Setups in the Philippines: Trends for 2025**](https://manilarecruitment.com/manila-recruitment-articles-advice/work-from-home-hybrid-setups-philippines-trends-2025/)( _Manila Recruitment discusses the latest trends, challenges, and solutions shaping hybrid and work-from-home setups in the Philippines._)
  - **Video:** [**How I Stay Productive While Working From Home \| Tips for Remote Work**](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=B-yibnWrFH8)( _A practical video on maintaining professionalism in remote work environments, from setting boundaries to staying organized._)

- **Professionalism in the Digital Age**

  - **Article:** [**The Importance of Business Etiquette in the Social Media Era**](https://www.elizabethalarcon.com/cultivating-professionalism-in-a-digital-world-the-importance-of-business-etiquette-in-the-social-media-era/)( _An article exploring why professionalism is crucial in today’s digitally connected world._)
  - **Article:** [**Personal Branding in 2024-25: Why It's Crucial for Business Leaders and Entrepreneurs**](https://esquire.com.ph/articles/personal-branding-in-2024-25-why-its-crucial-for-business-leaders-and-entrepreneurs)( _Esquire Philippines discusses the importance of personal branding for business leaders and entrepreneurs._)
  - **Video:** [**Professionalism in the Digital Age \| TEDx**](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=1aA1WGON49E)( _A TEDx talk discussing how professionalism has evolved in the digital age, particularly in remote work settings._)

- **Time Management and Accountability in Remote Settings**

  - **Article:** [**How Filipino Remote Workers Maintain Productivity and Well-Being**](https://www.linkedin.com/pulse/balancing-act-how-filipino-remote-workers-maintain-ronen-zuckerstein-opq0e)( _LinkedIn article exploring strategies Filipino remote workers use to manage time effectively._)
  - **Article:** [**The Rise of Remote Work in the Philippines**](https://www.thestudentpocketguide.com/2023/03/study/remote-working-philippines/)( _Student Pocket Guide discusses the benefits and challenges of remote work in the Philippines._)
  - **Video:** [**Time Management Strategies for Remote and Hybrid Careers**](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=O7jlbdh-fTw)( _A helpful YouTube video outlining key time management strategies for remote workers._)

## Personal Branding – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41130607331597-Personal-Branding

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41130607331597-Personal-Branding#main-content)

Build Your Personal Brand and Stand Out. Having an effective personal brand goes a long way in paving the way for career opportunities and valuable relationships. This selection of resources provides practical guidance—from being genuine and telling your story, to using LinkedIn and developing a portfolio that catches attention.

Whether you're at the onset of your career or wish to polish your image, these materials will equip you to confidently unlock new avenues. Start enhancing your personal brand today, so it represents you and is noticed!

- **Building Your Personal Brand**


  - **Article:** [**Building Your Personal Brand: Tips and Strategies**](https://www.michaelpage.com.ph/advice/career-advice/career-progression/building-your-personal-brand-tips-and-strategies)( _Michael Page Philippines offers insights into crafting a compelling personal brand, emphasizing authenticity and strategic self-presentation._)
  - **Article:** [**How To Build Your Personal Brand in 2025: 9 Simple Steps**](https://www.shopify.com/blog/personal-brand)( _Shopify provides a step-by-step guide to establishing a personal brand that resonates with your target audience and aligns with your professional goals._)
  - **Video:** [**5 Steps to Building a Personal Brand You Feel Good About \| TEDx**](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ozMCb0wOnMU)( _A TEDx talk focused on personal branding, including how to express your values and strengths online._)
- **Creating a Personal Brand on LinkedIn**


  - **Article:** [**How to Optimize Your LinkedIn Profile**](https://johnclements.com/the-looking-glass/career-advice/how-to-optimize-linkedin-profile/)( _John Clements Consultants provides a guide to optimizing your LinkedIn profile to enhance your personal brand._)
  - **Article:** [**17-Minute LinkedIn Personal Branding Strategy: A Game Changer**](https://taplio.com/blog/how-to-build-a-personal-brand-on-linkedin)( _Taplio provides a concise daily routine to build your personal brand on LinkedIn, focusing on content creation and audience engagement._)
  - **Video**: [LinkedIn Personal Branding Tips](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=-Vt_vlSlu0I)

    (A YouTube tutorial on personal branding using LinkedIn, including tips for optimizing your profile, network building, and job searching.)
- **Building a Personal Portfolio**


  - **Article:** [**Your Ultimate Guide to Creating a Career Portfolio**](https://ph.jobstreet.com/career-advice/article/your-ultimate-guide-to-creating-a-career-portfolio)( _JobStreet Philippines provides detailed steps on assembling a career portfolio, including organizing documents, showcasing achievements, and selecting appropriate platforms._)
  - **Article:** [**Create a Portfolio That Highlights Your Strengths as a Filipino VA**](https://leadsociety.org/create-a-portfolio-that-highlights-your-strengths/)( _Lead Society discusses strategies for virtual assistants to build portfolios that effectively showcase their skills and experiences._)
  - **Video:** [**How to Create an Online Portfolio with ZERO Experience**](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=1365WwwCTx4)( _A YouTube tutorial guiding beginners through the process of building an online portfolio from scratch._)
  - **Video:** [**Freelancer Portfolio for Beginners \| Victoria Nelle**](https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=2dhuZgZgRIA)( _Victoria Nelle shares tips on creating a freelancer portfolio, focusing on content that appeals to potential clients._)

## 2025-10/30 MMDC - Enter the Grid: Epic Trivia Night & Engage Grand Reveal! – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41133546714381-2025-10-30-MMDC-Enter-the-Grid-Epic-Trivia-Night-Engage-Grand-Reveal

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41133546714381-2025-10-30-MMDC-Enter-the-Grid-Epic-Trivia-Night-Engage-Grand-Reveal#main-content)

👻 Welcome to Engage, MMDC! 🎃 MMDC kicked off Halloween early with its first-ever Trivia Night, "Enter the Grid", where one team crushed the competition by just a few points! But the biggest reveal? The launch of Anthology Engage at MMDC! 🎃👻

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/41133575504013)

**🎃 MMDC - Enter the Grid: Epic Trivia Night & Engage Grand Reveal!**

The spooky atmosphere was electric at MMDC last Halloween Eve! Students gathered at Google Meet last **October 30, 5:30 PM** to **Enter the Grid** and destress before finals via a **Trivia Night**, capping off a week of intense mental competition and culminating in the much-anticipated **Engage Reveal!**

**🧠 Trivia Takes Center Stage**

MMDC's Halloween celebration kicked off with intense rounds of trivia designed to test general knowledge across a variety of subjects. Hosted by April Punay, the energy was palpable as our 3 major teams, **Puyat, Magiting,** and **Grave Concerns** battled for bragging rights and spooktacular prizes!

- Congratulations to the winning team, **Grave Concerns**! Their mastery across all categories secured them the top prize with 29 points! Other winners from the Pre-Game Puzzles and the Spooky/Futuristic/Witty Costume Competition may contact their respective IAs to claim their prizes.

**✨ The Big Reveal: Welcome to Engage, MMDC!**

Facilitated by Koji Odal, MMDC’s exciting new student platform was finally unveiled: **Anthology Engage!** This platform is your **central hub for your student life** at MMDC. It aims to:

- **Personalize:** You can join Clubs, connect within MCL & MMDC, and download your Events Transcript!
- **Manage Organizations:** Provide a dedicated space for student Clubs, making it easy to manage and organize activities!
- **Centralize Information:** Host all announcements, event calendars, and resources for the entire MMDC community!

This platform - accessible by the public and shared by the MCL Community - represents a massive leap forward in fostering a more active and connected MMDC community. Exclusive platform features are also available to those with MCL accounts; MMDC club members and Enter the Grid registrants have been pre-registered for MCL account creation, and they can expect additional instructions for activation soon. We shall release a follow-up form for students who would also like to register for their own MCL accounts - stay tuned!

**🎤 Important Notes**

Want more events like this? We encourage everyone to **accomplish the Feedback Form linked here:** [https://engage.mcl.edu.ph/submitter/form/start/382](https://engage.mcl.edu.ph/submitter/form/start/382)

The success of Enter the Grid proves that MMDC students are ready to enhance their overall experience and unlock their future - this also sets a powerful precedent for the rest of the academic year at Engage and total MMDC!

**👻 Are you ready to Engage, MMDC?** Account Registration and Guides for the MMDC Engage platform will be released soon. Make sure you don't miss out on the latest updates, organizations, and events here at Engage—your new digital hub!

## Welcome to MMDC: Essentials to Help You Succeed – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41133969319053-Welcome-to-MMDC-Essentials-to-Help-You-Succeed

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41133969319053-Welcome-to-MMDC-Essentials-to-Help-You-Succeed#main-content)

|     |
| --- |
| ## **Overview**<br>Starting your journey at Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC) means preparing the right tools and habits that will help you succeed in a fully digital learning environment. This article outlines the essential requirements—both technical and personal—to help you have a smooth and productive experience from day one. |

* * *

## **Table of Contents:**

1. [**Device Requirements**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41133969319053-Welcome-to-MMDC-Essentials-to-Help-You-Succeed#h_01KA0JAK8XEKD9BQS7KMYHYPHD)
2. [**Internet Recommendations**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41133969319053-Welcome-to-MMDC-Essentials-to-Help-You-Succeed#h_01KA0JAK97T8W9NVN37HGQDF50)
3. [**Software and Platforms**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41133969319053-Welcome-to-MMDC-Essentials-to-Help-You-Succeed#h_01KA0JAK9D3KT2V73BWX9A2TKQ)
4. [**Academic Readiness**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41133969319053-Welcome-to-MMDC-Essentials-to-Help-You-Succeed#h_01KA0JAK9HCB1168CHCX99S4YH)
5. [**Personal Skills To Build On That Help You Succeed**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41133969319053-Welcome-to-MMDC-Essentials-to-Help-You-Succeed#h_01KA0JAK9NXYVJTYVJWA4CM9N8)
6. [**Support Systems Available at MMDC**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41133969319053-Welcome-to-MMDC-Essentials-to-Help-You-Succeed#h_01KA0JAK9RECRDP2162EXZFZEM)

* * *

##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41133969319053-Welcome-to-MMDC-Essentials-to-Help-You-Succeed\#h_01KG4HGT9QG8Y4K21BRSX5W7K4)

### Device Requirements

To access your classes, complete assessments, and participate in student life activities, you need a reliable device that we recommend meets the following minimum specifications:

1. #### **Recommended Device**


- **Laptop or Desktop Computer**
1. Processor: Intel i5 / Ryzen 5 or higher

2. RAM: 8 GB (16 GB recommended for smoother performance)

3. Storage: At least 128 GB (SSD preferred for faster loading)

4. Operating System: Windows 10 or higher, macOS (latest versions)
- **Minimum Device Requirements**  1. Processor: Intel i3 / Ryzen 3

2. RAM: 4 GB

3. Working webcam and microphone

4. Updated browser (Google Chrome or Microsoft Edge)

**Why this matters:** A capable and stable device helps you avoid delays in class activities, ensures smooth meetings and consultations, and improves overall learning performance in a digital-first environment.

|     |
| --- |
| **📌 Note:**<br>While tablets and smart phones can be helpful for quick checks, messaging, or light coursework, they are not ideal for the full MMDC learning experience. Many activities—such as typing assessments, joining live sessions, using productivity tools, and navigating the Learning Management System—work best on a laptop or desktop. For this reason, we strongly recommend having a reliable computer to ensure smoother performance, fewer technical issues, and a more productive learning experience overall. |

* * *

##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41133969319053-Welcome-to-MMDC-Essentials-to-Help-You-Succeed\#h_01KG4HGT9QG8Y4K21BRSX5W7K4)

### Internet Recommendations

A stable and reliable internet connection is essential for attending classes, downloading materials, submitting assessments, and participating in group work.

#### **Recommended Internet Connection**

- **Speed:** At least 10–20 Mbps

- **Connection Type:** Fiber or broadband (preferred)

- **Back-up Options:**
  - Mobile data

  - Portable WiFi

  - Access to Learning Hubs (Makati or Bacolod)

|     |
| --- |
| **📌 Tip:**<br> If you experience connection issues, inform your mentor or advisor early so alternative arrangements can be made. |

* * *

##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41133969319053-Welcome-to-MMDC-Essentials-to-Help-You-Succeed\#h_01KG4HGT9QG8Y4K21BRSX5W7K4)

### Software and Platforms

MMDC provides access to essential tools and platforms you will use throughout your studies.

Prepare to regularly use:

- **Google Workspace**

- **Camu SIS and LMS**

- **MMDC Learner Email (@mmdc.edu.ph)**

- **Help Center** – for support and service requests

- **Anthology Engage** – for events, communities, and student life


|     |
| --- |
| **📌 Tip:**<br> Make sure to check your MMDC email regularly and log in to your learning platforms to stay updated with your academic requirements. |

* * *

##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41133969319053-Welcome-to-MMDC-Essentials-to-Help-You-Succeed\#h_01KG4HGT9QG8Y4K21BRSX5W7K4)

### Academic Readiness

Thriving in a digital-first college also requires building healthy habits and a mindset that supports independent learning.

#### **Key Attitudes for Success**

- **Consistency:** Show up regularly, manage your time well, and meet deadlines.

- **Openness to Feedback:** Apply mentor and instructor guidance to improve your skills.

- **Proactiveness:** Ask for help early when challenges arise.

- **Growth Mindset:** Believe that skills—especially digital and communication skills—improve with practice.


* * *

##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41133969319053-Welcome-to-MMDC-Essentials-to-Help-You-Succeed\#h_01KG4HGT9QG8Y4K21BRSX5W7K4)

### Personal Skills To Build On That Help You Succeed

While MMDC provides full support, these skills help you navigate college more confidently:

- **Communication:** Reply to messages, consult when needed, and share concerns early.

- **Digital Literacy:** Comfort with basic software, online tools, and troubleshooting simple issues.

- **Self-Management:** Plan your week, break tasks into manageable steps, and set achievable goals.

- **Resilience:** Stay motivated, especially during busy weeks or unexpected difficulties.


* * *

##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41133969319053-Welcome-to-MMDC-Essentials-to-Help-You-Succeed\#h_01KG4HGT9QG8Y4K21BRSX5W7K4)

### Support Systems Available at MMDC

You are never alone—MMDC is built with multiple layers of support:

- **Integrated Advising** for student support and guidance

- **Student Affairs** for student development, engagement and wellbeing

- **Career Development** for career coaching, resume building, and future planning

- **Learning Hubs** for study spaces and in-person student support

- **Help Center** for quick answers to student questions


Reach out anytime—your success is our priority.

* * *

##### [> > \> back to top](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41133969319053-Welcome-to-MMDC-Essentials-to-Help-You-Succeed\#h_01KG4HGT9QG8Y4K21BRSX5W7K4)

## Summary

To succeed at MMDC, you need:

- A reliable **device**

- A stable **internet connection**

- Familiarity with **digital learning tools and platforms**

- A positive **mindset**, good **study habits**, and proactive **communication**

- Willingness to grow, ask questions, and seek support


College is a journey—and MMDC is here to support you every step of the way.

* * *

## Calendar of Activities SY2025-2026-Term 2 – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41253055872781-Calendar-of-Activities-SY2025-2026-Term-2

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41253055872781-Calendar-of-Activities-SY2025-2026-Term-2#main-content)

## **Overview**

This article provides the **official Term Calendar for SY 2025–2026 Term 2**. It lists all key academic dates and deadlines for the term, including grade viewing dates, enrollment periods, holidays, and other important academic activities.

Use this calendar to plan ahead, manage workload, and stay on track with all requirements throughout the term. Keeping these dates in mind will help you avoid missing deadlines and ensure a smooth and organized academic experience throughout the term.

You may refer to the table below for the complete list of activities and schedules for the term.

* * *

**📌 Note:**

An additional table is provided for students who have unfortunately been affected by the recent typhoons and are under the submission extension program. Please refer to the second table below.

* * *

## OMG Awards! – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41307706765837-OMG-Awards

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41307706765837-OMG-Awards#main-content)

Who says LDRs don’t work?! 🤨

If there is one thing that MMDC Mentors consistently prove, it’s that distance – digital or otherwise – is not a barrier in fostering a caring and thriving learning community!

Through the dedication and guidance of your mentors, you have experienced how meaningful, supportive, and engaging learning can be, even from a distance. Just last week, you nominated the mentors who stood out the most for the first-ever **Outstanding Mentor for Growth (OMG) Award**! Despite the digital divide, these mentors lead thought-provoking discussions, share relevant industry know-how, and impart practical work skills for their students.

After reading your responses sent with heartfelt enthusiasm and filled with inspiring stories, we are proud to present _your_ very first **Outstanding Mentors for Growth (OMG) Awardees!**

### **GE OMG Awardee:  Mentor Mark Paulo Tanjente**

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/41307683487629)

### **BA OMG Awardee: Mentor Jocelyn Abad**

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/41307706762765)

### **IT OMG Awardee: Mentor Aldrin John Tamayo**

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/41307683491213)

### **Congratulations to our dear OMG Awardees! 🥳**

The stories behind the awardees, including your nominees _(Yes, we have already sent your personal messages to them!_ 😉 _),_ remind us that great mentorship can transform learning, spark confidence, and inspire growth, even across distances.

We know that these mentors represent just a few of the many dedicated educators who make learning at MMDC rigorous but at the same time fun and genuinely worthwhile.We honor and thank all mentors who have shown commitment, compassion, and consistency to our learners!

May this recognition continue to motivate our entire community to keep raising the bar for what distance learning _must_ be.

Now, let’s keep an eye on who can be the next OMG Award recipient! 💪

## Part 1: Preparing for Enrollment – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41438247045133-Part-1-Preparing-for-Enrollment

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41438247045133-Part-1-Preparing-for-Enrollment#main-content)

|     |
| --- |
| ## **Overview**<br>Preparing for enrollment is an important step in making sure you choose the right courses, stay on track with your curriculum, and manage your workload and finances effectively. This article guides you through what you need to review before enrollment begins — including your program’s **Curriculum Plan (** [**IT**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/sections/28639223603469-MMDC-s-Information-Technology-Program) **/** [**BA**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/sections/28639222873229-MMDC-s-Business-Administration-Program) **)**, academic standing, prerequisites, co-requisites, and time availability — so you can enter the enrollment period confident and ready.<br>This article works **hand-in-hand with** [**Part 2: Enrollment Guidelines & Policies**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41439901133965), which explain the rules and principles that should guide your enrollment decisions. Once you’ve completed your preparation, you may refer to [**Part 3: MMDC's Online Enrollment Steps**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41439855591437) for instructions on how to enroll in the system. |

## **Table of Contents:**

1. [**Who this Applies to**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41438247045133-Part-1-Preparing-for-Enrollment#h_01KAZW541Z26TRGPPAF5MJX91B)

[**Prepare for Enrollment in 3 Steps**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41438247045133-Part-1-Preparing-for-Enrollment#h_01KAZW5423RRRXYZXK7KMQF6T1)   - [**Determine your Workload for the Term**](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/41438247045133-Part-1-Preparing-for-Enrollment#h_01KAZW5424Y6DF4PAPZG3286FR)
