## Join the Celebration: MMDC's National Working Students Day – Year 2! – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/44223025655437-Join-the-Celebration-MMDC-s-National-Working-Students-Day-Year-2

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/44223025655437-Join-the-Celebration-MMDC-s-National-Working-Students-Day-Year-2#main-content)

_Whether you are currently working while studying, have done so before, or simply want to support fellow students who do — this celebration is for you._

This March, Mapúa Malayan Digital College invites you to take part in a series of activities in celebration of **National Working Students Day  on March 21** — a day dedicated to recognizing the perseverance, resilience, and aspirations of students who balance **work and education**.

This celebration forms part of **MMDC’s Step Up sa Pangarap campaign**, which seeks to highlight the realities of working students while creating spaces for reflection, connection, and support.

This year, three major initiatives will mark the celebration:

## **State of the Working Student (SWS)**

|     |
| --- |
| The **State of the Working Student (SWS)** aims to better understand the lived realities of working students across the Philippines.<br>Through a nationwide survey, working students have been invited to share their experiences related to academic access, work schedules, financial realities, well-being, support systems, and future aspirations. The insights gathered will be consolidated into the **State of the Working Student Report**, which MMDC will share publicly with schools, employers, policymakers, and other stakeholders.<br>The findings will be shared **on March 21**, marking the first public sharing of insights from this study. |

👉 Take the survey:

[State of the Working Student Survey](https://forms.gle/tohKAtRJXK4vLYq27)

👉 Learn more about the SWS initiative:

[State of the Working Student News Article](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/44220956273549)

* * *

## **Run for the Working Student — Nationwide Run**

|     |
| --- |
| On **March 21**, students are invited to take part in the **Run for the Working Student**, a simple but meaningful nationwide “run anywhere” activity.<br>By running, walking, or moving on March 21, you become part of **a collective gesture of support — a nationwide show of solidarity for those who work hard both in the workplace and in the classroom.**<br>Participants may complete their run anywhere that works for them — outdoors, at a gym, or even as part of a daily walk. Students are encouraged to share their participation online as part of the celebration.<br>1. **Wear a BLUE shirt** to symbolize support for working students<br>   <br>2. **Run or walk at your own pace**<br>   <br>3. **Track your distance or time** using any fitness or step-tracking app<br>   <br>4. **Share your run online** using the hashtags: **#StepUpForWorkingStudents**<br>   <br>   **#WorkingStudentsDayPH** |

👉 Learn more about the run and how to participate:

[3.21 Step Up & Go - A National Working Students Day Run-Anywhere Movement!](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/44222012162445)

* * *

## **Step Up Your Success: Career Conversations**

|     |
| --- |
| MMDC will also host a series of **Career Roadshows** designed to support ALL STUDENTS in preparing for the next stage of their professional journeys.<br>These sessions will feature conversations and engagements with industry partners covering topics such as:<br>• Career preparation and readiness<br>• Workplace expectations and opportunities<br>• Insights from employers across different industries<br>The roadshows aim to connect students with practical guidance and perspectives that can help them navigate both work and future career paths. |

👉 Learn more about the roadshows:

[Step Up Your Success: Career Conversations](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/44222730816781-Step-Up-Your-Success-Career-Conversations)

* * *

## **National Working Students Day Is a Movement**

At its heart is a simple belief: **every student’s journey deserves recognition.**

Some students are balancing work and school. Others support their families, take on side hustles, or quietly carry the discipline and sacrifices needed to pursue their goals. In many ways, **every student is a working student, working towards something** — a dream, a better future, or a responsibility they hold for themselves or for others.

MMDC hopes to create a space where these journeys can be seen, shared, and supported. The activities for National Working Students Day — the **State of the Working Student**, the **Run for the Working Student**, and the **Career Roadshows** — are ways for the community to reflect on these realities and celebrate the determination behind them.

But a movement only becomes meaningful when people **show up for it**.

Whether you are a working student yourself, someone who has experienced balancing work and school, or someone who simply wants to stand with fellow students, **you are invited to be part of this movement**.

**Because every student is working toward something — and every journey deserves to be seen, supported, and celebrated.**

## Calendar of Activities SY 2025-2026-Term 3 – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/44313019327885-Calendar-of-Activities-SY-2025-2026-Term-3

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/44313019327885-Calendar-of-Activities-SY-2025-2026-Term-3#main-content)

## **Overview**

This article provides the **official Term Calendar for SY 2025–2026 Term 3**.

It lists all key academic dates and deadlines for the term, including grade viewing dates, enrollment periods, holidays, and other important academic activities.

Use this calendar to plan ahead, manage workload, and stay on track with all requirements throughout the term. Keeping these dates in mind will help you avoid missing deadlines and ensure a smooth and organized academic experience throughout the term.

You may refer to the table below for the complete list of activities and schedules for the term.

|     |     |     |
| --- | --- | --- |
| **Term 3 SY 2025-2026** |
| **March 2026** |
| Eligibility Review, Academic Advising, and Early Filing Period for Prospective Graduating Students:<br>1\. Request for Study Overload<br>2\. Request for Enrollment of Courses with Pre-Requisites<br>3\. Petition for Special Classes | March 23 | Monday |
| Re-Enrollment Consultation for Students Transitioning from New Enrollees to Re-Enrollees | March 31 | Tuesday |
| **April 2026** |
| REGULAR HOLIDAY\*\*<br>MAUNDY THURSDAY & GOOD FRIDAY | April 2 - 3 | Thursday - Friday |

| REGULAR HOLIDAY\*\*<br>DAY OF VALOR | April 9 | Thursday |

## Guide to MMDC Discount and Scholarship Programs (FAQs) – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/44257513459981-Guide-to-MMDC-Discount-and-Scholarship-Programs-FAQs

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/44257513459981-Guide-to-MMDC-Discount-and-Scholarship-Programs-FAQs#main-content)

**Family Discount Program**

**What is the MMDC Family Discount Program?**

The MMDC Family Discount Program provides tuition fee discounts to immediate family members who enroll at Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC) during the same term. It is designed to help families pursue education together while making tuition more affordable.

**Who can qualify for the Family Discount?**

The program is open to immediate family members of an MMDC student, including:

- Siblings
- Parents
- Children
- Spouse

They must be enrolled in MMDC during the same academic term.

**How many family members can receive the discount?**

The program allows up to four (4) family members to participate:

- 1 primary enrollee (regular tuition rate)
- Up to 3 additional family members who may receive discounts.

**What is the discount structure?**

The Family Discount is applied on top of the standard 20% Asenso Discount, resulting in the following total tuition discounts:

- First family member: 20% (Asenso Discount only)
- Second family member: 30% total discount (20% Asenso + 10% Family Discount)
- Third family member: 45% total discount (20% Asenso + 25% Family Discount)
- Fourth family member: 60% total discount (20% Asenso + 40% Family Discount)

**Does the discount apply to miscellaneous fees?**

No. The Family Discount applies only to tuition fees and does not cover miscellaneous or other school fees.

**What are the eligibility requirements?**

To qualify, each applicant must:

- Be enrolled in an MMDC program with at least 9 academic units
- Provide proof of relationship through official documents such as a birth certificate or marriage certificate.

**What documents are required to apply?**

Applicants must submit:

- MMDC Family Discount Program Application Form
- PSA-issued proof of family relationship, such as:  - Birth certificate (for siblings or parent-child relationships)
  - Marriage certificate (for spouse)

**Do students need to reapply every term?**

Yes. The family discount must be revalidated every term to confirm continued eligibility.

**What happens if one family member withdraws from enrollment?**

If a qualified family member withdraws or cancels enrollment during the term, the family discount for the affected members may be forfeited for that term.

**Can the Family Discount be combined with other scholarships?**

The Family Discount cannot be combined with other MMDC scholarships or tuition discounts, except for the Asenso 20% Discount Program.

**NextGen Discount Program**

**What is the MMDC NextGen Discount Program?**

The MMDC NextGen Discount Program provides financial assistance to solo parents, children of solo parents, and working youth aged 18–25 who want to pursue college education while managing financial or work responsibilities.

**What benefit does the program provide?**

Qualified applicants will receive a 30% discount on tuition fees for one term only.

**Who can apply for the NextGen Discount Program?**

The program is open to new or incoming MMDC students who belong to either of the following groups:

- Solo parents or children of solo parents
- Working youth aged 18–25

**What are the eligibility requirements for solo parents or children of solo parents?**

Applicants must:

- Have a valid Solo Parent ID
- Provide a PSA-issued document verifying the parent-child relationship
- Belong to a household with monthly income not exceeding ₱25,000
- Enroll in at least 9 units at MMDC

**What are the eligibility requirements for working youth?**

Applicants must:

- Be 18 to 25 years old
- Have a minimum General Weighted Average (GWA) of 85
- Be currently employed (part-time or full-time)
- Submit a recommendation letter from their employer confirming work ethic and performance

**What documents are required to apply?**

Applicants must submit:

- MMDC NextGen Discount Program Application Form
- Supporting documents such as:  - Solo Parent ID or proof of relationship (for solo parent applicants)
  - Proof of employment
  - Academic records showing required GWA
  - Employer recommendation letter
  - Proof of income (e.g., ITR, payslip, bank statement, or affidavit of income)

Additional documents may be required depending on employment type (formal or informal).

**When will applicants receive the results?**

Applicants will be notified within five (5) business days after submitting complete requirements.

**Can the NextGen Discount be renewed?**

No. The 30% tuition discount is valid for one term only and is non-renewable.

**Can the NextGen Discount be combined with other scholarships?**

The NextGen Discount cannot be combined with other MMDC scholarships or discounts, except for the Asenso 20% Discount Program.

**What happens if enrollment is canceled or not completed?**

If a student fails to enroll within the given enrollment period, the NextGen Discount slot may be forfeited and awarded to another qualified applicant.

Since slots are limited and granted on a first-come, first-served basis, timely completion of enrollment is strongly encouraged.

**YGC–Ayala Employee Promotional Discount Program**

**What is the YGC–Ayala Employee Promotional Discount Program?**

The YGC–Ayala Employee Promotional Discount Program is a special tuition discount offered by Mapúa Malayan Digital College (MMDC) to students whose parent is a regular employee of a YGC or Ayala member company.

**What benefit does the program provide?**

Qualified students will receive a 25% tuition fee discount per term, which is applied on top of the Asenso Discount.

**Who is eligible for this discount?**

Students may qualify if their parent is a regular employee of a YGC or Ayala member company listed in the application form.

**What documents are required to apply?**

Applicants must submit:

- [Completed YGC–Ayala Employee Promotional Discount Application Form and Waiver](https://drive.google.com/file/d/1J-HYeMvtYmVGUmJyt1molhvDFVltczQl/view?usp=sharing)
- PSA Birth Certificate of the student
- Certification from the HR Head confirming that the parent is a regular employee in good standing

**How do students apply for the discount?**

For **NEW** Applicants:

1. Complete the Online Admissions Application Form
2. Submit initial documents through MMDC EnrollMate
3. Pass the MMDC Online Readiness Assessment
4. Submit required documents including the discount application form and HR certification
5. Finalize courses and schedules
6. Pay the enrollment fee with the 25% additional tuition discount applied.

For **CURRENTLY ENROLLED** Students:

1. Submit an email to **studentfinancialservices@mmdc.mcl.edu.ph** expressing your intent to apply for the YGC–Ayala Promotional Discount.
2. Submit required documents including the discount application form and HR certification
3. Pay the enrollment fee with the 25% additional tuition discount applied.

**Can this discount be combined with other scholarships?**

No. The YGC–Ayala Promotional Discount cannot be combined with other MMDC scholarship programs, except for the Asenso Discount.

**Will the discount still apply if the parent leaves the company?**

No. The discount may no longer apply if the employee resigns, is under disciplinary action, or is no longer officially connected with the company covered by the program.

**What happens if enrollment is canceled?**

If a student does not proceed with enrollment, the discount will not be applied.

**Continuing Education Scholarship Program**

**What is the MMDC Continuing Education Scholarship Program?**

The MMDC Continuing Education (CE) Scholarship Program is designed to support working students from partner companies by providing financial assistance to help them pursue a college degree at MMDC.

**What benefit does the scholarship provide?**

The scholarship covers:

- Tuition fees only

- Up to a maximum of 45 units

- Must be completed within 2 years


**How are scholarship slots allocated?**

Slots are determined through **industry partner nominations**:

- Each partner may nominate **5 employee-scholars**

- An additional **1 scholarship slot is granted for every 10 referred enrollees**


**What are the qualifications for selection?**

Applicants must:

- Demonstrate good character and work ethic

- Pass the MMDC PPC (Projects, Problems, Cases) Readiness Assessment

- Be selected by their employer based on performance and potential


**What are the maintaining requirements for scholars?**

To continue the scholarship, scholars must:

- Maintain a Term Weighted Average (TWA) of 2.50 or better

- Have no failing grades

- Have no disciplinary record

- Enroll in at least 6 units per term


**Can the scholarship be combined with other scholarship programs?**

The CE Scholarship cannot be combined with other MMDC scholarships, except for the Asenso 20% discount.

**What happens if enrollment is canceled?**

If enrollment is canceled, the number of units initially enrolled will still be deducted from the 45-unit scholarship allocation.

**Abanse Negrense 100% Scholarship Program**

**What is the Abanse Negrense Scholarship Program?**

The Abanse Negrense IT and Business Scholarship Program is a partnership between MMDC and the Provincial Government of Negros Occidental that provides full-ride scholarships to deserving students in the province.

**What does the scholarship cover?**

The scholarship provides a full-ride grant, which includes:

- Tuition fees and miscellaneous fees

- Coverage for the entire duration of the program (up to graduation)


**What are the qualifications to be selected?**

Applicants must:

- Be a resident of Negros Occidental (excluding Bacolod)

- Be an incoming freshman

- Be willing to render volunteer service for the Provincial Government


**How long is the scholarship valid?**

The scholarship is valid from first year until graduation, provided all requirements are met.

**What are the maintaining requirements for scholars?**

Scholars must:

- Maintain a TWA of 2.50 or better

- Have no failing or dropped subjects

- Enroll in a full load each term

- Follow MMDC rules and regulations

- Have no disciplinary record


**What happens if a scholar fails to meet the requirements?**

Failure to meet academic, behavioral, or service obligations may result in sanctions or loss of the scholarship, as determined by the Provincial Government and MMDC.

**Abanse Negrense Partial Scholarship Program**

**What is the Abanse Negrense Partial Scholarship Program?**

The Abanse Negrense Partial Scholarship Program is a financial assistance initiative by the Provincial Government of Negros Occidental in partnership with MMDC, designed to support students while requiring a shared financial contribution.

**What does the scholarship cover?**

Under the partial scholarship model:

- The Provincial Government covers up to ₱15,000 per term for tuition, laboratory, and miscellaneous fees

- Any amount beyond ₱15,000 per term will be shouldered by the student (grantee)


**What are the qualifications to be selected?**

Applicants must:

- Be a resident of Negros Occidental (excluding Bacolod)

- Be an incoming freshman

- Be willing to render volunteer service for the Provincial Government


**How long is the scholarship valid?**

The scholarship is valid from first year until graduation, provided all requirements are met.

**What are the maintaining requirements for scholars?**

Scholars must:

- Maintain a TWA of 2.50 or better

- Have no failing or dropped subjects

- Enroll in a full load each term

- Follow MMDC rules and regulations

- Have no disciplinary record

- Pay any tuition and fees exceeding ₱15,000 per term


**What happens if a scholar fails to meet the requirements?**

Failure to meet academic, behavioral, or service obligations may result in sanctions or loss of the scholarship, as determined by the Provincial Government and MMDC.

## Approved Petition/ Special Classes and Next Steps (T3-SY25-26) – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/44691384944141-Approved-Petition-Special-Classes-and-Next-Steps-T3-SY25-26

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/44691384944141-Approved-Petition-Special-Classes-and-Next-Steps-T3-SY25-26#main-content)

This advisory serves to inform students that the petitioned **Special Classes** for Term 3 SY 2025-2026 have been reviewed by our Academics Team. If you submitted a petition and your course is listed in the approved offerings, please carefully review the next steps and important reminders below.

For information on submitting a petition request, please see this guide: [Petition to Open a Special Class](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38541627793421)

* * *

## ✅ Approved Special Classes This Term

The following courses have been approved for special offering this **Term 3-SY2025-2026:**

![Screenshot 2026-03-30 at 1.57.38 PM.png](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/44691384940941)

You may also access the list via this sheet: [Term 3-SY2025-2026 Course Offerings](https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1vsxGa3L2zfiVg487CVsBHyzqokAhehz1W40dDo6WbPk/edit?gid=2007197335#gid=2007197335)

* * *

## Next Steps: Final Confirmation required

To proceed, students must submit their enrollment finalization for the approved special class listed above by completing the official Special Course Finalization Google Form. This confirms that they **agree to / accept / acknowledge** the tuition cost of the petition course they intend to enroll in.

The submission deadline is **April 8, 2026, at 5:00 PM**. Only students who accomplish the final confirmation Google Form will be considered **officially enrolled** in the petition course.

🔗 [**Enrollment Finalization for Approved Petitioned Special Courses T3-SY2526**](https://forms.gle/cv7XJGUeb1gf8xP58) 🔗

**Deadline to finalize:** April 8, 5:00 pm.

* * *

For more information on the **assessment of Petition Course Fees**, please refer to the help article: [Petition to Open a Special Class](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/38541627793421)

* * *

## Additional Next steps:

1. After your enrollment confirmation is received via the Gform, you will be manually enrolled to the course during the week of April 6-10. Please await your GSA by April 10-15.
2. Afterwards, please proceed with submitting the payment for enrollment no later tha **n April 17, 2026.** Please be reminded that synchronous sessions will start on **April 27, 2026.**

## Other important reminders:

- ❌ **No Revisions or Withdrawals:** Once you submit your confirmation to enroll in the special class, no further changes will be allowed.

- ⚖️ **Disciplinary Sanction for Non-Compliance:**

Students who confirm but **fail to proceed with enrollment** will be subject to disciplinary action as endorsed by the Registrar’s Office.

- ✍️ **Parental Consent Required (if applicable):**

The signed petition form must include your agreement, as well as that of your parent or guardian, to the **assessment of additional fees and course requirements**. If you are self-paying, please indicate this in the GForm.

## Student Assistant Hiring – LMS & Coursera Support – MMDC

URL: https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/44887271185421-Student-Assistant-Hiring-LMS-Coursera-Support

[Skip to main content](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/en-us/articles/44887271185421-Student-Assistant-Hiring-LMS-Coursera-Support#main-content)

|     |
| --- |
| ## **Overview**<br>MMDC is currently looking for a **Student Assistant** to support LMS-related tasks and learner access management. This opportunity is open to currently enrolled MMDC students who are interested in gaining hands-on experience in systems operations, coordination, and digital learning support.<br>The role provides an opportunity to build practical skills in working with learning platforms such as Coursera, while contributing to the day-to-day operations that support fellow learners. |

![](https://support.mmdc.mcl.edu.ph/hc/article_attachments/44887315616397)

## Position Title

Student Assistant – LMS & Coursera Support

* * *

## Type of Opportunity

Part-time student assistant role

* * *

## What You’ll Do

As a Student Assistant, you will support tasks related to learner access and platform management, including:

- tracking and monitoring LMS subscriptions
- managing learner access on Coursera
- handling communication and coordination using Google Workspace tools (e.g., Gmail, Google Sheets, Google Docs)

* * *

## Qualifications

To be eligible, applicants must:

- have been enrolled in MMDC for at least one (1) year
- be proficient in Google Workspace tools (Gmail, Sheets, Docs)
- have strong attention to detail and organization skills

**Preferred (but not required):**

- familiarity with LMS platforms and navigation

* * *

## Application Process

Interested students may apply by submitting their application through the form below:

👉 **Application Form:**

[https://forms.gle/iTMUz9DNVkti3JTQ7](https://forms.gle/iTMUz9DNVkti3JTQ7)

Please prepare the following before submitting:

- updated resume or CV
- cover letter

* * *

## What Happens After You Apply

Once your application is submitted:

- your application will be reviewed by the hiring team
- shortlisted applicants will be contacted for an interview

Please ensure that your contact details are accurate and regularly check your email for updates.

* * *

## Important Notes

- This opportunity is open to currently enrolled MMDC students who meet the eligibility requirements
- Only shortlisted applicants will be contacted for the next steps
- Submission of an application does not guarantee selection

* * *

## Tips for Applicants

To strengthen your application:

- highlight any experience using Google Workspace tools
- include any exposure to LMS platforms or digital tools
- keep your resume clear, concise, and relevant to the role

* * *
